 *YARIMA JUNAYD*
🌸🌸🌸🌸🌸🌸

   Na
Jiddah S Mapi

*Chapter 1*

*_Arewabooks Jiddasmapi_*


                ~Yarima!!! Yarima!!! Yarima!!! Ka rike hannuwana zan faɗi, sulɓi yana jana banaso na faɗi acikin Ruwan nan, Yarima!!!! Da sauri a farka yana furta "Innalillahi wa inna ilaihiraji'un" ganin yadda ya saki yarinyar ta faɗi a cikin ruwan, a ƴan kwanakinnan wannan mafarkin ya dameshi, baya taɓa kwanciya ya farka lafiya sai yayi mafarkin yarinyar da ko fuskarta baya gani, kafafuwanshi ya sauke daga kan Bed ɗin a hankali ya miƙe yana yamutsa fuska, Lips nashi wanda yake Red Color ya tura na kasan cikin bakinshi yana tsotsa, wannan ɗabi'arshi ne, saida ya mike na zuba mishi ido, wani Dogo ne yana da ɗan kauri, Hancinshi nada tsayi sosai, sai bakinshi dayake ɗan karami, idanunshi na gani irin na Turawa kwayan cikin idon Brown color, manyan ido ne mai ɗauke dogayen eyelashes Wanda yake baƙi sosai, gashin giranshi baƙi ne sosai shima a tattare, kanshi kuma yanada suma kuma yana samun gyara sosai, fari ne sosai, fuskarshi ɗauke da kwantaccen saje wanda yakara fito da asalin kyawunshi, Rigan dayake jikinshi ya cire nan na hango faffaɗan kirjinshi wanda yake cike da kwantaccen gashi, hannunshi ma yana ɗauke da gargasa, a hankali yafara cire kayan jikinshi.

Saida ya cire komai kafin ya ɗau wata ƴar karaman Towel datake shinfiɗe a gefen Gadon da alama an ajiye mishi ne domin hakan, Cikin ɗakin nagani, gadon silver color ne, anyi mishi ado da pink ɗin Kayan sarauta, gadon kaɗai abun tsayawa a kalla ne, balle kuma Mirror da Drower da sauran kayan da suke relative da gadon.

Cikin ɗakin kana gani kasan wannan ɗakin Sarauta ne domin an ƙayata shi da kayan ado na sarauta masu kyau da ɗaukan hankali.

A hankali yafara takawa zai shiga Toilet ɗinshi dayake haɗe da Bedroom ɗin, Handle ya murɗa yaji an rungumeshi ta baya, lallausan hannunshi wanda yake fari yasa ya riko hannunta, Fuskarta tasa a gefen wuyarshi tana gogawa tana dariya, wata kyakkyawan matace zata kai shekara 25 tana da kyau sosai, tayi Dressing cikin Atamfa sannan ta ɗaura bakin Alkyabba akai, hulan alkyabban tasa wanda yakara fitowa da farin fatar sosai.

A hankali ya zameta yana ɗan murtuƙe fuska, rikeshi tayi tana fuskantar shi hannunta kuma ta zagaye Waist ɗinshi dashi, ɗauke kai yayi yana kallon gefe, Towel ɗin tafara warwarewa da sauri ya rike hannunta yana girgiza mata kai.

"Why" tayi maganar tana kallon cikin idonshi, zame hannunta yayi daga jikinshi ya juya zai shiga yayi wankan shi, kara rungumeshi tayi ta baya tana ƙankameshi, cire hannunta yayi ya ture ta sannan yashiga toilet ɗin ya rufe, Bayanshi ya haɗa da jikin kofan yana kallon cikin kyakkyawan Toilet nashi, komai da komai akwai aciki, kama daga kan sabulu shower Jel da turaruka ga brush da makilin, cikin Toilet ɗin ma abin tsayawa a kalla ne.

A hankali yafara takawa har zuwa wurin da jaccuzzy yake, ruwan zafi da na sanyi ya tara, cire Towel ɗin yayi daga jikinshi ya zauna acikin jaccuzzy yanajin ruwan yana bin jikinshi, kunna shower yayi Nan ruwa yafara tsiyaya a kanshi, lumshe ido yayi yanajin nutsuwa yana shiga jikinshi.

Ya kai akalla minti 30 kafin ya mika hannu ya ɗau sabulu yafara gogawa a jikinshi, sanyin daɗi yaji a jikinshi domin sabulun yana ɗauke da sinadarin Menthol, Saida ya goga kafin ya kara kunna shower Nan yayi wanka, ya zura dogayen kafarshi zuwa waje ya ɗau Towel ya Kara ɗaurawa a waist ɗinshi, sannan ya ɗauki wani karami daga gefe yafara goge tulin sumar kanshi wanda suke a kwance.

Cikin takunshi na kasaita da isa da nuna shi ɗin jinin Sarauta ne yafara tafiya har ya buɗe kofa, Kamar koda yaushe Lips nashi na kasa ya tura cikin bakinshi yana tsotsa, ganinta a ɗakin ta ɗaura kafa ɗaya akan ɗaya tana latsa waya yasashi kawar da kanshi yana nufan inda zai zauna ya shafa mai.

Wasu lotions da creams da kuma Body kulacca ya ɗauka ya buɗe, drayer ya ɗauka ya kunna yana busar da gashin kanshi wanda yake a jike, Saida ya bushe kafin yafara shafa lotions ɗin yana kallonta ta cikin madubi, a hankali ta taso cikin takunta na kasaita da nuna itama jinin Sarauta ne ta karaso wurinshi, Lotion ta matsa sannan ta goga a hannunta a hankali tafara bin jikinshi da shafa, shiru yayi mata har ta gama yana kallonta ta madubi.

Taje gashin kanshi tayi sannan tayi mishi style dashi, murmushi ta sakar mishi tana ɗaga hannunta sama Alaman kayi kyau, Cikin fishi ya tashi zai tafi da sauri ta riko hannunshi.

"Haba yarima na kasan fa bazan iya jure fushinka ba, wallahi bada sona na jima a can ba nasan Kanada bukata ta amma ai bazan bar aiki saboda kai kawai ba...

Fizge hannunshi yayi dama yasani Ruma bazata taɓa canja hali ba, kullum batada lokacin shi, ga kishi ga isa ga gadara da raini, shi kaɗai take ɗan shakku a gidan amma ko me martaba baya faɗa mata tayi me kyau tayi, dole sai abinda ranta yaso shi takeyi.

Rigan Shadda yasa wani ash color sannan yasa wandon, ya ɗau alkyabba ya ɗaura a sama, ba karamin kyau yayi ba da shiga irin ta sarakai, bakin glass yasa a fuskarshi sannan ya ɗau turare mai daddaɗan kamshi ya feshe jikinshi dashi, saida ya gama ya kalleta, tasan me yake nufi, wayarshi ta mika mishi, sannan ta riko hannunshi suka nufi hanyar fita.

A ranta tana cewa "wannan da yana magana da ko nashiga uku, Gara da Allah ya toshe bakinshi da ya daɗe da sakina".

Falonshi suka wuce wanda yake cike da kaya irin na sarauta, komai na falon Purple ne, da fari, harda flowers Wanda suke cikin tukunyar flower, Shima flowers ɗin suna bada wani sihirtaccen kamshi na Musamman, wasu bayi ne su biyu ƴammata suka durkusa kasa suna gaishesu.

"Gaisuwa gareki Gimbiya Rumasa'u Mai martaba yana jiranku a fada, muna gaishe da Yarima Me jiran gado"

Kallon banza tayi musu kana cikin isa da gadara ta ɗaga musu hannu, cigaba sukayi da tafiya, suna wuce part part, ɗaki ɗaki na cikin gidan, Da fari wani Babban falo suka shiga Yarima ya durkusa kasa haka itama Ruma, Wata mata ce wacce bazata kai shekaru 50 ba, amma zata wuce 48 kyakkyawa ce fara sol tana da kiɓa, jikinta sanye da Atamfa tayi ɗauri irin na matan sarki, murmushi tayi ta amsa gaisuwan, A hankali yarima ya mike yana shagwaɓe fuska, gabanta yaje ya zauna ya ɗaura kanshi a cinyarta yayi kamar zaiyi kuka.

"Haba Junayd meyasa bakason cikin mutane ne? Meeting ne fa zakuyi dasu me martaba, kuma kasan dolene ka rinƙa Attending ɗin komai daya shafi sarauta a gidannan ko?"
Shiru yayi yana lumshe ido, Ruma chatting ɗinta take da friends nata na school, Kallonta Matar tayi tace "zo ki ɗau mijinki ku tafi kafin Mai Martaba yayi fushi"

"To Ammi" tafaɗa tana ci gaba da danna wayar, gaban Ammi tazo ta riko hannunshi, lumshe mata ido yayi yana kwaɓe fuska, a hankali tace "tashi muje sauri nake kuma wallahi Zan tafi school Ni banson rigima"

Ammi shiru tayi dan tasan kaɗanne daga cikin aikin Ruma ta juya ta tafi, yanzu ma dan Mai martaba ne yace suke idan ba haka ba bazata je ba.

Tashi yayi yana yiwa Ammi Bye Bye, suna fita tayi tagumi a fili tace "Yaushe ne zanji muryan ɗana? Yaushe Allah zai buɗe maka baki Babana? Yaushe zaka fara magana kamar yadda mutane suke yi?".

"Ammi ki daina sa kanki a damuwa Hamma Junayd ai zaiyi magana tunda ba haka aka haifeshi ba"
Wani matashi ne wanda bazai wuce shekara 20 ba, kana ganinshi kasan kasan Junayd ne domin kama sosai ya bayyana a fuskarsu.

"Auta har yaushe ne hakan zai faru? Ina kwaɗayin ganin wannan rana".

"Ammi banason ganinki cikin damuwa dan Allah ki daina banaso" yafaɗa yana gyara igiyan wandonshi, yana kama da Junayd sosai saide yafi Junayd yarinta da kuma fara'a.

"To Safwan zan daina"
Wurinta yazo yayi mata kiss a gefen fuska "that's my Mom Haka nakeso naji, yanzu yimin dariya kaɗan nagani"
Dariya Ammi tayi dama idan Safwan yana wuri dole kayi dariya.

"Ammi na shirya zan tafi school nifa Ammi nafison Aure akan school ɗinnan gashi Abba ya dage sai nayi school so nake naga nima inada yaro".

Cikin kunya Ammi ta kauda kanta, Yaro Babu kunya haka ko kaɗan?
Yasani shiyasa yayi dariya kawai yafita.

Suna fita suka shiga ɗayan ɗakin dayake gefen na Ammi, A hankali Suka durkusa suna gaida matar datake kwance tana cin Tufa, Hannunta ta ɗaura akan Timtim ɗin dayake tsakar falon, Bayi guda uku ne suke matse mata jikinta, biyu kuma sunayi mata fifita, kallon su Ruma tayi tace "Sannunku sai yanzu?"

Dariya Ruma tayi tace "Fulani Ai kinsan Yarima da rashin saurin shiri, shi ya daɗar damu"

Dariya tayi tace "nasan halin ɗan nawa"
Yarima murmushi kawai yayi mata yasa hannu ya ɗau Apple guda ɗaya a hankali yafara tauna yana kallon Ruma datake cigaba da Chatting ɗinta, mikewa yayi saida ya ɗan Taɓata kafin ta mike tana yamutsa fuska, fita sukayi matar tanayi musu murmushi.

A bakin kofa suka haɗu da wani matashi zai kai 26 year Yana ganinsu yanemi canja hanya, Yarima ne ya riko hannunshi, ya juyo ya kalleshi, gira ya ɗaga mishi Alaman ina zaije?"

Sosa Kai yayi yace "ina kwana Unty Ruma"

"Lafiya kalau Munir ya kake?"

"Ina lafiya"

"Ina kwana Hamma Junayd?"

Kallonshi yayi sama da ƙasa yanajin wani warin kayan shaye shaye yana tashi daga jikin Munir ɗin, kallon tuhuma yayi mishi kafin a hankali ya matso da fuskarshi wurin bakin Munir ɗin, tabbas yasha abu ba hancinshi ke mishi gizo ba, sakinshi yayi yabar wurin ranshi a matuƙar ɓace.

Binshi tayi baice komai ba, har suka isa fadan mai martaba, gaisuwa sukayi mishi, Dogarai suka fita a fadan, Babban fada ne na zamani, an ƙayata shi da kayan kyale kyale na zamani, sarki dayake kishingiɗe akan Kujeran sarauta ya ɗago yana kallon Junayd, nan naga kama sosai a tsakaninshi da Junayd ɗin, mikewa yayi yaje ya zauna a gefen Babanshi, wani kyakkyawan darduma ne aka shimfiɗa a tsakar falon, tareda Timtim irin na sarauta kallon Junayd yayi yace "Yarima? Me ya sameka ka ɓata rai haka?"

Turo baki yayi gaba yana kallon ƙasa, hannunshi mai martaba ya riko yace "banson abinda zai taɓa ka faɗamin meya sameka?"

Biro ya ciro a aljihun riganshi yafara rubutu, saida ya gama ya mikawa mishi
_muneer bai daina shaye shaye ba Abba, gaskiya sai an kara yimishi faɗa tunda yaƙi jina_"

Numfashi mai martaba yaja sannan yace "Nasani bai daina ba amma na rasa yadda zanyi dashi saide hakan bazai hana nayi mishi faɗa kuma na hukunta shi ba"

Murmushi Junayd yayi saboda bayason yana ganin Kanin nashi acikin wannan hali na shaye shaye, waya ma martaba ya ciro ya danna Number ɗin muneer "ka zo Fada"

Muneer dayake kwance a gefen Ummanshi jin mai martaba ya kirashi yasa ya kalli Umman nashi cikin Ɓacin rai da hura hanci yace "Umma kin gani ko? Yanzu yaje ya haɗani da mahaifina nasan faɗawa Abba yayi ina shaye shaye wallahi Umma bazan yadda ba, Ni kaɗai ne a gidan? Ni kaɗai ne?"

Murmushin gefen baki tayi, hannunta tasa ta shafo kanshi tace "Kada ka damu Ɗana ka tashi kaje kaji kiran da yayi maka, barni dasu zanyi maganin kowa a gidan"

Tashi Yayi dan yasan Umman nashi zata iya komai, ɗakin mai martaba yaje yana hararan Junayd har ya zauna a gefe ya dukar dakai yace "gani"

"Kana ganin abinda kake ya dace?"
Shiru yayi, cikin tsawa mai martaba yace "kai ba magana nake maka ba?"

"Ayi hakuri Abba zan daina"

Ganin ran Abba zai ɓaci ne yace "tashi kafita" fita yayi, Ruma ce ta duka tace "Yallaɓai nikam zan wuce domin inada class"

"Kenan class nata yafi mata kiran Mahaifina?"

Takalmi tasa sannan tafita a ɗakin, Mai martaba ya kula da halin daya shiga "Ka daina damuwa Komai yayi farko zaiyi karshe kuma ko ba komai ai Ruma kanwarka ce tunda mahaifinta ɗan uwana ne".

Shiru kawai yayi ranshi in yayi dubu to ya ɓaci, ko a wurin kwanciya ba kulashi take ba, sai kishi kamar Hauka, gashi Allah yayi shi Mabuƙaci ne sosai, yanada karfin sha'awa sosai, ya ma rasa yadda zaiyi da Ruma.

Jiddah S Mapi

*Chapter 2*

*_Arewabooks @Jiddasmapi_*


                ~Asalinsu ƴan garin Gombe ne, mahaifinsu shine Sarkin Garin, shi ɗin Asalin bafulatani ne yayi gadon sarauta tun daga wurin iyayenshi wanda suma suka gada daga wurin kakanni, Yanada mata biyu Maryam da Suwaiba, Suwaiba itace Babba wato mahaifiyar Muneer sai kuma Maryam mahaifiyar Junayd da Safwan da kuma Ibtisam, Junayd shine Babba Allah ya ɗorawa Mai martaba soyayyan Junayd saboda lalura dayake ɗauke dashi, laluran shine yana ji amma baya iya maidawa, magani ana nema mishi a ko ina amma ba'a dace ba, hakan kuma baisa sun fasa nema mishi ba.

Ibtisam tana karatu anan cikin garin Gombe Secondary school take domin bazata wuce 16years ba, Mai martaba yanada ɗan uwa a garin Adamawa wanda suke Alaqa sosai dashi, ɗan uwan kuma shine Sarkin Garin Yanada yarinya guda ɗaya tilo wanda Allah ya bashi domin duk sauran Maza ne, hakan yasa ya ɗau soyayyan duniya ya ɗaurawa yarinyar, babu wani gata da bata ganshi a duniya ba, kuma har yanzu tana ganin gata, ba kowa bace face Rumasa'u matar Junayd, anyi aurensu lokacin Junayd yana karatu a malysia yana karanta medical doctor, Saida ya dawo yaji labarin an ɗaura mishi aure da Ruma duk da baiji daɗi ba amma ya yiwa iyayenshi biyayya.

Yanason Ruma amma halayenta ba abun so bane, bata da kunya ko kaɗan gata da gadara da tsiwa, Ta maida hankalinta ne akan karatu bata bashi kulawa yadda ya kamata, saide tana sonshi sosai kamar ta lashe shi, tana takama da kyau da kuma cewar itama ƴar sarki ce gata da bin kawayen banza ƴaƴan masu kuɗi da sarauta, a Kawayenta babu yaran talaka.

A rayuwa babu abinda yarima yakeso dama da iyayenshi da kuma kannenshi, yana da Babban Asibiti wanda Abba ya buɗe mishi, acan yake aiki, Nakasanshi baisa ya kasa ba, shi ya yadda da wannan Magana da hausawa suke cewa NAKASA BA KASAWA BACE yana da kasaita dama asali shikam bai fiye son magana ba kuma sai Allah ya jarabceshi da rashin magana.


              "Aneesa kiyi hakuri mana tun ɗazu fa yarinyar nan take baki hakuri amma kinki sakinta? So kike Mama taji hankalinta ya tashi? Wata Kyakkyawar yarinya ce take magana shekarunta ba zasu wuce 23 ba tana sanye da kaya irin na fulani, sai jan kanwarta take amma yarinyar taki zuwa ta dage saita rama abinda akayi mata, ranta a ɓace ta juyo tana kallon Addan Tata, Nan naga fuskarta kyakkyawa ce itama harma tafi Tayar Tata kyau, farace sol ga ta da dara daran idanu masu kyau da ɗaukan hankali, bakinta ɗan karami dashi, Lips nata pink ne gashin kanta an kame wuri ɗaya an kitse shi guda biyu, gefe da gefe, Kitson ya sauko har gadon bayanta gashi baƙi kirin, yatsun hannunta farare sunsha lalle jaa, jikinta sanye da Kayan Fulani itama, a shekaru bazata wuce 17 ba.

Goshinta an ɗiga mishi wani farin fenti irin yadda Fulani suke ado, Adda surayya ki barni na koyawa yarinyar nan hankali" tayi maganan da zazzaƙan muryanta tana fizge kanta.

"Ya Allah Aneesa wai meyasa bakida hakuri ne? Tin ɗazu fa nake lallaɓaki wallahi zan sake ki naje gida nakira Mama, idan bakiji nawa ba zakiji nata"
Daina fizge kanta tayi tana tura baki gaba, tasan idan Mama tazo yau dole sai taci duka, kallon Yarinyar data tsokaneta tayi ta nuna ta da yatsa tace "wallahi idan muka haɗu ko a ina saikin raina kanki"

Kwaryan dayake gefe ta ɗauka ta ɗaura a kanta, Itama Surayya wacce take ta nishi domin Aneesa ta gajiyar da ita, ta ɗauko nata ta ɗaura suka fara tafiya, Surayya na baya Aneesa na gaba.

Cikin kauye ne sosai na fulanai ruga dayawa acikin garin ga kuma Fulani da shanaye wanda suke ta yawo cikin garin, kashin shanu shine ya cika musu hanya Aneesa sai tsaki take ita kuma Surayya shiru tayi mata tana cigaba da tafiya, inda sabo ta saba da halin Aneesa, kanwarta ce amma bata ɗau halin Mahaifiyarsu ba na hakuri da kawaici, Batada fitina amma idan an taɓota bata da hakuri ko kaɗan, yanzu ma a hanyan dawowa ba ita aka tsokana ba, Surayyan aka tsokana amma tace saita likiɗa yarinyar, ƴan kauyen sun san halinta shiyasa basa tsokananta saide ita Surayya wacce take shiru shiru.

Rugansu suka iso nan naga Aneesa ta ajiye Kwaryan ta mika wa wata mata kuɗin hannunta, matar ma kana ganinta kasan itace ta haifesu domin itama kyakkyawa ce kamar daga kasar India, tana mika mata ta juya buta tafara wanke kafarta, saida tagama ta buɗe labule zata shiga ɗaki Mama ta kalleta tace "Aneesa? Aina kuka tsaya tun ɗazu?"

Shiru kawai tayi tarasa abin faɗa, ba tambayarki nake ba?

Surayya datake wanke kafa itama tace "Mama mun tsaya neman canji ne shiyasa kikaga mun daɗe"

"Kin tabbata gaskiya kike faɗamin? Dan fa nasan halin Aneesa da rashin hakuri, bansan yaushe yarinyar nan zata koyi hakuri ba, baki san inda zaki kare rayuwarki ba, kina mace bai dace ace baki da hakuri ba, wallahi Aneesa ina guje miki zama da kishiya bazakici riban zaman aure ba"

Tura baki tayi tashiga ɗaki, saida tashiga tafara gunguni tana shafa mai aikinta kenan wanke jiki da shafa mai, ko akan datti tana iya shafa mai ta zauna, hakan ne yasa farin fatar ta yake ɗan dishewa wani lokacin, Allah ma ya taimaketa tana kyaun fata da jiki mai kyau.

Saida mama tagama surutu kafin tacewa Surayya ta ɗauka musu abinci a kitchen, kitchen ɗin na kara ne an kewaye da zana, cikin gidan ma da zana aka kewaye.

Ɗaukan samira tayi ta nufi ɗaki dashi, Mama abin yana matukar ɓata mata rai, ya dace ace Aneesa ce zata ɗauko musu abinci harda ruwa Amma Surayya ce take yin hakan Wannan wace irin yarinya ce?

Tana kaiwa Aneesa ta kalleta cikin tura baki tace "Adda me aka dafa ne?" Hausanta baya fita sosai domin sunfi yin fulatanci a garin.

"Idan kin sakko zaki dan menene"
Sauka tayi daga kan gado me rumfa tana leko abincin, ganin dambu ne ta sakko tasa hannu tafara ci, tanason dambu sosai hakan yasa idan taga anyi sai taji farin ciki, kuma koda fushi take tana danne fushin taci dambun.

"Aneesa?"

"Na'am" tafaɗa tana cika ɗan karamin bakinta da dambun.

"Inaso muyi magana dake amma banaso Mama ta sani" tayi maganan tana ajiye cokalin dayake hannunta.

"Tom ina jinki"
"Kimin Alkawari"

"Nayi alkawari"
Gyara zama tayi tana kallon Kanwar tata "Aneesa kinsan har yanzu inason Giɗaɗo ko?"

Waro mayan idanunta tayi tana buɗe baki cikin mamaki tace "Adda? Wai ke har yanzu bazaki cire Giɗaɗo a ranki ba? Kin manta cin mutuncin da yayiwa Mama a nan gidan? Kin manta dukan daya gama yimiki, ki tuna da lokacin dakike gidanshi Ni wannan nafiki kauri nida ake cewa kamar tsinken tsire, kin fita a hayyacinki ba abinci me kyau ba ba suturan arziki ba, Bakida tunkiya balle Shanu".

"Hakane Aneesa Amma ai kinsan tsakanin Mata da miji sai Allah.."

"Haba Adda wani irin mata da miji sai Allah? Giɗaɗo fa ba karamin ɗan banza bane, shan me kika gani a jikin giɗaɗo har kika yadda kika aureshi? Gashi da katon kai ga wuya kamar fartanyan, Ni banga abin so ajikin giɗaɗo ba, to me ma kikeso kice zakiyi?"

"Aneesa banfa ce ki zagemin Miji ba yawwa"

"Miji kuma? Saki biyu fa yayi miki kuma bai maidaki ba, yanzu me zakiyi?"

Matsowa tayi tace "yawwa Aneesa so nake na aikeki wurinshi, saboda jiya ya turo sannan kanin nashi iliya yabani hakuri inaso kije wurinshi kice yaje ya samu Baba a daji sai suyi magana".

"Shine abinda kike so nayi kawai?"

Giɗa mata kai tayi, "to babu damuwa yanzu ma kuwa zanje"

"Yawwa Aneesa ta ƴar kyakkyawar Mama auta me hakuri".

Saida ta koshi kafin ta wanke hannunta ta zari bakin mayafi ta yafa, silifas blue tasa, hakan yasa farin kafarta ya bayyana yayi kyau sosai, ɗan kwali ta ɗaura sannan ta saki kitsonta zuwa gadon bayanta, hanyan soron gidan ta nufa tana shirin fita cikin sanɗa.

"Ina zakije?" Mama tafaɗa tana fitowa daga kitchen, tsayawa tayi cakk tana zaro ido tareda motsa baki taki juyowa.

"Ba tambayarki nake ba? Aneesa"

"Inna zanje na duba Kulu ne cikinta yana ciwo tun jiya kuma banje rugarsu ba" tayi maganan cikin rashin gaskiya.

"Allah sarki Kulu ashe siyasa ban ganta ba yau, idan kinje ki gaida innarta"

cikin murna tace "To Mama zataji" 
Fita tayi tana tafiya ta ɗau wani kara tana wasa dashi tana ɗan waƙa da fulatanci "Sauti kan sauti wallahi fasi mittako"
tana rera waka har ta iso Rugan su Kulu, lekawa tayi ganin Kulu tana wanke wanke ta kirata a hankali, ganin Aneesa ne yasa ta tashi cikin sanɗa ta fita, ɗankwalin kanta ta cire ta yafa a jikinta sannan suka tafi, Kulu ma bafulatana  ce, tanada kyau amma batayi ko rabin Aneesa ba, kallon ta tayi "ke Anee? Meya faru? Ina zamuje?"

"Gidansu Giɗaɗo"
Hannu tasa ta dafe kirjinta "gidan su Giɗaɗo kuma? Me zamuje yi? Kin manta ranɗin abinda yayi mana?"

"Ban manta ba Adda Surayya ce ta aikeni"

Jin haka yasa hankalin Kulu ya kwanta, dan bata manta ranar da Aneesa tayi mishi rashin kunya yaje ya hushe haushi akan Surayyan ba.

Suna isa Rugansu Giɗaɗo tayi Sallama, Mamanshi na zaune tana dama fura, ta durkusa kasa itama Kulu haka suka gaisheta, fuska a ɗan dame ta amsa, zama sukayi a gefe, Aneesa ce ta buɗe baki tace "Ina Giɗaɗo?"
Da mamaki Mamanshi ta kalleta, Giɗaɗo kuma? Dama yarinyar ba kunya ne da ita ba.

"Gani" yafaɗa yana shigowa gidan, dogone sosai baida wani tsari ko kaɗan sai hanci da baki me ɗan kauri, kallonshi tayi sama da ƙasa kafin ta mike tace "dama Adda Surayya ce ta aikoni".

Washe haƙora yayi yace "to to to muje daga waje ko?"

"A,a anan zamuyi magana dan tace tanaso Mama taji"

"To babu damuwa"

Gyara tsayuwa tayi tace "Dama cewa tayi wai ta haɗaka da girman Allah kada ka kara aika mata yaro gida, ka fita a hanyarta batason damuwa, ka barta ta huta haka ta gaji, ta gaji, ta gaji, idan har kai ɗin ɗan halak ne ka fita harkanta".

Mamanshi da take zaune ta mike tace "ki koma kifaɗa mata babu abinda Giɗaɗo zai kuma yi da ita, ga ƴammata a Rugan malam Aliyu tuli tuli sai wacce ya zaɓa, zan nuna mata cewar Giɗaɗo ba shege bane kufita kubarmin gida, kai kuma da kai kamar an soya fanken da yist yayi mishi yawa idan ka kara zuwa inda take saina ɗaga maka nono".

Fita Aneesa sukayi sukabar gidan itada Kulu wacce taketa aikin rike gefen mayafin Aneesa ɗin, jira take kawai abin gudu ya tashi ta ruga.

"Ke dalla sakeni, kinada tsoro sosai, kuma kina mace bai kamata ki zama mai tsoro haka ba, anason mace ta zama da jarumta, nima dukda inada tsoro bakiga yadda nake kokarin danne tsorona ba? Ai mutanan duniya idan ka nuna tsoro sai su rainaka su maidaka bakasan komai ba, bakiga Adda Surayya ba? Bakiga tsorone yasa tasha wahala a wurin Giɗaɗo ba? Banso nayi musu rashin kunya ba, amma idan na tuna abinda suka yiwa Addata sai inji kamar nasa wuta na ƙona rugarsu"

Suna hira har ta ajiyeta a gida takoma Rugansu, Lokacin Baba ya dawo a hankali ta durkusa kasa tana gaida Baba, cikin fara'a yace "Mamana daga ina?"

"Kulu ce babu lafiya shine naje dubata"

"Allah sarki Allah yabata Lafiya"

"Ameen Baba" 
Baban nasu ma asalin bafulatani ne kyakkyawa dogo siriri da hancinshi dogo shima, ita Aneesa tana kama da Baba sai kuma Surayya wacce take kama da Mama.

"Zo Mamana"
Zuwa tayi ta durkusa a gabanshi, wata ƴar karamar waya yaciro yace "Yayanku ya kira ɗazu amma bana jinshi kinsan garin namu babu network"

Karɓa tayi tana zubawa wayar ido, batasan komai ba akan waya sai de tayi ta latsawa, gefe ta danna sai gashi yafara kira, a hankali taji yace "Baba nyalli jamna?"

A hankali tace "Ba Baba bane nice"

"Bawa Baba wayan" yafaɗa, Dama itafa bason waya takeyi da Hamma Umar ba, ya fiye masifa da rashin fara'a garama wa Adda Surayya amma itakam ya tsaneta"

Baiwa Baba wayan tayi ta Shiga ɗaki, tana tura baki, dan yana karatu a Birni shine zai rinka yiwa mutane tsawa?.

"Yawwa kin dawo? Zo nan kada Kowa yaji"

Zuwa tayi tafara kakalo hawaye, a rikice Surayya tace "meya faru?"

"Korata yayi wai idan ban fita ba zaimin duka, ko tsayawa nayi magana baiyi ba"

Janyota jikinta tayi tana bubbuga bayanta a hankali "shiii yi shiru banson kina kuka, bazan kara yimishi magana ba kinji Ƙanwata?"

"Eh"
Shiru Surayya tayi zata iya jure komai amma bazata juri a taɓa mata kanwa ba, dolene ta cire Giɗaɗo a ranta.


*Asalinsu*

Malam Yusuf Arɗo shine asalin sunan Baba, ɗan Asalin garin Adamawa ne kuma anan suke zama a wani kauye me suna Ganye, Mama ma ƴar asalin garin Adamawa ce, anan iyayenta suke da zama, cikin kauyen, iyayen Baba sun rasu, Sunada yara huɗu Umar, Abdul, Surayya da Aneesa itace ƴar auta, Abdul ya rasu tun yanada shekara ɗaya a duniya yanzu su uku ne suka rage, shi kuma Umar baya nan yana karatu a garin Gombe, Baba ne yayi iya kokarinshi yasa shi karatu domin yanaso kauyen nasu yasamu ci gaba, Aneesa basu fiye shiri da Umar ba, ya lura tana da raini shiyasa bai fiye yimata dariya ba, yafison Surayya.

Ita kuma Surayya ta taɓa aure anyi mata aure tun tana da shekara 15 yanzu haka tanada shekara 23 tayi shekara 8 da aure babu abinda take karba sai wahala, duka rashin abinci me kyau, har noma saida tayi domin ta ciyar da kanta, a haka kuma baya ganin darajanta, ta samu ciki sau biyu yana zubarwa tsabar jaraba, baida hakuri ta wurin kwanciya ko kaɗan hakan yasa taga bazata iya ba ta nemi ya sawwaka mata, ai kuwa kamar jira yake ya turo mata saki biyu, wannan dalilin yasa ta dawo ta zauna agida gaban iyayenta.

Suna saida nono itada Aneesa a kauyen dayake kusa da su, Baba aikinshi shine bada magani, na gargajiya yana zuwa daji ya nemo magani, kuma da yaddan Allah ana dacewa, wannan baiwa da Allah yabashi shiyasa ya tura Umar zuwa karatun likitanci a cikin garin Gombe, Aneesa Tanada hakuri amma idan an taɓota batada hakuri ko kaɗan gashi batada yafiya gata da riko.
Kawarta ɗaya ce a garin itace Kulu, da ma batada kawa sai Addan tawato Surayya amma Kulu sun shaƙu sosai.

                ~Shiri yayi cikin kayanshi na doctor fuskarshi babu walwala, kayan ya amshi jikinshi yayi kyau sosai, gaban mirror yaje yaja wani stool ya zauna, wani hair oil ya ɗauka ya zuba a tafin hannunshi yana murzawa, a kanshi ya shafa yana kallon fuskarshi ta jikin madubin dayake gabanshi, a nutse yakeyin komai, da sauri ta tura kofan tashigo tana waya, buɗe Drower tayi taciro wasu takaddu kallo ɗaya tayi mishi ta watsar, ganin ta shigo yasa ya juyo yana kallonta da lumsashen idonshi, ganin zata fita yasa ya ɗaga mata hannu, langwaɓe kai tayi tana kallonshi Alaman tana sauri, hannu yasa ya yafito ta, alaman tazo, tsaki taja kaɗan sannan tafara takowa zuwa gabanshi, hannunta ya riƙo ya ɗau oil ɗin ya matsa a tafin hannunta ya haɗa ya murza sannan ya mika mata kanshi, so yake ta shafa mishi, haɗe rai tayi tace "Gaskiya Yarima kana da Damuwa yanzu fa jirana ake kawayena suna class nikuma Ina Nan gida? Nawa zan raba hakalina?"
Shiru yayi mata yanajin yadda take murza gashin kanshi, saida ta gama ta yago Tissue ta goge hannunta, takaddun ta tattaro ta juya zata fita, hannunta ya riƙo ya jawota zuwa kan cinyarshi, dogon hancinshi yafara gogawa a wuyanta yana lumshe ido, tareda shaƙar ƙamshin Turarenta mai daɗin gaske, kwacewa ta fara domin taga Alaman so yake ya hanata tafiya School, hannu yasa yafara shafa jikinta mai laushi da kuma santsi wanda yaji hutu kuma yake samun gyara, hannu yakai wurin Breast nata yafara cusa hannunshi ta saman riganta dayake a buɗe, da sauri ta buge hannunshi ta tashi daga cinyarshi da sauri ta dau takaddun, tana ɗan haɗa fuska tafita, yana ɗaga mata hannu taki sauraranshi, kanshi ya ɗaura a gaban Drower yayi shiru yanajin gashin jikinshi yana mimmiƙe wa, so yake yaji ɗuminta a yanzu, so yake ya kasance tare da ita, amma bataso bata bashi lokaci ko kaɗan.

Tana fita ta nufi Parking space, takalmin kafanta nada tsayi amma haka take tafiya dashi cikin kwarewa da wayewa, Bodyguard dasuke tsaye a gefe yana ganin tafito ya tashi da ɗan gudu ya buɗe mata marfin haɗaɗɗen motar kafin ta karaso, tana zuwa tashiga gidan baya ta zauna, glass Baki half face tasa a idonta sannan ta ɗau jarida tayi crossing leg ta maida hankalinta kan jarida, Driver ne yazo yafara jan ta, wasu motoci guda biyu wanda yake cike da dogari da Bodyguard sune suka fara binsu a baya, Wayarta taji yana Ruri ganin Mom yasa tayi murmushi ta ɗaga.

"Momy na? I miss You kinzo kin ajiyeni anan garin kusan 3years babu me kulani daɗin abun kawai Inason Yarima ne da ko na daɗe da dawowa gida"

Dariya Momyn nata tayi nan suka fara hira har ta ajiye wayar bayan tace "I love You Momy, a gaidamin Dad ace Ina missing ɗinshi sannan acewa brother's ɗina nayi fishi dasu"

Tafiya akeyi da ita har saida suka isa wani babba University sannan aka buɗe musu Get, Gaba ɗaya waɗanda suke hanya matsawa sukayi, dogarai suna bin bayanta tana taku kamar bata taka kasa, basu koma ba saida tashiga class kafin suka koma gefe, suna jiran ta gama karatu su koma da ita gida, Kawayenta ƴaƴan masu hannu da shuni sune suka zagayeta suna hira, tana saman Bench tace "ke Nadiya meyasa kikayi latti yau? Gashi har narigaki zuwa?"

"Hmm kibari Kawai Gimbiya Ruma wannan nataccen mijin nawane saida ya takura min yasani wankan safe"
Dariya suka kwashe dashi, Ruma tana rufe baki da hannu domin Nadiya tafara fusata tace "ohhh sorry Very sorry dear Nima Haka Yarima na yaso yimin amma kinsan banson damuwa wallahi fitowa nayi dan har yafara bani haushi, kuma kinsan Ni ban saba datakura ba, ta yaya zan zauna ya takura min?"

Shewa sukayi kamar ba'a class suke ba "ke sai yaushe zaki haifo mana Baby?" Nadiya ce ta tambayi wata datake latsa waya tana yanga da yauki tana taunar Cingum, kallonta tayi tace "Me? Me Lubcy? Na haihu yanzu? Do you want me to die? Infact ko ban mutu ba my breast will fall down ai, kuma kinsan I can't take it ko?"

Dariya Ruma tayi tace"you're right my dear haihuwa yanzu ko masifa da karatu zamuji ko da rainon yaro?"
Hiransu sukaci gaba dayi har Lecturer Yashigo, Basu daina kus kus ba har yafita, da suka tashi kowacce taje wurin motar ta Driver yajata, Itama Ruma Janta akayi suka koma gida.

Saida yayi kusan minti 10 a haka kafin ya mike jikinshi a mace, ya sa takalmi ya ɗau car keys takunshi me cike da kasaita da izza yafara, falon Ammi yawuce Safwan na zaune akan Sofa ya kunna Tv yana game, Farin Vest ne a jikinshi da kuma gajeren wandon, hankalinshi gaba ɗaya ya maida kan game ɗin, yana ganinshi ya ajiye remote ɗin, Ya Junayd? Kana buƙatar wani abu ne? Yayi tambayar domin yana ganin idon yayan nashi yasan akwai abinda yake bukata, girgiza mishi kai Junayd yayi a ranshi yace "koda na faɗa maka bazaka iya min magani ba"
Hannu Saf ɗin ya ɗaga mishi yace "Bye Bye"
Murmushi yayi yanajin son ɗan uwan nashi yana ratsa jini da zuciyarshi, a bakin kofa masu bashi tsaro na musamman suka amshi jakan dayake Hannunshi, wurin motar dayake hawa ranar Tuesday suka kai mishi, a ka'ida baya hawa mota sau biyu a sati, kowani rana da irin motar da zai hau.

Guard uku ne suke bin bayanshi har ya isa wurin motar, buɗe mishi akayi a hankali yashiga gidan baya ya zauna, sannan suka rufe, Driver ne yazo yana gaidashi hannu kawai ya ɗaga mishi, ciro wayarshi yayi yana danne danne, kallon wurinda take ajiye motarta yayi, ɗan tsaki yaja a ranshi bata da aiki sai yawon zuwa school batasan hakkin miji ba, ko dan taga baya magana ne oho.

Dogarai suka cika mota suma sunabin bayansu, a karamar takadda yayi rubutu ya mikawa Driver, ya karantawa yakira waya yana cewa "yarima yace bayason rakiyan dogarai"
Dama ya saba hakan, bai fiye son idan zai fita ayita rakashi ba, shi yasan Allah ne me karewa, su biyu dagashi sai Driver suka kama hanya, cikin garin mai kyaune yana bin ko ina da kallo, yanayin yanayi mishi daɗi yanayin sanyi sanyi kaɗan, lumshe ido yayi yana jin iska yana shiga jikinshi domin ya sauke glass da jimawa, mutane suna ɗaga mishi hannu shima yana ɗaga musu a hankali.

Wani katafaren Asibiti Suka shiga wanda aka rubuta Yarima Junayd special Hospital, haɗaɗɗen Asibiti ne private, komai na asibitin a tsare yake, daga ma'aikata har masu jinya, a ka'ida mutane biyu basa zama akan mara lafiya ɗaya, komai yana yinshi ne yadda yaga anayi a kasar malysia, akwai wadatattun likitoci wanda suka san aikinsu.

Buɗe mishi marfin mota akayi, kafarshi yasa zuwa waje yana bin cikin asibitin da Kallo, cikin takun kasaita wanda ya ke nuna shiɗin jinin Sarauta ne ya fara ratsa mutanen dasuke durkusa wa kasa suna gaisheshi, hannu yake ɗaga musu, Driver ɗinshi ne a bayanshi da lema a hannunshi, a bakin Office ɗin Junayd ɗin ya koma kamar yadda ya saba, shikuma Junayd makulli ya ciro daga Aljihunshi ya buɗe kofar Office ɗin, shiga yayi yana shaƙar sani daddaɗan kamshi, cikin Office ɗin komai tsaf idan ka gani zakace ɗaki ne, marabanshi da ɗaki shine babu gado, amma kujeran dayake cikin office ɗinma Kamar wani gado ne, an Kawata shi da kaya irin na gidan sarauta, Office ɗin yarima kaɗai abun tsayawa a kalla ne, komai na ciki silver color ne da fari, da alama yanason color ɗin sosai.

A kan wani kujera wanda aka yi shi kamar na sarki ya zauna, kujeran a baje yake, daga sama kuma a tsuke, Laptop ya jawo gabanshi ya kunna, nan ya maida hankali kan aikin daya kawoshi, Knocking akayi sannan aka buɗe wani ne sanye da Kayan Doctor da kuma abin gwaji a wuyarshi, yana ganin Yarima yayi dariya ya janyo kujera ya zauna.

"Kaga Yarima Doctor Junayd, Yarima Me jiran gado wata rana kaine sarki"

Murmushi kawai yayi dan yasaba da tsokanan Asad, Takadda ya yago yace "kai banson surutu yanzu aiki nake, ya kukayi da wancan mara lafiyan?"

Yana karantawa ya ɗan canja fuska Alaman damuwa, "gaskiya Yarima mutuminnan yabani tausayi, saida mukayi mishi operation yanzu ma haka daga wurinsu nake, da so samune a fita dashi kasar India kawai"

"Nawane zai fitar dashi?"
Yana karantawa yace "Eh to sai an kira waɗanda suka sani anyi tambayesu tunda nikam duk yawona ban taɓa zuwa India ba".

"Idan An tambaya a sanar min saimu fitar dashi" Asad yana karantawa yace "Allah yabaka lafiya kamar yadda kaima kake taimakon mutane"

"Ameen" yafaɗa acikin zuciyarshi.

Asad ganin yarima kamar yanada damuwa yace "babu dai matsala ko?"
Girgiza kai yayi yana kallon Asad ɗin.

"Ka tabbata?"
Shiru yayi, akwai matsala Amma bayaso yana tona asirin matarshi, saide babu yadda ya iya dolene ya sanarwa Abokin nashi tilo wanda shima baya iya ɓoye mishi sirrinshi komin girmanshi.

Takadda ya ɗauka yafara rubutu, saida ya gama ya ɗago lumsashun idanunshi yana kallon Asad ɗin, karya wuya yayi alaman abin yana damunshi, Asad karɓan takaddan yayi yana karantawa.

"Bata kulawa dani yadda ya kamata, bata bani hakƙina kuma kafi kowa sanin Ni ɗin Mabuƙaci ne, gashi banson bin matan banza Asad na rasa yadda zanyi da Ruma"

Shiru Asad yayi, Yarima yana bashi tausayi yasan yanada bukata amma Ruma batada lokacinshi, tana kishinshi amma bata nuna mishi soyayya da kulawa na musamman "kaci gaba da hakuri komai zai daidaita da yaddan Allah kaji!"

Giɗa kai yayi, janyo Laptop ɗin yayi ya dukar da kanshi yana cigaba da Aikinshi, Asad kuma fita yayi domin shima acikin asibitin yake aika, shiɗin Aminin Junayd ne.

Yarima baya aikin komai sai zama a Office idan anzo ganin likita azo a ganshi yabada takadda, sai kuma Idan tiyata ya tashi sai yaje suyi tare da sauran likitocin.

Karfe 5 cif ya tashi kamar yadda ya saba kullum, saida ya duba Patience gaba ɗaya kafin ya fita ya tafi, Get na gidansu anyi tambarin sarauta Wanda kana gani kasan wannan ɗin shine gidan sarki.

Bacci yanzu?"

Ɗago idanunshi da suka fara rinewa yayi yana kallon Ammin nashi, giɗa mata kai yayi alaman eh bacci zaiyi.

"Tashi babu kyau bacci War haka, kabari sai an idar da sallan Isha kaji?"

A hankali ya langwaɓe kai yayi yanayin shagwaɓa wallahi bacci sosai yakeji, tashi yayi lankwasa kafa akan kujeran ya zauna yana bin ɗakin da kallo, dariya kawai tayi ta wuce tasan ba da sonshi ya tashi ba.

Safwan dayake gyara wando yafito yana kallon Yayan nashi, harara Junayd ya aika mishi, wato shikam kullum yana kan gyara wando kamar wani kwarto, hannu yasa yayi mishi Alaman "zo nan" baki Saf ya turo wandon yaki zama a jikinshi yarasa me yake yiwa wando a rayuwarshi bayason zama a jikinshi in kaga ya zauna lafiya da wando to saide gajere, yana karasowa Junayd ya janyoshi ta hanyar rike wandon dayake kokarin sauka kasa, igiyan yasa ya ɗaure mishi mai kyau, saida yaga ya ɗauro yadda bazai kwance ba sannan yaturashi baya yana hararanshi, dariya Saf yayi sannan yace "Nagode" zama yayi a ƙasa gefenshi yayi shiru, Junayd ya fahimci akwai abinda yake son faɗa, a hankali ya taɓashi tareda ɗaga mishi gira Alaman menene?

"Ya Junayd? Wata ƴar Sarkin wani garine tace wai tana sona, kuma da aure take sona, nikuma nace mata ina school yanzu, kuma ai shekara na yanzu 21 ne, amma tace zata jirani idan mun gama school sai muyi aure"

Tun da kanin nashi yafara magana ya zuba mishi ido har ya gama yana kallonshi, Ruma ce ta shigo ɗakin bata ganshi a part nasu ba tasan yana wurin mai martaba ko kuma yana nan, Saf ne ya gaisheta ta amsa a tsanake, kallon Junayd tayi tana yamutsa fuska, a hankali ta zauna a cinyarshi tana shafa fuskarshi, baki takai saitin kumatunshi tayi mishi kiss, tasa hannu a aljihun wandonshi ta ciro Key sannan ta miƙe tana taku cikin isa tabar falon.

Kallon Safwan yayi wanda ya dukar da kai kasa yana wasa da yatsun kafarshi.

Takadda ya ɗauka ya rubuta mishi kamar haka.

"Kagani ai da idonka ko? Kaga yadda nake fama da Ruma?                 ~Bacci yake cikin kwanciyar hankali har yanzu hannunshi yana kan cikinshi, a cikin bacci yafara mafarkin yarinyar da kullum sai ya ganta amma baya ganin fuskarta, har yau ma ihu take tana kiran sunanshi daya taimaketa ya cirota daga cikin ruwan datake, a firgice ya tashi yana salati ganin ya saki hannunta ta faɗi ciki, kallon inda yake kwance yayi, ruwa yaga ya jiƙa Sofan da mamaki ya kuma kai hannunshi yaji wurin a jike, a mafarki ruwan ya bayyana gashi kuma ya ganshi a zahiri, da sauri ya sauka yana salati a zuciyarshi, waya ya dauko ya laluɓo number Ibtisam yayi mata Text "kina lafiya?" Kasancewa ita a boarding school take, amsa tayi mishi da lafiya ta kalau Yayana.

Hamdala yayi ya tashi ya kunna Ac yakuma kunna fanka, so yake kujeran ya bushe, cikin Bedroom ya nufa tayi bacci ta ɗaura wayar a kirjinta, da alama tana karatu baccin ya ɗauketa, saida ya cire wandon jikinshi dama tun a Falo ta kwaɓe mishi rigan, wani karamin wando yasa, yakai ɗayan cikin washing machine, kashe wutan ɗakin yayi, ya haura Bed ɗin, wayar yacire daga kirjinta ya kashe ya jona mata a caji, dim light ya kunna nan Gadon ya ɗau wani haske me ɗan duhu, blue ɗakin ya koma, a hankali ya matso wurinta ya rungumeta ta baya yana sauke ajiyar zuciya, acikin bacci taji an riketa da sauri ta cire hannunshi tana turo baki, itafa bataso ana taɓata musamman idan tana bacci ta tsani takura wallahi.

Shikuma Yarima yanason jikin mutum, so yake yaji shi a jikinta, kodan laluran dayake ɗauke dashi ya dace taji tausayinshi ta jashi jiki, ya so ya hanata wannan karatun amma ta nuna mishi Sarauta da sarauta basa tafiya daidai, Gashi mai martaba yana biye mata, Pillow ya janyo ya rungume, baiji daɗi ba hakan yasa yacire Pillow yayi wurgi dashi, janyota yayi da karfi ya haɗata da jikimshi, so take ta kwace ya matseta da karfi, dan dole ta hakura tafara bacci, tana sonshi shiyasa bazata takurashi sosai ba.

Da asuba ya farka, saida yayi alwala kafin ya tasheta tayi sallah, cikin bacci tace "To zan tashi" fita yayi yaje masallaci ya idar da salla, Fada yaje suka gaisa da Sarki, acan ya tadda Ammi da Umman Muneer zama yayi suka fara hira gaba ɗayansu, Auta ne yazo cikin shirin school, uniform ne a jikinshi riga baki da zanen fari, sai takalmi baki, sai kuma necktie da jakanshi na gefe, yayi kyau sai zuba kamshi yake, gaidasu yayi yana kallon Yayanshi.

Murmushi yayi mishi yace "Na wuce school"
Gida mishi kai yayi alaman Allah bada sa'a "Ameen" yafaɗa domin yana gane Yaren yayan nashi sosai.

Bataso a zagi ɗan nata shiyasa take goya mishi baya, har yafita tana kallon bayanshi kamar ta mike tayi mishi duka takeji.

Wayarshi ya ciro ya rubuta kowa ya fita abar mutane biyu akanshi, fita sukayi atare, sukabar mutane biyu a kanshi, suna fita Asad ya kalleshi hannunshi cikin aljihun rigan doctor yace "Junayd a kullum Addu'a ta shine Allah yasa kafara magana kamar yadda kowa yake yi, kana taimako sosai Allah yabiya ka da gidan Aljanna"

Jinjina kai yayi yanayi mishi alama da shikam zai tafi gida, cikin wasa Asad yace "Ruma tana jiranka kenan"

"I wish that Amma hakan bazai taɓa faruwa ba" yafaɗa a ranshi, a fili kuma ya harari Asad ɗin kafin ya mika mishi hannu suka gaisa, wurin motarshi yaje yashiga sannan yafara tuki cikin nutsuwa, waka ya kunna na Rema,  a hanya ya hango wani shagon Chocolate tsayawa yayi yafito daga motar, yana shiga shagon mutane suka fara shirin fita, ɗaga musu hannu yayi alaman su zauna, baida fara'a shiyasa da an ganshi sai a zata yanada girman kai, kuma Yarima ne dole a bashi girma, kwalin Chocolate sun Kai biyar ya ɗibo yazo wurin payment, ATM nashi ya miƙa musu, kin karɓa sukayi sukace sun bar mishi, wannan dalilin ne yasa bai fiye zuwa siyan abu  da kanshi ba, basa karɓan kuɗin hakan kuma ba daɗi yake mishi ba, godiya yayi musu sannan ya koma mota, Driving ya fara yana tunanin rayuwa, gashi Allah ya bashi komai, duk wani kyaun halitta na ɗa namiji Allah yabashi saide baya iya magana, iyayenshi sunce ba haka aka haifeshi ba daga baya ne abin ya sameshi, yayi dasu su faɗa mishi ya akayi hakan ta faru amma kowa sai kame kame yake mishi.

                ~A cikin unguwa sai ɗaga mishi hannu ake, kasancewar ya sauke glass ɗin motar, ganin ɗaga hannun yayi yawa yasa ɗage glass din, tinted ne babu me ganinshi saide shi ya gansu.

A bakin kofar gidansu ya tsaya, ganin dogarai suna zaune suna hira yasa yaji inama ace shima yanada bakin magana haka, duk da shi ba ma'abocin son surutu bane Amma yanada burin yaga shima yana magana, Buɗe mishi makeken Get ɗin akayi a hankali ya danna hancin motar zuwa cikin gidan, da Mamakinshi yaga itama Ruma Yanzu take gyara Parking, to Ina ta tsaya da har sai karfe 5 zata dawo? Taɓe baki yayi yana gyara Parking ɗinshi, Fitowa yayi yana miƙa, tana ganinshi tayi murmushi tafito daga motar Tata, rufe marfin yayi yakama hanya zai shiga cikin gida,  ganin haka yasa ta taɓe Baki itama ta nufi hanyan, yau kowa yanaji da na sarauta.

A Falo yaga kowa suna zaune suna cin abinci, ciki harda mai martaba, dama yunwa yakeji jonasu yayi ya zauna a gefen Sarki, yana kallon Warmer da suka cika da abinci na alfarma, ganin Abbanshi yanashan ferfesu shima ya mika hannu ya ɗibi ferfesun kayan ciki yafara sha, saida ya cinye ya ɗau Apple yanaci, yaɗau inibi yaci sannan yasha ruwa ya mike zai tafi, yana ganin Ruma tana cin abinci baiko kulata ba yashige ciki.

Umman Muneer ce tace "Ruma ya karatu?"

"Alhmdllh Umma karatu da godiya"

"Tom Masha Allah ubangiji ya cika Miki burinki ki dage da karatu ki dage sosai kinji ƴata?"

Cikin jin daɗi Ruma tace "insha Allah Umma Suwaiba zan dage"

Ammi na jinsu batace komai ba, tasan da gayya Suwaiba tayi maganar ta lura Junayd baya samun kulawa shiyasa.

Abba ma yanaji baice komai ba, Muneer dayake jin haushin Junayd ɗin daɗin Shawaran da Ummanshi ta bayar yaji, shifa da za'ace Junayd ya mutu da yafi kowa jin daɗi.

Akan Sofa ya kwanta sanyin Ac yana ratsashi har bacci ya ɗauke shi.

Tana shigowa ta ganshi a kwance itama baccin zakeda bukata dan yau sun gaji da karatu, can kasa ta kwanta bayan ta cire kayan jikinta ta rage daga ita sai karamin wando da half vest.




              "Adda Surayya gaskiya hannunki da zafi shiyasa nafi gane Kitson Kulu wallahi, Aneesa tayi maganan tana turo karamin bakinta, yayinda take zaune a gaban Surayya gashin kanta a taje ya kara tsawo da cika, duk da bai taju me kyau ba, saboda taki yadda wai zafi yake mata, itafa dama ba son kitso take ba, tafi gane a kame mata shi biyu ta sake a gefen wuyanta tayi adonta taje ta saida nono ta dawo.

"Ai dole hannuna yafi na Kulu zafi tunda ita Kulu tana binki a hankali nikuma banida wannan lokacin" Surayya datake sauri tayi maganar, so take su tafi talla kada suyi rana, Aneesa sai rurrufe ido take tana cije baki, da kyar suka gama guda shida sauran sai sun dawo, Wanke kafa tayi ta shirya cikin kayan Fulani kamar yadda suka saba, kundra tasa ta ɗau Kwaryan Nono, itama Surayya shiri tayi tasa kayanta, fitowa sukayi da Kwaryan akansu, Baba na shirin fita daji shima, aka kawo wata mara lafiya, komawa yayi ciki domin jin abinda ya sameta.

Cutan kuturta ne yake damunta, Baba yace su zauna a nan zuwa gobe zai nemo musu wani magani wanda zai taimaka mata, Aneesa ce ta kalli Surayya tana buɗe baki, anan zata kwana kenan? Tayi mata alama da ido, Kawar da kai Surayya tayi tace "muje ko"

Tafiya suka fara Aneesa tace "Adda? Kenan anan zasu kwana? Nikam banson mutum kazami ya zauna mana a Ruga wallahi"

"Ke ɗin tsafta ne dake?"

Shiru tayi tana murguɗa baki, ƴan kauyen suke gaisarwa, Aneesa sai wanda jininta ya haɗu dashi take gaishesu, da haka har suka isa wurin saida Nono, karamin kasuwa ne wanda yake cike da mutane, wasu na saida Nono wasu kuma ɗanyen rogo, wasu suyayyen dankali, masu suya kosai suna gefe, Abu dai iri iri acikin kasuwar, Aneesa a karkashin wani bishiyan darbejiya ta ajiye kwaryanta, itama Surayya haka, basu daɗe ba, akazo aka siye na Aneesa, danƙawa Surayya kuɗin tayi tace "zan dawo yanzu"

"Aneesa ina zakije kuma? Bazaki tsaya nasaida nawa mutafi gida ba?"

"Adda kinsan Bama iya zuwa nan har nakoma gida banje bakin kogi ba ko? Kinsan dole ne naji nayi wasa a cikin Ruwa"

"Shikenan ki dawo da wuri kuma kibi a hankali kinsan yanayin garin namu"

"Ba komai" saida tasiyi kosai tanaci tana tafiya, kana ganinta kasan akwai Wauta da yaranta a kanta, domin tana tafiyane tana waka kaɗan kaɗan, tayi tafiya ne dan nisa kafin ta hango kogin, Murmushi tayi domin a rayuwa tanajin shauki idan tana cikin kogin nan, ƙarasawa tayi tana kallon yadda mutane suke wanki a gefe, wasu kuma suna cikin ruwan, wasu masoya kuma kafafuwansu suka zuba a ruwan suna hiransu.

Wuri mai inuwa ta samu ta zauna,fararen dogayen kafafuwanta ta zuba a cikin ruwan ta ɗibo kananan duwatsu tana jefawa aciki, karan faɗuwan dutsen yanayi mata daɗi sosai, wani nutsuwa ne taji yana sauko mata a cikin jikinta.

A hankali ta kumshe kyawawan fararen idanunta, eyelashes nata ne ya sauka har wurin dogon hancinta, wani irin Murmushi take wanda yake bayyana sihirtaccen kyawun da Allah yayi mata, gefen kumatunta yana lotsawa (Dimple).

Wasu samari biyu ne suka ganta ɗayan yace "Kai Babu? Kaga wata kyakkyawa" yayi maganan da harshen fulatanci.

"Kai wannan fa Aneesa ce ƴar Rugan Malam Arɗo, kada kayi mata magana zata yi maka rashin mutunci"

Basu mata magana ba suka wuce, murmushin gefen baki tayi, dama da sun mata magana bazata yimusu rashin mutunci ba, amma tunda basuyi ba babu damuwa, batason kula samaran kauyen nasu, domin da farko idan sun auri mace rimi-rimi kamar zasu haɗiyeta sai daga baya su fara bawa yarinya wahala kamar zasu kashe ta, shiyasa Aneesa bata damu da soyayya ba, tafi damuwa da talla cikin rufin asiri ta rufawa kanta da iyayenta Asiri.

Saida ta shafe kusan Awa biyu a bakin kogi kafin ta mike cikin gajiya tana shirin tashi, ji tayi kamar zata faɗi wani irin ihu ta kwala tana salati da kyar tasamu tasa kafarta waje, numfashi me nauyi ta sauke, wannan kogin baya sabo da ita ne? Kullum tana zuwa amma sai yayi kamar zai kadata idan tazo tashi? Tana surutu har tabar wurin, Surayya ta siyar da nata itama tun ɗazu, ganin Aneesa bata zo ba yasa tafara taya wata mata saida Dankali a wurin, Aneesa tana dawowa ta ɗau Kwaryan tace "muje"
Harara ta banƙa mata.

"Kiyi hakuri Adda Surayya bada so na bane na jima kinsan yadda nakejin daɗin bakin kogi ai"

Shiru kawai tayi mata, ranta ya ɓaci domin batason ta rinƙa yimata faɗa, tafison su zama kamar kawaye ta yadda Aneesa bazata ɓoye mata komai na rayuwanta ba, wani lokacin Gara kanwarka ta faɗa maka matsalarta akan ta faɗawa Kawarta, su kawaye yanzu ba abin yadda bane.

Tafiya suke Aneesa tace "Yanzu Adda mu haka zamuci gaba da zama cikin Kauyennan muna saida Nono bawani ci gaba?"

"To yaya zamuyi haka muka tarar da iyayenmu sunayi dole mu bisu yadda suke so, ko so kike mu ɓata musu al'adarsu?"

"Nikam bance haka ba, amma kullum daga saida nono sai komawa gida babu wani cigaba, nifa ko karatu ban iya ba, saide na Allo ne na iya kaɗan kaɗan, Ni gaskiya Inson ci gaba a rayuwata"

Gaskiya take faɗa Amma ai yanzu tayi ƙanƙanta domin bazata wuce 17 ba a shekaru
"Aneesa kefa yarinya ce, baki kai shekara goma sha takwas ba, Bakida yadda zakiyi da rayuwarki sai yadda iyayenki sukayi dake"

Shiru Aneesa tayi badan taso ba, Ita kanta tasan tanada kokari gashi sunashan madara kullum, dole kwakwalwarsu ta buɗe, amma babu karatun boko babu na addini sai saida Nono.
Allah ya kawo mana mafita, tafaɗa a zuciyarta.

Sun isa gida lafiya, Surayya ce ta fara girki, Aneesa batason girki kuma ga bakuwan da Baba Yace ta zauna a gidansu, fita tayi da sunan zata ɗibo kara, jin haka yasa Mama ta kyaleta, a haɗe da Batajin daɗi tun da safe yau.

Aneesa saida taje Rugan su Kulu ta ɗaukota kafin sukaje daji domin ɗibo kara, saida sukayi hira sukayi ta shashanci kafin suka dawo kusan bayan sallan Mangariba, Aneesa hannunta rike da wasu kara kanana kaɗan, sai haƙi take wai ta gaji, tana sallama ta ga Hamma Umar Zaune akan kujera yana kallon lokacin da zata shigo, jikinta ne yafara ɓari ganin yadda ya 
Haɗe fuska yana aika mata kallon daga ina kike?

Shima yana kama dasu, yama fi kama Da Aneesa domin bambancin su shi yanada saje ita kuma bata dashi, manyan idanunta take fitarwa waje tana kallon kasa.

Yayi kyau acikin Dressing na ƴan birni, idan ka ganshi zakace ba a wannan rugan ya fito ba.

Bakinta yana rawa tace "Itace naje ɗiba"

Baiyi magana ba sai kallonta yake, kamar zatayi kuka takara cewa "Itace naje ɗiba wallahi Tallahi na maka rantsuwan musulmi, idan karya Azara ya hanani kwanciyar kabari"

"Da karfe nawa kikaje?" Yayi magana da wani zazzaƙan murya, tace "Da karfe 5"

Hawaye ya cika idonta saura kaɗan su zubo "zo nan"

Ajiye karan tayi ta karasa wajenshi ta durkusa, tsoronshi take sosai domin karamin aikinshi ne ya kamata ya zane, hatta Surayya dukanta yake balle ita karan kaɗa miya, kayan dayake gefenshi ya ɗauka yace "Oya gashi ɗauki ki wanke"

Karɓa tayi jiki na rawa, ta ɗibo ruwa ta fara wanki, saida yayi alwalan isha yafita kafin ta jiƙa kayan ta shanya sannan ta gudu ɗakinsu.

                ~Bayan ya dawo yaga kayan a jike akan igiya, dama yasan za'ayi haka, kiranta yayi, tana ɗaki a lungun gado, saida ta idar da sallan mangrib da isha kafin taja bargo tayi shiru kamar bai bacci, Surayya tanaji tace "tayi bacci"

"Gobe zata tashi ai" shine abinda yafaɗa ya wuce ɗakinshi, yanason Aneesa amma ya lura tanada raini sosai, shiyasa yakeso ta rinƙa jin tsoronshi bayaso ta rainashi ko kaɗan.

Dariya ta baiwa Surayya ganin yadda ta taƙure tana shirin yin baccin dole "tashi to mu karasa Kitson"

"Barshi sai gobe Adda"
"Kitashi da Allah shigowa zaiyi ne?"

A hankali ta mike tana leka kofan, zafi takeji a cikin dakin domin ɗakin kasa ne, kanta ta kwantar a cinyar Surayya, Kitson tafara yimata har tayi bacci, yau Aneesa ce batayi kukan kitso da surutu ba? Lalle Boss ya dawo.

Saida ta gama mata, ta kwantar da ita akan shimfiɗar dayake kasa, matashi tasa mata wanda yasa Aneesa sauke ajiyan zuciya cikin bacci.

Kwanciya tayi a gefenta ta ɗaga kanta sama tana tunanin maganar da Aneesa tayi mata ɗazu.

"Aneesa yarinya ce Amma tafini tunani me kyau, babu ci gaba acikin wannan ƙauyen babu malamai babu ruwa isashe sai bakin kogi, babu abinci me kyau sai nono da dambu, sai ayi wata ɗaya basuyi shinkafa ba, saide tuwon dawa da miyan kuka ko Lawashi, tayi aure bataji daɗi ba, gashi idan batayi Sa'a ba acikin kauyen zata kara yin auren, a haka ƴaƴan ta zasu tashi suma sukara dawwama acikin kauyen, haka kuma Aneesa zatayi aure a kauyen ta kara dawwama aciki? Allah kaine mafi sanin Daidai ka kawo mana ɗauki cikin gaggawa Ameen"
Batayi bacci ba saida takai kusan karfe ɗaya, ganin Baccin yaki zuwa ta mike ta ɗibo ruwa a buta tayi alwala, tazo tafara salla bata wani iya karatun salla sosai ba, amma tana iya kokarinta domin taga tayi sallan daidai, saida ta idar tayita addu'a, addu'an nata yafi yawa akan Aneesa.

Tanason Kanwar Tata sosai, shiyasa ta dage a wurin Allah tana Roƙan ya bawa Kanwar Tata mafita Ameen.

Kusan 3 kafin ta ninke sallaya ta kwanta.

Aneesa sai bacci take dama ta gaji da yawo, gashi taje daji dole ta gaji ai, baccinta take cikin kwanciyar hankali da rashin damuwa.


  *Washe gari*

Aneesa ta tashi da ciwon ciki sosai, tunda Asuba take murƙususu akan Gado, ɗankwalin kanta ta kunce tana birgima harda ihu, azaba takeji ba kaɗan ba, Amai takeyi kamar zata amayar da hanjin cikinta, Baba dayake tsaye a bakin kofa yana ganin yadda ta galabaita ta fita a hayyacinta, fuskarta tayi fayau, bata iya ɗago ido ta kalli mutum me kyau, hannunta yanakan cikinta tana matsawa da karfi.

Surayya na tsaye itama ta rike kwankwaso ta rasa abinyi sai sannu take aikin faɗa mata, Mama na saman gado tana kallon Aneesa wacce take kuka sosai.

Hamma Umar ne ya shigo hannunshi rike da wani bakin leda ya mikawa Baba, Yana karɓa ya ce abashi cokalin kwarya, bashi akayi ya ɗibo ruwa kaɗan yasa maganin aciki, wurinta yaje yace ta buɗe bakinta, batason magani amma azaban datake karɓa yasa dole ta buɗe baki tana karɓan maganin.

Saida ta shanye tass kafin ta koma ta kwanta tana cigaba da jujjuya kai, dogon hancinta ya koma jajur.

Fita Baba da Hamma Umar sukayi, ba'afi minti talatin da shan maganin ba, taji wani abu yana saukowa daga kasanta zuwa farin zanin Fulani dayake jikinta, a hankali ta mike tana duba ko menene, ganin jini ya ɓata mata jiki ta kwala ihu tana rike Mama da karfin tsiya.

"Ke menene?"

"Mama shikenan mutuwa zanyi jini yafito daga jikina Mama mutuwa zanyi"

Kallon zaninta Mama tayi yanzu ta gane abinda yake damun Aneesa, Al'ada zata fara kenan shiyasa yake sata ciwon ciki sosai haka? a hankali tafara bata hakuri itada Surayya sunayi mata bayani.

Kunya taji sosai, Mama tace taje ta shirya kanta a banɗaki, da Taimakon Surayya ta kimtsa jikinta, Saida ta dawo ɗaki mama tace.

"Buɗe kunnenki ki jini, kinga wannan abin da kika fara? Idan kika sake namiji ya taɓa hannunki sai kinyi ciki, ciki irin na Altine ƴar Rugan Malam Buba, kuma mutanen kauye suyi ta miki dariya suna nuna ki, nasan baki son wasa da maza amma idan kika kuskura kika fara wasa da maza sai kinyi ciki kina jina?"

A tsorace tace "Eh Mama dama bana wasa da maza"

"Yawwa Aneesan Baba, ga magani acan idan kinci abinci sai kisha ba?"
Giɗa kai tayi takasa sakin jikinta har yanzu a tsorace take.

Hamma Umar dama yazo hutun kwana biyu ne, gobe zai Koma school insha Allah.


             "Akwai wani me magani da zaizo Anjima Ku fadawa Yarima ya shirya" mai martaba ke yiwa Jakadiya bayani, amasawa tayi tana mikewa.

Ba ɓata lokaci aka sanar da Yarima mai magani zaizo Anjima, shifa ya gaji da magani kullum magani gashi har yau ba'a dace ba? 

Yau Weekend shiyasa suke gida gaba ɗayansu, bayan sun cinye breakfast ya kalli Ruma yana lumshe ido, tasan me yake buƙata haɗe fuska tayi tana shirin tashi a wurin, hannunta ya riƙo ya janyota ya ɗaurata a cinyarshi, akan kujeran Dining yake, a hankali yasa hannu cikin kasan Riganta yana shafa cikinta, da sauri tafara zamewa itafa gajiya ne bataso, shi baya hakura da ya fara abu ɗaya sai taji bayanta kamar tayi ihu kafin ya kyaleta, rike hannunshi tayi tana langwaɓar da kai.

Bai kulata ba yaci gaba da shafa cikinta, a hankali yake sama da hannunshi har yakai kan Breast nata wanda tasa bra, ɓalle bra yayi sannan ya ɗaga Riganta ya cire, cire bra ɗinma yayi ya zubawa kirjinta ido, a hankali yakai bakinshi kan ɗayan yafara lasa, ɗayan hannunshi kuma ya ɗaura akan ɗayan yana matsawa, numfashi yake fitarwa da sauri da sauri.

Fara kwace kanta tayi dan taga yafara kunnuwa sosai, ganin haka yasa ya ɗagata cakk ya wuce Bedroom da ita, bai tsaya ko ina ba sai kan makeken Bed ɗinshi, kwantar da ita yayi ganin zata tashi yabita ya danne, hannu yasa ya kwance Belt ɗin wandonshi, idan yae zai biye Ruma to babu shakka zai yiwa kanshi illa, saida ya maidasu Naked kafin yafara bin jikinta da lasa, shiru tayi tana ɗan biye mishi badan taso ba.

Bakinshi ya haɗa da nata hannunshi na kan Breast ɗinta yanayi musu wani irin matsa wanda ya nuna yayi missing ɗinta sosai.

Biye mishi tayi tana bashi haɗin kai, a hankali yafara karanto addu'a a cikin zuciyarshi wani irin Ajiyan zuciya ya sauke lokacin daya samu yashiga jikin Ruma, tana shiga hakkinshi yanason abin sosai amma bata bashi haɗin kai.

Yayi kusan 1hour yana abu ɗaya, ganin ta gaji tafara tureshi tana kuka, so yake ya takaita amma ya kasa, yanaso ya bita a hankali amma ai itace take jawo hakan tunda ba kullum take yadda dashi ba.
Saida yakara kusan 30mins kafin ya kyaleta ya koma gefe, badan ya isheshi ba.

Sauka tayi akan gadon a fusace tana hararanshi, wanka taje tayi tadawo ɗakin tana tsaki, waya ya rubuta mata "wa kikewa tsaki?"

Ba kunya tace "Kai"
Wani irin zazzafan mari ya wanke fuskarta dashi, sa'anta ne shi da zata mishi tsaki? Babu abinda ya tsana kamar ayi mishi tsaki "Bazan taɓa yafewa ba,har zaka mareni dan nayi tsaki? Ka gama duk abinda Zakayi dani yanzu kuma kazo kana bina da duka?" Tsaki ta kuma ja me karfi, mari ya Kuma kai mata wanda yasa ta rike fuska ta durkusa tana ihu.

Waya yaciro ya rubuta "niba sa'anki bane kuma dan na karbi hakƙina a wajenki shine kike cewa nagama abinda zanyi dake? Wallahi zan ɓaɓɓallaki idan kika kara yimin tsaki ko da kinga ina ɗaga miki kafa"

Karantawa tayi takuma jan wani tsakin, Ruma akwai taurin kai, wannnan karon wani mahaukacin mari yayi mata wanda yasa tafara ganin abu uku uku, kanta ne ya bugu da bangon ɗakin, yana nufota tana ja da baya, yau kaɗai yaji bakin cikin rashin maganar dayakeyi.

"Bazaiyu ka auroni ka maidani jaka ba, dame gidanku sukafi namu?sarauta ko mulki? Kuɗi ko kwanciyar hankali? A kuɗi dai kasan saide ubana ya kara da naka ko?"

Jin kalamanta yasa ya zaro Belt yayo kanta ya ringa zabga mata tana ihu tana rike Belt ɗin, saida yayi mata duka me kyau kafin ya barta awurin, domin idan yaci gaba da tsayuwa sai yayi mata illa.

A hankali ta mike tana gyara ɗaurin Towel ɗin jikinta, gaban madubi taje tana kallon fuskarta, ya kumbura ga shatin mari jikinta ya nuna shatin Belt, ihu tayi tasa hannu a jikin madubin ta buga, nan madubi ya tarwatse ya zube a kasa, kayan mai dasuke gaban Drower ta watsar kasa, masu fashewa suka fashe masu kara sukayi kara.

Hakan bai mata ba ta rinƙa buga kanta da jikin bango tana kuka, yana cikin Toilet duk abinda takeyi yana jinta, kanshi ya sakarwa shower yanajin sanyin ruwan yana bin duk wani kofan dayake ɗauke da gashi na jikinshi, ta saba haka idan ranta ya ɓaci tayi ta illata kanta, barinta yayi idan taji zafi zata daina.

Buga kanta take da bango tana marin fuskarta kamar wacce ta haukace, ganin bai fito ba, taje ta fara buga glass ɗin window nan suka fara fashewa, karamin Towel ya ɗaura yafito, jin zata ɓata mishi ɗaki, yana ganinta ya riko hannunta da karfi yanufi ɗakinta, babu me shiga part nasu shiyasa yafita ahaka.

Tana fizgewa tana bugunshi har da cizo saida ya kaita cikin ɗaki kafin ya ɗau igiya ya ɗaureta a jikin gadon ya fita ya rufe kofar, ihu ta fara tana kiran sunanshi, dawowa yayi cikin nutsuwa ya buɗe wani Drower yaciro solatep yazo ya manne bakinta, tana fizge kanta har yagama yafita yabarta a dakin.

Ɗakinshi yaje yayi wankan Tsarki kafin yazo ya shafa mai yasa jayan shan iska ya nufi Lambun dayake cikin gidan nasu.

Bakin swimming pool ya zauna yasa kafarshi cikin ruwan, wasu kananan duwatsu ya ɗibo yana jefawa cikin ruwan, ji yayi wani nutsuwa yana sauko mishi, a duk lokacin da ranshi ya ɓaci idan yazo cikin ruwan yana wasa dashi sai yaji zuciyarshi tayi sanyi kamar kankara.

Saida ya tabbatar tayi shiru ta gaji kafin ya mike yakoma cikin gidan, buɗe ɗakinta yayi yana kallon yadda kanta yake kasa, gashin kanta sun zubo zuwa fuskarta, fuskar tayi jajur, bakinta har rawa yake, jikinta yayi jaa sosai sannan ta rufe ido Alaman tana baccin wahala, kwanceta yayi, ya gyara mata gashin da suka zubo kan fuskarta, ya maidasu baya ya kame da roba balm, cire towel ɗin yayi ya ɗauko wata ƴar karamar riga pink yasa mata, a hankali ya kwantar da ita akan gadon ya kunna Ac yaja mata Blanket, kashe wutan ɗakin yayi yafita.

Komawa cikin ruwan yayi wannan lokacin da tufa a hannunshi yanaci, wayarshi yaji yana Ruri, yana ɗagawa yaga mai martaba ne, Amsawa yayi ya kara a kunnenshi, "kazo mai magani ya karaso"

Badan yaso ba ya mike, ya koma ɗaki saida yasa kaya manya kafin yafita zuwa cikin fada,
Zaune suke gaba ɗaya su Ammi su Umman Muneer da Muneer ɗin da Saf dukka suna ɗakin.

A hankali ya zauna a gefen Abba, gaishesu yayi da Yaren kurame, kowa ya amsa, Mai magani ya karaso da jakarshi a hannu , dudduba Yarima yayi sannan yace "ɗan buɗe baki kamar Zakayi magana dai muji"

Gwada buɗe baki yayi yanaso yayi magana amma yaji bakin yayi mishi nauyi.
Kallonshi mai magani yayi yace "gaskiya yallaɓai bazanyi muku karya ba, bazan iya bada wannan magani ba, kada na cuceku nima Allah zai nunamin tun a duniya, maganin wannan yaron baya nan garin yana wani kauye me nisan gaske bazan fada muku inda zaku samu kauyen ba amma inaso yayita sallan dare ya roki Allah ya nuna mishi inda kauyen yake, shine iya taimakon da zan iya" 
Yayi maganar ne domin yaga Alaman akwai mugaye a kewaye da Yarima, idan ya faɗi inda me maganin yake zasu iya zuwa kafin shi suyiwa meshi illa ko kuma suyi wani abun na daban.

Sarki ya fahimci hakan, sai kawai yayi mishi Godiya ya bashi Alkhairi masu yawa ya sallameshi.
Kallon Yarima yayi yace "kaji me yace ko."

Alaman Eh yayi wa Abba, hira suka danyi, Umman Muneer tace "Ina Rumasa'u ne?"
Kallonta yayi bata taɓa tambayarta a daidai wannan lokacin ba sai yau? Ko dai tasan abinda yayiwa Ruma ɗinne?
Hannu ya nuna mata Alaman tana ɗaki.

Murmushin gefen baki tayi tace "Allah sarki bacci take?"
Da mamaki ya giɗa mata kai.

Kallon Munner tayi shima ya kalleta, Ammi ta fahimci da wata a kasa, bari tayi sai Anjima zata tambayi Junayd ɗin.

Wani zafi taji yana ziyartan jikinta a hankali ta mike tana kallon shatin Belt da kanta wanda ya fashe ta jikin madubi, hannunta wanda ya tsage da madubin daya fashe ta duba, ruwan ɗumi sosai ta haɗa tashiga tayi wanka tana runtse ido, har wani zazzaɓi taji yana shirin sauko mata jikinta yayi zafi, tasan ɓacin ran Junayd babu kyau amma meyasa zaiyi mata wannan dukan?
Lips nata sai rawa suke sun koma jawur, dama Ajebo ce batason wahala, riga mara nauyi tasa, tafito Falo ta buɗe Frij taciro Youghurt ta buɗe tana sha.
Akan Sofa ta zauna ta taƙure wuri guda.

A hankali ya murɗa handle ɗin yana shigowa, ganin ta tashi yasa ya haɗe fuska yazo gabanta ya ajiye plate ɗin dayake Hannunshi, juya mishi baya tayi tana share hawaye, tausayi tabashi, a hankali ya zauna a gefenta, janyota yayi jikinshi, babu musu ta kwanta luff a kirjinshi tana sauke ajiyan zuciya, abincin kan plate din ya ɗibo a spoon yakai bakinta, kin karɓa tayi sai hawayen dayake bin kumatunta, juyo da ita yayi yana kallon yadda Lips nata yake rawa, hannu yasa yafara bin Lips ɗinta da yatsanshi ɗaya, matso da fuskarta yayi zuwa nashi, a hankali yasa Lips nashi kan nata, harshenshi ya tura mata cikin bakinta, tsotsa tafara a hankali tana kallon cikin idonshi, saida yaga ta ɗan sakko kafin ya cire bakinshi daga nata yafara bata abincin, ba laifi taci kaɗan, 
tun yanason Ruma har tafara fita a ranshi saboda halayenta amma ya zaiyi? dole ya kula da ita saboda matarshi ce.

*Chapter 7*

*_Arewabooks @Jiddasmapi_*


                ~A hankali take sauke ajiyan zuciya har bacci ya kara ɗaukanta, shafa kanta yake a hankali, saida tayi nisa ya kwantar da ita yana kallon fuskarta.
Fita yayi ya koma Part nashi yayi alwala yayi sallah.


Da dare tashi yayi, sallah yafara jerawa yana addu'an Allah ya nuna mishi inda zai samu maganin cutanshi, saida yayi Sallah sosai kafin ya kwanta yayi shirin bacci, bai wani kula da Ruma ba dan yasan koda yaje wajenta yanzu ba dolene yasamu abinda yake so ba.
Acikin bacci yafara mafarki kamar yadda ya saba koda yaushe idan ya kwanta, yauma kamar kullum a cikin ruwa take tana kokarin faɗuwa tana cewa ya cirota, bai sani ba har ta faɗa cikin ruwan.

Mafarkin har yafara zame msihi jiki.

"Washe gari yakama Lahadi yauma ana Weekend, a lambu yake kwance yana tunani kamar yadda ya saba kullum, idan baida aiki saide yazo lambu ya kwanta, ganin baida nutsuwa yasashi mikewa yaje wurin swimming pool yasa kafafuwanshi, nutsuwa yaji yana sauko mishi a hankali.

Saf ne yazo yana karanta jarida a hannunshi, ganin Ƴayanshi a lambu yazo ya zauna a gefenshi shima yasa kafarshi cikin ruwan, da sauri ya cire jin sanyi yana shiga jikinshi, kallon Junayd yayi yana mamakin yadda yayanshi baya jin sanyin ruwa, kullum saiya zauna a wurin ruwan, gefe ya koma yana cigaba da karatunshi, Ammi ce tazo wurin itada bayi guda biyu a bayanta, hannunsu rike da basket cike da kayan Fruit, hango Junayd a bakin ruwa yana jefa duwatsu yasa taji tausayinshi ya kamata, yana bukatan kulawa, yanason yajishi a jikin mutum ko dan laluran dayake sashi, saide Allah bai bashi mace ba, gani take kamar daidai take dashi, idan kuɗi ne itama suna dashi, idan sarauta ne itama Gimbiya ce bawai saida tazo gidansu tasamu sunan ba, idan wayewa ne Shima akwaishi, shiyasa take yiwa yaron mata Addu'a Allah Ubangiji ya bashi mace ta gari wacce zata kula dashi, wacce zata bashi haɗin kai a duk lokacin dayake sa bukatar hakan.

Kallon bayin tayi tace "ku kai mishi nasan yana so su"
Kai mishi Basket ɗin sukayi a hankali ta karaso wurin itama, zama tayi a wani dakali dayake gefen ruwan, a hankali tace "Gobe mai martaba zai fita kuma zaiyi kwana biyu shi sa waziri, fada zai dawo hannunka na kwana biyu"

Kallon Ammi yayi, shifa baison wannan rike fada ɗin yana amincewa ne saboda Amminshi tana fushi idan yaki, murmushi yayi mata a hankali ya giɗa mata kai, saida ta ɗan jima tana yanka mishi Fruit ɗin yana karɓa yanaci kafin ta mike ta zata tafi.

Saf dayake zaune a gefe ya shagwaɓe fuska cikin shagwaɓa yace "Ammi Ni bazaki bani Fruit ɗin ba?"
Dariya tayi tace "kai kaci da hannunka, jimin yaro fa kishi kake da yayan naka?"
Turo baki yayi yana kallon Ammi.

Tafiya tayi tana dariya, wani abin idan Saf yayi ko ibti bazatayi ba ita da take auta.
Yanzu shi suke cewa Auta domin shine ya ɗauki halin Autan.

Junayd yana jinsu saide shi yau hankalinshi ya koma kan maganar da Mutumin yayi musu jiya na cewar maganinshi yana wani kauye, haka kawai yaji yana yadda da maganar mutumin, Addu'a yake Allah ya nuna mishi inda maganinshi yake.


              "Aneesa ki tashi a bakin ruwan nan kizo ku tafi, wallahi idan kikayi wasa yau saina faɗa wa Mama abinda kike yi"
Kallon Surayya tayi bata cire ƙafan a ruwa ba tace "kema fa Adda kinason zama a wurin ruwan nan, kuma kinsan ba lafiya ne dani ba, ruwan ne yasa nafito talla yau, idan kika fadawa Mama nima saina faɗa mata kin turani gidansu Giɗaɗo"

"A,a ke kuma bakya mantuwa ne? Inace maganar ta wuce ko?"
Turo baki tayi "bai wuce ba"
"To kanwata kiyi hakuri kinji tashi mu tafi gida to"

A hankali ta cire kafarta zata fito taji kamar zata faɗi, riketa Surayya tayi da karfi tace "ki kiyayi ranan da zaki faɗi a cikin ruwan nan"
"To Adda zan kiyaye"
Tafiya sukayi saida ta tsinki Mangoro a hanya ta cika kwaryanta dashi, yau kwana uku kenan, a kwana uku Period ɗin ya dauke, dama Allah Allah take ya tafi dan ya mugun takurata.

Mangoro ta zauna tasha a kofan gida, tasan Hamma Umar ya tafi shiyasa tayi badarinta, wata ƴar budurwace sa'ar Surayya tazo wucewa, kallon Aneesa tayi tace Aneesa? Shan Mangoro a waje?

"Adda mairam wallahi na gaji ne daga saida nono muka dawo nida Adda Surayya"
"To ai bai dace ki ci abu a waje ba kina budurwa"
Dariya tayi dan ance mata budurwa, Innar ku na gida?

"Eh tana ciki"

"To bari nashiga na dubasu na daɗe banzo ta ruganku ba" 
Shiga tayi ta gaida Mama, suka shiga ɗaki da Surayya sunata hira, yaushe Aurenki mairam?

"Aurena saura sati Uku kinsan Baffa ba bayida hakuri yanata masifa wai nayi daɗe a gida na tsaya zaɓe sai rawan ido, duk samarin kauyen nan nakasa shire na aure, shine kawai ta shire Hammadu ɗan Rugan malam Buba"

Dafe kirji Surayya tayi "ɗan Rugan Malam Buba wannan marasa jin? Kinsan gidansu basu da hankali amma ki yadda zaki aureshi? Mairam gaki kyakkyawa ina guje miki irin aurena, babu riba a aurena, kinsan fa ba saurin aure shine farin jini ba, addu'a da neman dace shine a gaba"

"To ya zanyi shurayya?" Hausanta baya fita ko kaɗan, "min ma ba da shona Baffa ya takuramin shoshai Surayya minkam min Boni fa"

"A,a ki daina faɗan haka insha Allah zaki dace kinji Kawata?"
Saida sukayi hira sosai kafin Surayya ta rakata, har yanzu Aneesa na kofa tana kallon duk wani me shiga da fice na Rugan, tana jiran Baba ya dawo shiyasa taki shiga gida, gashi batason aiki, ta iya girki sosai amma batason yi, wanki ma idan taga dama zata wanke duk kayan gidan idan bataga dama ba tun safe har dare tanakan wanke kaya uku.

Baba ne ya dawo da gudu taje ta karɓi ledan hannunshi, "ƴar gidan Baba? Kina jiran dawowana ne?"
Giɗa mishi kai tayi tana dariya, idan tana dariya kamar kada ka daina kallonta, tsabar kyawunta yasa ƴan garin suke kiranta da Boɗɗo, tana dariya har suka isa gida ta ajiye ledan, bata taɓa buɗe ledan da aka kawo har sai idan Baba ne yace ta buɗe.

"Buɗe mana ƴar gidan Baba" tana buɗewa taga lemo da ayaba, dama abinda takeso kenan, ɗauka tayi yace "ɗauki ɗayan ledan ki kai Rugan Baffanku, ɗaukan ledan tayi tanacin ayaba tana tafiya, babu nisa sosai a tsakaninsu, wani rugane babba tashiga, a soro tayi sallama.
Sun amsa a hankali tashiga tana sunnar da kai kasa ganin Hamma Faruk yana Alwalan sallan mangrib, murmushi yayi yace "Aneesan Baba Aneesan Farouk" dariya kawai takeyi tana kallon kasa cikin kunya.
Ganin Innansu a cikin gida tace "ina wuni inna Mairo"

"Aneesa kece da yamman nan?"

"Nice Inna" tayi maganar tana ajiye ledan a gaban Faruk, suna fulanai ne kyawawa dasu, Hamma Faruk ɗinma kyakkyawa ne Chocolate color, har yaso yafi Hamma Umar nasu kyau, da gani kasan jininsu ne, Baban Hamma Faruk yayan Babansu ne, siyasa suke cemishi Baffa, yanada kanne dayawa gidansu babban gidane, akwai ƴammata saura sunyi aure sauran kuma sa'o'in Aneesa ne, suna son Aneesa Amma tanada raini bata fiye kulasu ba, Hamma Faruk yanayi mata tsokana wai ita matarshi ce shiyasa idan ta ganshi takejin kunya.

"Anee wa Ni kaɗai kika kawowa ledan ne?"
"Baba ne yace na kawo muku"
Buɗewa yayi ya ciro ayaba ya ɓare, faraci yayi yace "muje to saina rakaki ko? Kinga su Dija basa nan sunje  Rafi"

"Tom Inna sai yeso"

"A,a Aneesa sai Jango dai nasan bazaki dawo ba"
Dariya tayi kawai suka jera da Hamma Faruk suna tafiya, hira sukeyi irin na yaya da ƙani wanda suka shaƙu da juna, tana kunyarshi amma baya hana suyi hira dashi sosai.
Yawancin matsalolinta tana iya faɗa mishi kuma yana bata shawara sosai, saida suka isa kofa sannan ya juya yace "Aneesan Faruk? Nikam zan tafi masallaci"
Cikin shagwaɓa tace "ka shiga ka gaida Baba mana"

"To ai zanyi laiti Aneesan Baba, Amma Anjima zanzo muyi hira ko?"
Murmushi tayi tace "Tom"
Tana shiga gida Mama tace "kun tsaya da Faruk ko"
Zama tayi tace "wallahi Mama kamar kin sani yanzu ya tafi masallaci nikuma nashigo gida"

Baba ma ya tafi masallaci, kulan abinci ta janyo tana cewa "Allah yasa dambu akayi"
Harara mama tayi mata "dashike mune mayun zogale ai dole kullum mu rinka yin dambu"
Ganin tuwo ne yasa ta haɗa fuska tana rufe kulan, kwarya ta ɗauka ta ɗibi Nono tazo tasa sugar datafara sha, Kallonta Mama tayi saida ta gama tace "Bazakiyi salla bane?"

"Bana salla ai Mama tunda abin can ya sameni"

"Jinin bai dauke bane?"
Cikin kunya tace "ya ɗauke tun da safe"
"To ai idan ya dauke ba'a jinkiri sai kiyi wankan Tsarki kamar yadda malaminku ya koya muku a makarantar Allo, idan mace tana jinkirta wankan Tsarki Allah yana tanada mata azaba me yawa"

Watarana manzon Allah SAW suna wucewa da sahabbai ta wurin wasu kabari, sai Manzon Allah ya tsinki Ganye yasa akan kabari guda uku, sai Sahabbai sukace ya manzon Allah meyasa kasa wannan ganyen akan kabarinnan?
Manzon Allah yace domin a sassauta musu azaban dasuke sha kafin ganyen ya bushe Allah zai sassauta musu, sukace wani laifi sukayi haka har ake musu Azaba?
Sai yace na farko macen tana jinkirta wanka idan jininta ya ɗauke, to kinga ai jingirta wanka yanada matsala.

"To Mama su biyu kuma laifin me yace sunyi?"

*Aneesa gaskiya na manta ki tashi kije kiyi wanka, tunda na manta kinga bai dace nayi miki karya ba"
Tashi tayi taje tayi wanka kamar yadda malam ya koyar mata.

Ruwa ta ɗibo a bokiti sannan tasa kaɗan a buta, hannu biyu tasa ta ɗibo ruwa ta wanke hannunta, sannan ta karkata bokitin tace "niyyatul ghuslul janabati" ma'ana nayi niyyan wankan janaba, ta ɗibo ta wanke daga kasan cibiyanta zuwa cinyarta sau uku, sannan ta wanke hannunta zuwa wuyan hannu sau uku, ta kuskure bakinta sau uku, ta ta shaki ruwa a hanci ta fesar sau uku, sannan ta wanke fuskarta sau uku, sai hannunta shima sau uku, daganan ɗibo ruwa ta zuba a kanta ta wanke zuwa wuyanta sau uku, saida gashin yasamu ruwa ko ta ina, sannan ta wanke rabin jikinta na dama, ta dawo ta wanke na hagu.

Ruwa ta ɗibo ta watsa a jikinta, ko ina yasamu ruwa, saida ta gama ta ɗau ruwan buta ta wanke kafafuwanta.

Haka ake wankan janaba wallahu A'alamu
