                ~Ruma kada kiyi haka, kibari Allan daya baki cikin ai yafiki sanin kina school ɗin, kuma shine yasan yadda zaiyi dake" Nadiya ce a gaban benchi tana bawa Ruma shawara, Lubcy babu abinda take sai taɓe baki, Ruma data sa hannunta a goshi ta dafe domin surutun Nadiya ya isheta wallahi, tace "Look Nadiya Kinsan yanzu nake tsaka da karatu ko? Kuma fa har yanzu am 25 tayaya Zan iya haɗa raino da karatu? Kinsan hakan bazai yiwu ba ko?"

Lubcy datake taɓe baki taciro Chocolate a jakanta tana ci, tace "Nifa idan nice ke da na jima da cire wannan cikin bansan ma me kike jira dashi ba wallahi kamar ba mace ba"

Kallon Lubcy tayi tace "Kawata saifa yau ya nasamu yasamin hannu ba tareda ya duba takaddan ba, kinsan fa daya karanta bazaisa hannu ba, shiyasa nabari saida yaje aiki nabishi domin nasan acan zai ɗan zama Busy"
Nadiya ganin baza taji shawaranta ba, tace "shikenan je ki cire"

"Ko baki faɗa ba dama ai cirewa zanyi Beb kada ma ki ɓata bakinki"
Da aka tashi suka shiga motan Nadiya ta kaisu Asibiti duka nuna mishi takaddan sign na mijinta, nan akace itama tasa hannu, tasa, suka shiga da ita ɗakin cire ciki, sun kai awa ɗaya a ɗakin kafin aka fito da ita, da kyar take tafiya ta galabaita tafita a hayyacinta, su Lubcy ne suka riketa bayan sun biya kuɗin aiki suka sata a mota, sukayi hanyan gida da ita, tun a hanya Nafiya tace "yanzu me zamuce ya sameta?"
Lubcy tace "Faɗuwa tayi a school bamusan abinda ya sameta ba, sauran idan tadawo hayyacinta zatayi musu bayani ai ita ba yarinya bace"
"Tom ba damuwa"

A kofar get na masarautan suka tsaya suna horn, megadi daya leka yasan motar kawar Gimbiya Ruma ne, da sauri ya buɗe musu yana ɗaga musu hannu.

Saida sukayi Parking suka fito suna riketa, nasu aiki da bayine sukazo wurin suna yiwa Gimbiya sannu, har suka shiga da ita dukda cikin gidan yanada nisa da wurin ajiye motoci, basu gaji ba saida suka kaita har cikin babban falon, yana ɗakin motsa jiki, Saf Yashigo yana cewa Ruma babu lafiya, fitowa yayi da murɗaɗɗen jikinshi wanda ya nuna ba karamin Exercise yake yiba, ganin sun riketa yaje ya ɗagata cakk yana kallonsu Alaman meya sameta?
Kallon juna sukayi kafin Lubcy tace "wallahi muna tafiya a cikin school ta faɗi yanzu ma mun bar motar ta acan a tawa muka taho"

Shiga ɗaki yayi da ita su kuma suka juya simi simi suka fita daga gidan, Ammi dataji labari da wuri tazo ɗakin, har yafara haɗa allura yanaso yayi acikin ruwan dazai ɗaura mata, akan gadon ɗakinta ya kwantar da ita, Ammi ta karaso da sauri tana tambayar meya sameta?

Shiru yayi saida ya haɗa allura ya ɗaura mata ruwa, tana kallonshi har yagama komai, idonta biyu, saida ya sa mata ruwa kafin ta lumshe ido tanajin cikinta yana wani azaban ciwo, bacci yaki ɗaukanta dan Azaba.

Ammi sai sannu takeyi mata, zama yayi a gefen gadon yana karantar yanayinta, hannu yasa a kanta yana shafawa, yana jin zuciyarshi bata kwanta da wannan rashin lafiyar ba.

Riko hannunshi tayi tana kallon yadda ya zuba mata ido kamar wanda ya ajiye abu a fuskarta, so yake ya gano menene abinda yake damunta, saurin kawar da zargin da zuciyarshi yakeyi mishi yayi.

Da kyar bacci ya ɗauketa, Ammi fita tayi, shikuma ya zauna zan kallon Ruma, haka kawai ta faɗi a school? To meya sameta? Kodai ciki ne? Da cikine ba karamin farin ciki zaiyi ba, bari ta danji karfi zai gwada yaga ko cikine da ita domin yana kula da ita a kwanakin nan tana cin abinci sosai.

Yana zaune a wurinta har tayi bacci me isanta ta farka, saida ya ciyar da ita abinci ne kyau ya bata Malt da Madara kafin yace taje tayi wanka, so yake yaje ya duba fada tunda an bashi amana, tana shiga wanka, yafita yaje ya zauna a fada, mutane suna shigowa suna kawo matsalolinsu, rubutawa yake idan mai martaba ya dawo zai karanta yayi musu maganinshi, Jakadiya ce tashigo tana mika mishi gaisuwa.

Murmushi yayi mata yabata takadda, bayan ta karanta tace "zan sanar musu insha Allah yarima"
Tashi tayi ta fita, takira dukkan bayin gidan da ma'aikata duk suka hallara a fada, Takadda ya rubuta yabata tana karantawa da karfi.

"Anason kafin mai martaba ya dawo a gyara komai da komai na cikin gidan, a yanke flowers aje wurin shakatawan me martaba a gyara, sannan aje Lambu shima a gyara komai da komai, motocin gidan duk a wanke,

Dama yarima ya saba haka duk lokacin da mai martaba yayi tafiya to sai yasa anyiwa gidan sabon gyara, hakan yasa koda Abba yayi tafiya hankalinshi baya tashi domin yasan yabar yaro me kwazo a gida.

Saida aka gama jawabi ya bata jakan kuɗi ta rabawa kowa, ai kuwa godiya suka domin dama wasu sunada bukatar kuɗin sosai.

Saida ya daidaita komai ya koma Part ɗinsu, ɗakinta yaje lokacin tayi wanka kuma tacire ruwan daya sa mata, zama yayi a gefen gado yana kallonta, waya yayi mata rubutun taje tayi fitsari tazo, tashi tayi babu tsoro taje tayi ta kawo mishi, gwadawa yayi, tana kallonshi taga yadda ya bata rai, babu ciki kawai rashin lafiya ne, tayi mamakin yadda yake doctor Amma yakasa gane ta zubda shegen cikin daya addabeta a kwanakinnan.
Wayarta ta ɗaga takira Babanta
"Hello Dady? Banda lafiya bazaka kirani kamin ya jiki ba? Kuma su Ajmar basu kirani ba"

Hakuri Baban nata ya bata yace "ya karatu?" 
"Dady karatu ai bana wasa dashi ina kokari sosai"
Hira sukayi sosai kafin ta kashe tana cewa idan an basu hutu zata zo.

Kallonta Junayd yayi, kenan zataje koda bata tambayeshi ba? Tashi yayi yafita a ɗakin, baya samun nutsuwa idan yana tare da Ruma ko kaɗan, zama yayi a ɗaya daga cikin kujerun falon yayi tagumi, wallahi ya zata ciki ne da Ruma, domin tayi kama da me ciki a ƴan kwanakin, ƴammata biyu sanye da Rigan bayi sukazo sunayi mishi firfita, Ruma ce ta fito da waya a hannunta, ganinsu yasa ta haɗa rai ta kashe wayar tazo wurinsu, wani irin tsawa ta daka musu tace "bance ku daina zuwa wurin mijina ba? Ku tashi ku fita kafin nayi muku rashin mutunci"

Jikinsu yana bari sukace "Allah ya huci Ran Gimbiya dama Ammi ce ta turomu muzo mu kula dashi saboda Bakida lafiya"

"Bani da lafiya shine zakuzo ku kanainayemin miji? Ku fitamin banida bukatarku"
Fita sukayi, yana kwance ya lumshe ido yanajin duk abinda sukeyi, tsaki taja tawuce tabar wurin, badan bata da lafiya ba saiya ɓata mata rai akan wannan tsakin datayi, tashi yayi yakoma Lambu ya kwanta akasa jin bayida wani nutsuwa yaje ya faɗa cikin swimming pool ya kwanta yanajin sanyin ruwan yana shiga jikinshi, baison ya ɗago kai yakalli upstair Dan gani yeke kamar zaiga Ruma kuma haushi take bashi ba kaɗan ba, ganin bayajin daɗi ya turawa Asad sako cewar yana zuwa yanzu.
Shirin da baiyi niya ba yayi, cikin kananan kaya ya shiga mota shida kanshi yayi tuki zuwa gidan su Asad.

Mahaifin Asad ya daɗe da rasuwa kuma yanada ɗan rufin asiri yanzu Asad shine yake kula da gidansu da Mamanshi da kannenshi duka, a bakin Get yayi parking ya buɗe yashiga, ganin Mama acikin gida ya durkusa zai gaisheta itama durkusawa tayi tace "Yarima da kanshi?"

Dariya yayi ya gida mata kai, sannu da zuwa tayi mishi sannan ya mike yana kallon side ɗin Asad, hannu ta nuna mishi tace "yana ciki?"
A hankali yafara takawa har ya isa bakin kofar dakin Asad ɗin, budewa yayi Asad na kwance a Falo yana kallon Indian film, Zama yayi a gefenshi yana maida kanshi zuwa Tv, ganin yadda ake Romance a film ɗin ba kaɗan ba yasa ya ɗago kai yana kallonshi, yasan me yake nufi yace "kai kaga nufa Film ɗinne yamin daɗi idan ba haka ba kasan babu abinda zan kalla anan"
Dariya Yarima yayi har fararen hakoranshi suka fito, yana kyau idan yana dariya, waya yaciro yace "Gara ka daina kallon irin Film ɗinnan tunda ba aurene da kai ba"
Yana karantawa yayi tsaki, yaci gaba da kallonshi, Mama ce ta shigo tana rike da babban plate Wanda ta cika da doughnuts da cincin, karɓa mata Junayd yayi ya ajiye a gabashi, ya zauna akasa yasan washi aka kawo shiyasa yafara ci, kunun aya me sanyi ta ajiye mishi, ya cika Cup dashi yafara sha, yamishi daɗi shiyasa yakeson Maman Abokinshi tana kula dashi idan yazo gidan, dama yanason kunun aya da kuma Zoɓo komai dai idan anyi local yafi mishi daɗi.
Asad ne yasa hannu zai ɗauki Cup ɗin shima yasha, da sauri ya rike hannunshi yana mishi kallon bafa wa kai aka kawo ba.

"Kai dalla malam Kaɗan zan sha"
Saida ya shanye na Cup ɗin, Junayd ya kara mishi, kallon Junayd yayi yace "gaskiya Junayd banida burin daya wuce naga kafara magana, duk da Allah ne ya ɗaura maka amma tunda akwai magani ai ya dace mu tashi mu nema wata kila Allah ya datar damu, duk da nasan ba karamin kokari mai martaba yayi ba dan ganin kasamu sauki amma hakan bazaisa mu zauna ba"
Kallonshi Junayd yayi, hakika abokin shi yana sonshi to amma ai anyi maganin yaki yiwuwa, yanzu yabar komai a hannun Allah.

Saida ya wuni a gidansu Asad kafin da yamma yafito zai tafi, mama ta fita shiyasa ya ɗau kudi yacewa Asad ya ajiye mata, yaki karɓa saida ya ajiye mishi yafiya, cikin kwanciyar hankali yake tuki yana tunanin makomar rayuwarshi.
Har ya isa gida, Umman Muneer ce ta kirashi ta bashi kayan Fruit, karɓa yayi yana murmushi, yana zuwa lambu ya zubar ya ɗibi wani yafara ci.


         "Ke waye ya taɓamin shanu na?"
Jikinta ne yafara rawa, bakinta dayake ɗan karami shima yafara ɓari, hannu tasa ta riko gefen Riganta tana murzawa tayi zuru zuru da ido tana kallonshi, ganin yadda ta tsorata ya kuma daka mata tsawa "bazaki faɗa min ba?"
Aneesa tana mugun tsoron wannan yaron mugun mashayi ne ga iya duka kamar yasamu jaki, a hankali ta buɗe bakinta dayake rawa tace "bani bace" 

"To waye? Ki faɗamin ko ɗan gidan uban wayene saina cimishi mutunci"
"Wallahi ban sansu ba"
Ganin bazata faɗa ba kuma ga shanunshi yana magagin mutuwa, Aneesa ce ta wurgi shanun da dutse dan yasa ta faɗi ta zubar da nono, bata sani ba ashe yaji rauni a wuya, mutane ne suka taru aka yanka shanun, tana zaune a gefe tana cijan leɓe tana karanto Addu'a a ranta, Tambayan yaran gefe yayi waya wurga mishi shanu? Sukace basu sani ba, Allah ya taimaketa sun rufa mata asiri da yau me karɓanta a wurinshi sai Allah.

Da kyar ta koma gida gabanta bai daina faduwa ba, tararda Mairama tayi tace musu gobe karɓan kayanta, Aneesa datake a tsorace tace "Zamuzo Adda Mairama insha Allah"
Mama ce ta kalleta tace "lafiya Aneesa?"
"Eh mama faduwa nayi"

"Sannu jeki ki wanke jikinki" har kitsonta yaɓaci da nono kwancewa tayi ta wanke tulin gashin nata, saida ya bushe mama ta kame mata guda biyu, ado tasa akan Kitson nan tafito asalin bafulata.

                ~Yayi shiri tsab aciki wani Shadda Milk color, rigan daidai gwiwa sai, ba karamin kyau yayi ba, riganshi na Doctor ya rike a hannunshi Yana takowa cikin tafiyarshi me cike da ƙasaita, kamar ko yaushe Lips nashi na cikin bakinshi yana tsotsa, fuskarshi tayi kyau sosai domin Sajen ya gyara mishi fuska kuma yakara fitowa da asalin kyawunshi, idan Ka ganshi zakace Balarabe ne, ko kuma ya haɗa jini da larabawa, a bakin Get ya tsaya yana kallon yadda Megadi suke musu da wani bawan Allah, hannu ya ɗaga yayiwa megadi Alaman ya barshi ya shigo, Guard ne sukayi checking nashi, su duba har Aljihunshi kafin suka barshi ya karasa ciki.

Yana zuwa ya durkusa a gaban Yarima yana gaisuwa, ɗagoshi Junayd yayi yana yimishi Alama da me ya faru?"

"Yallaɓai Matata ce babu lafiya haihuwa zatayi munje asibiti sunki kulamu saboda banida kuɗi, na buga tanan na buga ta can ban samu ba, shiyasa nace bari nazo wajenka kamar yadda kake taimakawa mutane nima ka taimaka min"

Tunda yafara maganan ya zuba mishi ido, hannunshi cikin aljihun wandonshi yana kallon yadda mutumin yake a firgice, ciro kuɗi yayi ƴan dubu ɗaya ɗaya bandir biyu yamika mishi, bai jira yayi mishi Godiya ba ya juya ya tafi.

Mota aka buɗe mishi, ya shiga yana kallon wayarshi, so yake ya isa Asibiti da wuri domin wanda suka yiwa Theater jiya bai farfaɗo ba"
Driver ne ya jashi, Yana Kallon wayarshi har suka isa cikin Asibitin, buɗe mishi marfin mota akayi a hankali yasa kafafuwanshi zuwa waje, ya ɗau rigan Dr yasa, kara kyau yayi domin rigan yana karɓanshi sosai, tafiya yafara kamar mai tausayin kasa.

Bai tsaya ko ina ba sai cikin ɗakin dayasan mutumin yana ciki, abin mamaki har yau ko ƴan uwanshi basu zo ba, yana shiga sauran likitocin suka shigo, fara dubashi yayi, yaciro Allura yayi mishi, da yaddan Allah sai gashi ya farfaɗo, ruwa ya ɗaura mishi wanda zai bashi karfi, sauke ajiyan zuciya ya sauke domin ya ceto rayuwar mutum godiya yayiwa Allah da ya bashi wannan baiwan.

Office ɗinshi yaje yana mamakin yau Asad bai zo ba, Asad da baya wasa da aiki yasan akwai damuwa, rigan saman yacire ya rataya ajikin kofa sannan ya jawo kujeran da aka tanada domin shi ya zauna yana ciro waya daga Aljihun wandonshi, Text ya turawa Asad yana tambayar meya faru yau baizo Ba.

Mayar mishi yayi da yana hanya Mom nashi ne bata ɗan jin daɗi, bayan ya karanta ya buɗe Datanshi yafara Duba sakonnin Watsapp, ganin sakon sunada yawa ya ajiye wayar ya ɗau Laptop Yana jiran sakon su gama shigowa, saida suka gama shigowa kafin ya ɗaga wayar yana dubawa, Reply yayi wa duk wanda ya dace yayi, yawanci abokanshi ne ƴan school nasu, sauran ƴan malysia saura Kuma ƴan nan gida Nigeria, kashe datan yayi dan baya jimawa a online, hankali ya maida kan Laptop ɗinshi yana cigaba da aiki, knocking akayi sannan yaga an turo kofar an shigo, Ruma ce tayi shiri cikin Abaya pitch color, tasa glass Baki kamar yadda ta saba, takalmi da jaka baƙi ne, takalmin dogo ne sosai, tana taunar Cingum abinda ya tsana kenan, rufe kofar tayi tana mishi murmushi, yasan akwai abinda ya kawota haka kawai bata zuwa Asibitinshi, karasowa tayi ta ɗauke Laptop ɗin daga gabanshi ta tura gefe, zama tayi a cinyarshi ta saƙala hannayenta a wuyanshi tana kallonshi tana murmushi, shima murmushi yayi mata, yana ɗaga gira Alaman meya faru?.
Hannu tasa acikin jaka taciro wani takadda ta mika mishi.

Jikinta har yanzu da shatin bulala, goshinta kuma a kumbure kaɗan an rufe ciwon da bandage, Koda zata fito gida bata bari kowa ya ganta ba.

"Junayd a school ne akace nakawo maka kasamin hannu a wannan takaddan"
Bai wani tsayawa ya karanta ba yayi sign ɗin ya bata.

Shafa fuskarshi tayi tace "Thanks You Junayd"
Asad ne ya turo kofan ya shigo, ganin su ahaka yace "Ohh sorry" juyawa yayi zai fita, ta sauka tana cewa "Tsaya Asad yanzu ai zan tafi"

Gaisawa sukayi tayiwa yarima Bye Bye ta fita, Asad ya zauna akan Kujera yana kallon Junayd da ya maida hankali kan Laptop, janye Laptop ɗin yayi yace "ji rainin wayo, yanzu nazo naga kana zaune da matarka sai kuma ka buge da aiki?"

Tsaki yaja a ranshi, shifa Asad yafara isanshi da surutu wallahi, waya yaciro yace "ai matata ce kama kayi auren mana"

Taɓe baki yayi "dole ma nayi auren ko dan nima a zaunamin a cinya"
Harara Junayd yayi mishi.

A school ya maida hankalinshi kan karatu, ya fita a harkan Gimbiya datake damunshi da zancen aure, Safwan mutum ne me kamun kai, kuɗi da mulki baisa yazama lalatacce ba, zaune yake akan bench Yana karanta wani  handout taɓashi akayi a firgice ya ɗago kai yana kallon baya, Wani freind nashi ne, numfashi ya sauke yace "kai Ahmar zaka tsoratani ai"

"Kai dalla sai kace wani wanda yake karanta abinda ba daidai ba? Handout fa kake karantawa amma ka firgita kamar me kallo Bf"
Tsaki yaja yaci gaba da karatunshi, zama Ahmar yayi a gefenshi yaciro waya, wasu hotuna ya buɗe ya nunawa Safwan ɗin, kallo Saf yayi ganin ƴammata ne sunsa ɗamammun kaya rabin jikinsu duk waje da alama ma ba ƴan nan Nigeria bane dan fatarsu ba irin namu bane.
Da sauri ya ɗauke kai yace "miye wannan ɗin?"

"Kai Saf yaushe zaka waye ne? Kana ganin hot Girls kana cewa miye wannan? Kaga wannan ta tsakiyar" kallonta Safwan yayi yaga duk cikinsu kamar ma tafisu fitsara kuma tafisu kyau.

"To jiya da ita na kwana kai kasan yadda Babyn ta haɗu kuwa? Har gari ya waye ban sani ba"

Shiru Safwan yayi, yana sha'awan hakan amma yana tsoron Yayanshi da mai martaba, idan suka gane yana wannan harkan zasu iya yimishi hukunci mai tsanani, da fari bayaso amma Ahmar yana kwaɗaita mishi, kara matsowa Ahmar yayi ya ɗauko hoton wata yarinya itama ta haɗu bana wasa ba ya nuna mishi, cinyoyinta duk a waje gashi jikinta yana shining.

"Wannan tana nan Nigeria a Abuja take zan haɗaka da ita tanada sauƙin kai, kufara Chatting ku saba kafin ka shiga layi, dan naga har yanzu tsoron mata kake"
A ɗan tsorace ya karɓi Number ɗinta ya buɗe Data yayi mata hi, hoton Dp ɗinta yafi wancan iya shege, kashe datan yayi, Ahmar yace "tana da Number ɗinka ai nayi mata bayani tunda wuri, tana ganin hotonka tace itafa dole na haɗaku"
Murmushi yayi mishi.

"Dole ka shigo hanya Saf kasan babu yadda za'ayi inajin daɗi kai kuma kana nan kana wahalar da kanka a karatu, kasan iyayenmu sunada kuɗi karatun nan suna ne kawai, ko yau mukaso aiki ai zamu samu"
Shima Ahmar Babanshi yanada kuɗi domin a yanzu shine mataimakin governo na garin Gombe, ajiye handout ɗin yayi suka fara hira.

Sai kusan bayan Azahar kafin Nurse ta shigo tace "Sir Mutumin ya tashi daga bacci fa" 
Mikewa yayi suka fita tare, ɗakin da yake kwance sukaje, Junayd ganin ya tashi yanacin Ayaba yasa yayi ajiyan zuciya, ƙarasawa yayi yana taɓa jikinshi, da ɗan zafi kuma hakan normal ne, a hankali mutumin ya gaisheshi, zai kai shekara 50 saide jikinshi ya nuna akwai kuɗi, hannu Junayd ya ɗaga mishi, da mamaki yakuma cewa "Nagode da taimakon da kuka yimin"
Girgiza kai Junayd yayi.

"Baka magana ne?"
Giɗa kai yayi yana miƙa mishi wani magani, "Allah sarki"
Karɓa yayi yasha yana kallon Junayd ɗin, gashi namiji har namiji amma baya magana, ikon Allah kenan akace idan baka mutu ba, ba'a gama yimaka halitta ba.

Saida ya Kuma checking ɗinshi me kyau kafin ya tabbatar babu wani matsala, ajiye maganin yayi ya rubuta mishi yadda zai sha, da kuma Time ɗin da zai sha.
Godiya mutumin yayi.
Fita Junayd yayi yana kallon Agogo 3 ya kusa, bari kawai yajira yayi sallan La'asar saiya tafi, duba marasa lafiya yafara, yanabin kowani ɗaki, na magani ya bashi na allura kuma yayi musu.

Yana yiwa mutane Allura amma shi ya tsani ace za'ayi mishi, bayason magani sam sam balle kuma Allura.

Bayan yagama duba wanda sukafi bukatar a dubasu, ya zauna acikin asibitin akan kujeran da aka tanadar mishi domin zama a cikin asibiti, kallon duk wani abinda yake gudana yake, ganin flowers sunyi tsayi babu gyara ya turawa Me duba flower da basu ruwa saƙo cewar a gyara flowers yanzu yanzu.

Ba ɓata lokaci yaga ma'aikata masu gyaran flower sun tashi sun fara gyara saura suna sharewa wasu kuma suna bayinshi.

Saida suka share tas harda cikin asibitin wanda yake a share, yaga yakara Zama need, Kamar ka kwanta a asibitin kayi bacci tsaban kyau da kuma haske.

Ana kiran sallan La'asar aka kawo mishi buta yayi alwala yashiga masallacin dayake manne a jikin Asibitin, ya gina ne domin kawo wa masu jinya sauƙin yin salla basai sunyi nisa ba.

Salla yayi ya zauna yayita addu'a kafin ya koma cikin Asibiti ya shiga mota suka shiga hanyar gida.
Suna isa gida ya shiga wurin mai martaba, shirye shiryen tafiya sukeyi saida aka shirya mishi komai kafin ya kalli Junayd yace "ka dawo?" Giɗa kai yayi, yace "to Yanzu zamu tafi Sarkin Adamawa, mahaifin Ruma kenan, yana jiranmu a airport munada kiran gaggawa daga shugaban kasa kuma zamuyi kwana biyu ko fiye da haka, yanzu mulki ya dawo hannunka kaine zaka kula da komai kafin na dawo, Kannenka amana ne a wurinka a kula dasu da iyayenka kaji?"
Giɗa kai yayi shifa baison wannan abin kawai zai karɓa ne saboda baison fishin Sarki, wani sanda yabashi wanda akayi mishi Adon jaa da fari, sandar sarauta ne, karɓa yayi ya ajiye a gefe yana kallon Babanshi yana shirin tafiya"

Langwaɓe kai yayi yana kallon Abba "kaga yanzu fa ka girma banson shiririta, Kanada mata amma har yanzu bazaka daina shagwaɓa ba?" Shiru yayi yana kallon Abba, saida ya shirya cikin kayan sarauta yakira waziri, shigowa yayi yabashi jaka, sannan yakira Ammi da Umman Muneer, sallama yayi musu sukayi mishi addu'a, can cikin gida kuma an shirya motocin da zasu raka mai martaba, mota ishirin da uku ne duka da nashi, dana dogarai, buɗe mishi marfin mota akayi, Safwan ne yazo ya rungumeshi zana cewa "Allah ya kiyaye hanya"

"Ameen ka kula da yayanka sannan ka kula da Muneer kaji?"
Giɗa kai yayi.

Ammi sai murmushi take Umman Muneer kuma ganin Babu Muneer a wurin ba karamin bakin ciki tayi ba, kawai yake take don kada Abba ya gane.

Suna ɗaga mishi hannu har suka tafi, kallonta Ammi tayi tace "ina Muneer ne? Ban ga yazo sunyi sallama da Abban nasu ba"

"Eh aikanshi nayi shiyasa baizo ba"
Tana gama maganar tashiga ciki, ɗakinta ta wuce ta ɗau waya ta lalubo number ɗin Muneer, bugu kusan huɗu kafin ya ɗaga.

"Dan ubanka ina kaje? Ko ban sanar maka yau sarki zaiyi tafiya ba? Muneer so kake ka kasheni da bakin ciki? Muneer idan na mutu kaine ka kasheni"

"Haba Umma ba ga Ya Junayd a wurin ba? Dole saina zo ne?"

Shiru tayi jin yanayin muryanshi da sauri tace "ina kake? Nakejin muryanka haka?"

"Umma ba dole kiji muryata haka ba, nida budurwata ne fa"

Bawa yarinyar waya yayi, ta kashe murya tana gaida Umma, wawuro ashar tayi ta aikawa yarinyar, ranta in yayi dubu to ya ɓaci, itada takeson ya maida hankali ya koyi mulki, tunda wannan Kurman bazaiyu yayi mulki ba, amma yaje yana bin mata da shaye shaye? Kashe wayar tayi ta nemo wani Number.

"Kizo gobe da safe zaki rakani wani wuri, yaron nan ba shiryuwa zaiyi ba"

"Tom zanzo"
Safwan dayake tsaye a bakin kofa, yazo duba Muneer sai kuma yaji wayan da Umman takeyi, a hankali ya juya ya koma baya.

A Falo ya kwanta ya ciro waya ya kunna Data, yarinyar tayi mishi reply, sunanta Sophy, Chatting duka fara sosai.

Kusan mangrib tace bayan sallan Isha zasu cigaba da Chatting, Saida yayi salla a falon, yaci abinci lokacin Junayd ma Yashigo, kwanciya yayi akan carpet Yana cigaba da Chatting ɗinshi, wasu shegun hotunanta ta tura mishi, wanda daga ita sai bra da gajeren wando, ido ya zubawa hoton yana jin jikinshi yana sauyawa, a hankali idanunshi suka fara canja kala, message ta tura mishi "I need zou badly" shiru yayi ya zubawa wayan ido, kamar yasani shima ya daina kallon Laptop ɗinshi ya maida hankali kan Safwan ɗin, ganin mood nashi ya canja yasa yaji mamaki sosai, bai saba ganinshi a wannan halin ba.

Saf? Ɗago kai yayi a ɗan tsorace yana kallon Yayanshi, ganin yanayin idonshi yace "meya sameka?"

"Babu komai Yaya karatu nake"

Shi ba yaro bane yanzu haka zaikai shekara 29 so babu abinda Saf din zai iya ɓoye mishi, yasan wannan yanayin, yasan sai kana tare da mace ko wani abu makamancin haka, saide sanin halin Safwan ɗin yasashi mayar da hankalinshi kan aikinshi, yasan kaninshi a nitse yake.

Saf da sauri ya goge chat ɗin hadda hotonta yasa wayar a key ya ajiye a gefe, kwanciya yayi rub da ciki akasa yana tunanin yanayin suran jikinta, Allah yayi mata sura mai kyau.

 *Chapter 12*


                  ~Mai Martaba kullum saiya turawa Junayd message domin yaji ya suke acan, Junayd yanajin daɗin hakan, idan suna Chatting da Babanshi yana samun nutsuwa, Safwan ma kullum sai sunyi Chatting, Ruma ce dai sai idan taga dama tayi mishi hi, idan yaga dama ya amsa idan baiso ba ya kyaleta.

Shima yau zaman kaɗaici ya isheshi, fita yayi a dakin yaga Mama tana surfa Dawa, durkusawa kasa yayi yana ɗaga mata hannu, Tausayi yabata sosai, ga mutum har mutum ga kyau ga hutu ga amma babu magana Ikon Allah kenan "ka fito ne Junayd?"

Girgiza kai yayi yana kallon ƙasa, "to Masha Allah zaka tayani hira kenan yau" dariya yayi, ta ɗau kujera ta ajiye mishi a tsakar gida, zama yayi akai, dama da Hijabinta a jikinta, taci gaba da Surfe tana cewa "ku kam acan bakwa wani Surfe mu kuma nan yazama mana dole babu inji dole kai Zakayi abinka da kanka"

Murmushi kawai yake mata, tace "ina rokon Allah yabaka lafiya kaima kafara magana kamar yadda abokinka yake hira, saide kai naga kamar baka fiye son surutu ba"

Shiru yayi, "kamar Aneesa haka take bata fiye surutu ba, amma idan ta saba da mutum tana yawan yimishi hira"

"Aneesa" ya maimaita sunan a ranshi, yasan wannan mara kunyar ne, ai kuwa kafin ya gama tunanin tashigo tana sallama, wajen mama taje ta tsaya tana ɓoye hannunta a baya "Me kika dawo yi?"

Dariya tayi wanda yasa gefen kumatunta lotsawa, kyakkyawar fuskarta ta juya zuwa baya tana zare abu a leda, mikawa mama tayi tana dariya, karɓa mama tayi tace "Goro? Shiyasa kika dawo yanzu?"

"Eh mama kinsan Anjima zanzo in zubar shiyasa na kawo miki"
Tayi maganan da zazzaƙan muryanta siriri kamar na mama ɗin.

Buta ta ɗauka ta wanke kafarta dayayi kura, Mama tace "ina Asad ɗin?"
"Yanacan shida Adda Surayya tana nuna mishi gari"
Saida ta gama ta kalleshi bayan ta ajiye butan taɗan russuna tace "ina wuni?" Tasan bazai amsa ba itama ta gaisheshi ne saboda maka na tsakar gidan, ta lura yanada ɗankaren girman kai, wucewa tayi ɗaki ta shafa mai tafito "Mama Hamma Faruk yace zaije wurin" 
"To Allah ya kaishi lafiya"

"Ameen Mama"
Kallonshi tayi taga ba ita yake kallo ba,  kamar tayi mareshi takeji mutum kamar gunki baya magana haka?
Fita tayi tana waka a bakinta, bin bayanta yayi da kallo, ganin yadda ta kumbutsa gashi wuri biyu yasa yaji a ranshi Attachment take sawa, dama idonta a buɗe yake zata iya, idan ba haka ba ga Yayarta bata da wannan gashin, amma ita ace wannan duka gashinta? 
Ko juyawa bata kara yiba taci gaba da tafiyarta bata tsaya ko ina ba sai gidansu Mairam, lokacin an kawo manyan speaker zasu fara gudanar da wasa.

Asad na gefe da Surayya suna ta hira harda dariya, tanada daɗin Zama haka ya fahimta kuma tanada hakuri, son yarinyar yake sosai, tanada shiga rai.

An fara gudanar da wasa da karfe 5 na yamma, kawayen Amarya ne zasu shiga fili a kunna musu waka suyita rawan Fulani, sannan abokan ango su shigo suma.

Ganin Surayya batada miyan tashi yace "bazakiyi rawan bane ke?"
Dariya tayi sosai kafin tace "ina ma iya rawa?"
Kallonta yayi yadda take dariya yana tafiya da imaninshi, baison ya daina hira da ita domin yanajin shauki tare da ita.

Hamma Faruk yazo shima sunyi ta hira da Aneesa, sai kusan 6 na dare aka tashi daga wasan, Surayya ta nemi Aneesa bata ganta ba, hakan yasa suka tafi ita da Asad, suna tafiya suna hira a kofar gida sukaga Baba yana alwala, kallonsu yayi suka gaisheshi ya amsa yana kallonsu har suka shiga gida.

Junayd da Baba tare sukaje masallaci, saida aka idar da isha kafin Aneesa ta shigo itada Hamma Faruk, gaishesu yayi, ya gaisa da Asad kafin yace "Aneesan Baba nikam na tafi"
"To Hamma Faruk a gaida gida"
Fita yayi mama tace "bazaki rakashi bane?"

Binshi tayi a baya saida ta rakashi kaɗan kafin ta dawo, Mama tana kallonsu a ranta tace Allah ya haɗa kanku.

Baba yace akira mishi Surayya, yana ɗakinshi taje ta durkusa, Mama na gefenshi yace "Surayya? Inaso kibani hankalinki kiji maganan da zan miki"

"Tom Baba"

"Surayya kinsan wannan bako ne ko? Kuma bamusan inda suka fito ba, kuma kinsan wannan yayi miki nisa saboda masu kuɗi ne"

Shiru tayi tasan gaskiya Baba yake faɗa, "to inaso ki fita a harkanshi saboda su ƴan birni ba abun yadda bane"

"Tom Baba Zan fita insha Allah"
"Allah yayi miki Albarka"

"Ameen Baba"

Tashi tayi tafita, a bakin gadonsu ta zauna tayi tagumi, dole ta fita a harkanshi domin fa Baba yayi gaskiya, bata sanshi ba batasan daga ina yafito ba, gashi suna neman su shaƙu da juna?"

Aneesa ta lura akwai damuwa a tare da Surayyan saide batason yawan shishigi.

Yau saura kwana uku su bar garin, Junayd ji yake kamar kwana ukun bazaizo ba, ya gaji da garin yayi missing ɗin family nashi, so yake yaga Ammi da Safwan, Ibti yana yawan tambayarta babu damuwa? Tana cewa babu, to yanzu so yake yaga ya koma gida, gashi yana bukatan Ruma sosai yasan ba dole ta bashi haɗin kai yadda yaso ba amma ai zai ɗan rage zafi, zaune yake akan katifa Yana kallon Waya, yana tsotsan lips nashi na kasa, sai lumshe ido yake yau yana cikin yanayin son kasancewa da matarshi.

Asad yana naɗe kayansu da Surayya ta wanke, kallon Junayd yayi yace "yadai? Ya kaketa lumshe ido haka? Bacci kakeji?"

Baiyi magana ba sai kallon Asad yake, "kaga nifa banson namiji yanamin irin wannan kallon kabari Surayya tamin ba kai ba"

Kwanciya yayi akan katifan yanajin haushin maganan Asad ɗin.

Kwana biyu Surayya bata shigowa ɗakin saide Aneesa takai musu abinci, wasan ɓuya tafara yi da Asad, bataso ya ganta balle ya jata da hira, gashi yadamu ya haɗu da ita kuma gobe zasu koma Garinsu, Aneesa ce ta shigo da kwaryan nono a hannunta itace ta dama musu, tana ajiyewa Asad yace "Anee? Ina Surayya?"

Shiru tayi dan ta fahimci abinda yake faruwa, Baba ya hanata kulashi gashi itakam bata iya karya ba, ganin tayi shiru yace "ina taje?"

"Baba ne yace ta daina biye maka domin akwai banbanci tsakanin ku, mu yaran talaka ne ku kuma yaran masu kuɗi, garinmu ba ɗaya ba al'adarmu ba ɗaya ba, kayi Hakuri Adda Surayya bazata kara biye maka ba, domin munajin maganar Baba"
Fita tayi tanajin ba daɗi a ranta, tunda ta fara maganar ya zuba mata ido har tagama ta fita.

Shiru yayi jikinshi yayi sanyi, jingina yayi da jikin bangon ɗakin yayi shiru, Junayd ya fahimci halin da yake ciki, waya ya ɗaga yace "idan kana sonta da gaske kasamu Baban nata kayi mishi magana"

Jinjina kai yayi bashida tabbacin idan sun tafi gobe zasu kara dawowa garin nan, tunaninshi ya rabu biyu ya rasa yadda zaiyi, Junayd baison abokin nashi yashiga damuwa a hankali yakara yimishi rubutu _be a man kaje kayiwa Dad nata magana_

"Tom shikenan zanje nayi mishi magana insha Allah"

Da yamma Mama taje makota, ita kuma Surayya ta zauna a waje ta buga tagumi, Aneesa ce ta ɗau maganin da Baba ya bata ta daka a turmi, ta tanakaɗe tasa a ruwa, zama tayi tarinka karatu a ciki tana tofawa kamar yadda Baba yace tayi.

Asad ne ya fito tana so ta tsayar dashi ya tsaya idan ta gama ya kaiwa Abokinshi amma bazaiyu ta dakata da karatun ba, yana ganinta ya wuce yafita, gefen Surayya ya zauna akan dutse yace "Gobe zamu tafi"

Tashi tayi tana murmushi tace "Allah ya tsare muku hanya"
So take tashiga gida kafin Baba ya dawo ya ganta, "Surayya ki zauna inason magana dake"
A hankali ta koma ta zauna, tana wasa da kara karami a hannunta.

"Surayya ina sonki kuma Aurenki nakeso nayi"

"Asad nida kai akwai banbanci nifa Ƴar kauye ce daga daji nake, kuma nataɓa aure kai kuma saurayine hakan bazai yiwu ba, idan kai ka amince ba lallene ƴan uwanka su Amince ba"

"Manzon Allah SAW ya auri Nana Khadijah lokacin dayake saurayi itakuma ta taɓa aure shin hakan ya haramta ne a addini?"

Shiru tayi batace komai ba, tunda yace Manzon Allah ya gama komai.
"Surayya inason nayi magana da Baba amma saikin amince min, shin kin yadda zaki Aureni?"

Shiru tayi, yace "kin Amince?"
"Kayiwa Baba magana idan ya amince nima na amince saɓanin haka kuma nima zanbi duk abinda yace".

Aneesa saida tagama tofa karatun kafin ta mike tashiga ɗakin dayake, bakinta ɗauke da sallama, saida Surayya tace mata baya iya maida magana kafin ta fahimci dalilin rashin maganar tashi.

Yana kwance akan Katifa ya rufe ido kamar me bacci, ajiyewa tayi ta rike kwankwaso tana kallonshi, "ya Allah yanzu ya zanyi? Gashi Baba yace kada nabari maganin ya ɗau lokaci batareda yasha ba, gashi yayi kane kane akan katifan Hamma Umar yana bacci"
Yi tayi kamar zata tasheshi sai kuma ta koma baya.

"Ta ina zan tasheshi? Mama tace kada na taɓa maza saide Hamma Umar" 
Yana jin duk abinda take faɗa shiru yayi mata, saida ta gaji da tsayuwa ta buga jikin bangon tana cewa "Bawan Allah katashi ga maganinka"

Yana jinta yayi kamar yana bacci, saida tace Bismillahi kafin ta buga kafarshi tana kiran sunanshi "bawan Allah? Ka tashi mana Baba yace kada maganin yaɗau lokaci"
Tayi magana a shagwaɓe, a hankali ya buɗe ido yana kallonta, dabarcewa tayi, hannunta tafara murzawa tana kallonshi da Manyan idanunta, bakinta yana ɗan rawa tace "ga maganinka"

A hankali ya mike yana kallon Kwaryan, zama tayi a gefenshi ta mika mishi, bai kalleta ba ya karɓa, sawa yayi a bakinshi yayi sipping kaɗan, runtse ido yayi dan yaji wani ɗaci ya ziyarci bakinshi.

Ajiye Kwaryan yayi yana rufe ido, Matsowa tayi ganin bazaisha ba, taɗau Kwaryan ta matso bakinshi, haɗe fuska tayi tace "Haa"
A ranshi yace "ji wani raini?"

Bai karasa magana ba ta kai bakinshi, a hankali ya buɗe baki tasa mishi, bata cire ba saida ya shanye, yana kauda kai yanajin kamar zaiyi amai, saida ya shanye tass kafin ta cire kwaryan, yana namiji amma sai Ragonta, Allah yasa gobe da safe su tafi ma ko zata huta.

Yana kallonta mike da kwaryan a hannu zata fita, baki ya buɗe yanajin kamar wuyanshi yana kaikayi, hannu yasa a wuya yanajin wani abu ya tokareshi, bakinshi yayi nauyi jikinshi yafara ɓari.
Sanyi yafara ji atake jikinshi yafara rawa, a take Jajayen Lips nashi suka kara komawa jaa, a hankali ya buɗe baki yace "Anee?? Aneeeeesa"
Muryanshi baya fita sosai amma taji yayi magana.

Da wani irin Murmushi ta juyo tana kallonshi, Kwaryan ta rungume a cikinta tace "kamar ka kirani?"
Giɗa kai yayi yana rawan jiki hannunshi a wuyanshi, tace "kara kiran sunan dai"

Lips nashi yana rawa yace "Aneeee"
Da sauri ta karaso tana dariya tace "karasa"
"Aneesa" yafaɗa da karfi yana jin kamar zai mutu, bargon dayake gefenshi ya janyo ya lulluɓa jikinshi dashi, sanyi yakeji sosai, Aneesa ta rufe kafarshi dayake a waje, ganin ya lumshe ido tafara jin daɗi.

Da gudu ta fita wurin su Asad tace "ya Asad ya fara magana"
Asad baisan lokacin daya tashi yashiga gidan ba, cikin wani irin murna yashiga ɗakin nasu, ganin Junayd a kwance yace "Junayd" 
Hannu ya mika mishi yana daga kwance, "Junayd kayi magana, kayi magana inji muryanka Junayd"
Aneesa da Surayya suna tsaye a wurin, Junayd yace "Asad Zan mutu jikina ciwo"
Hawayene yafara bin fuskar Asad, hawayen farin ciki da tausayin Abokinshi.

Surayya ma taji daɗi sosai, kallon Aneesa datake ta murna tayi, bata taɓa ganin Aneesa tayi farin ciki da samun lafiyan mutum a gidansu ba kamar wannan.

Aneesa kuwa murnan Yasamu sauki zasubar musu gida take, batason ganinshi dan yafiye iyayi, yanzu koba komai zasu tafi kuma bazasu kara dawo musu gida ba, dama sun takurata ba kaɗan ba.

                ~Aneesa Saida tayi kwana biyu bata fita, har karɓan kayan mairam bataje ba, tana gida a zaune kamar mara lafiya, Mama taso ta fahimta amma ta share kawai tana ganin kamar batajin daɗi ne.

Mama nada hawan jini shiyasa bata fiye damuwa dasa kanta a lamarin Aneesa ba, batason hayaniya kuma batason damuwa, ita Addu'a take Allah ya bawa Aneesa miji tayi aure ko zata koyi hakuri idan an taɓota.

Yau taga dama itace tayi girki a gidan, dambu ta dafa sannan tayi shara ta kimtsa gidan yadawo fes fes, wanke wanke tayi ta jera kwanukan a ɗakin mama, ta kai abincin ɗakinsu da Adda Surayya ta kimtsa ɗakin shina ta shirya, ɗakin Baba ma taje ta gyara, ta shimfida mishi zanin gado akan katifarshi dayake shimfiɗe acikin ɗakin, dukda dakin taɓo ne amma yana nan tsab tsab babu kazanta, gefe kuma magunguna ne na gargajiya suma an ajiyesu cikin tsari, sai kwarya manya manya da kanana a jere a gefe, shimfiɗa tabarma tayi ta kakkaɗe ko ina ta share.

Saida ta gama aikin mama tana zaune tana kallonta tana Addu'a Allah yasa Ta ɗore a haka, da kullum haka takeyi ai da taji daɗi, Nono ta diba a kwarya ta ɗau maburgi tafara kaɗawa, saida ya kaɗu ta ɗauko Fura ta guggutsura aciki, tasa sugar ta rufe Kwaryan da faifai takai bakin randa inda zai sashi yayi sanyi sosai.

Ta ajiyewa Baba ne dan tasan yana son hakan, Alwala tayi taje ta idar da sallan mangrib ta dawo tsakar gida ta zauna, Mama ganin tayi shiru tace "lafiya dai ko?"

"Eh lafiya lau Mama"
Saida Baba Yashigo kafin Surayya ta shigo itama, sannu da zuwa tayi mishi ta ɗibo ruwa a kofi ta kawo mishi "yawwa Aneesan Baba" karɓa yayi yasha, suka gaisa da Mama, Surayya ma wanka tayi, ta idar da salla ta dawo cikin gida, Aneesa tasa musu dambun suka fara ci, Baba ta bashi Furan data dama mishi, sai sa mata Albarka yake, Mama ma taci dambun yayi mata daɗi, hira suka farayi, sun idar da isha suka kara fara wani hiran basu yi tashi a wurin ba sai kusan karfe 10 na dare, dama suna hakan a lokacin zafi, su zauna suyita hira har dare ya tsaga kafin su koma ɗaki.

"Adda yau kin jima a waje me kikeyi haka?"

"Nayi sabon saurayine kuma aure zamuyi"
"Waye haka?"

"Ɗan Rugan su Iliya ne fa wannan mai saida rake a Bakin hanya ɗin"

"Adda badai wannan guntun me idanu a waje ɗin ba"

"Aneesa banason iyayi da iskanci fa, ya zaki rinƙa zagarmin samarai?"

"Allah yabaki hakuri" tasan yaron wani guntu da katon kai ga rashin dariya, ita kam sam baiyi mata ba, ta rasa meyasa Adda Surayya bata iya zaɓen saurayi ba, daga dogon da babu fasali sai guntu mai katon kai, haka lokacin data zaɓo giɗado kamar ta gudu idan ta ganshi, gata kamar ka sace ka gudu tsaban kyau amma sam munana take zaɓa tarasa dalili.

Itakam shiyasa take son Hamma Faruk saboda yana da kyau gashi da tsari ga iya magana da dariya da son mutane, amma Adda kam Allah baya bata miji me kyau, ita kuma haka nata ƙaddaran yazo.

Shimfiɗa musu makwancinsu tayi, Surayya tayi fishi taki yimata magana, kallonta tayi tace "kiyi hakuri nifa ba wai zaginshi nayi ba daga kwatance?"

"To sa'arki ce Ni dazaki rinƙa kwatancen saurayina? Ko dan kinga inayi miki dariya muna zama kamar kawaye ne?"

"A,a kiyi hakuri" dama Surayya akwai son mutum, idan tafara son saurayi bataso a zageshi, ko ba komai zatasha rake.

Kwanciya tayi taja bargo tafara baccinta, Surayya batayi bacci ba ta tashi ta kunna fitila ta shimfiɗa salla tayita salla har bacci yafara ɗaukanta, Addu'a take Allah ya kawo musu mafita a wannan ƙauyen.

Washe gari kowa ya tafi tallan nononshi babu wanda yashiga harkan wani, a can wurin Saurayin Surayya yazo, Aneesa tana ganin yadda take ta sunnar da kai suna hira shikuma sai washe haƙora yake yasamu kyakkyawa, bakin ciki ne ya cikata tana gama saida nonon ta dau Kwaryan ta tawuce Kogi, ajiye Kwaryan tayi da kuɗin a gefe tasa kafafunta cikin ruwan tana lumshe ido, saida ta gaji kafin ta mike zata koma gida, duba kwarya tayi taga babu balle kuɗi, ko ina tafara dubawa babu kuɗin babu Kwaryan, Tambayan mutanen gefenta tafara ko sunga kwarya da kuɗi? Kowa yace bai gani ba, Aneesa ta ruɗe tana dube dube.

Idonta ne yacika da hawaye ta rasa yadda zatayi, a hankali tafara tafiya tana shiga cikin dajin ko zata samu, duba ko ta ina take bataga komai ba, kuka tafara tana tuna jibgan da Mama zatayi mata.

Bata koma gida ba har yamma yayi, gari yafara duhu, gefe ta zauna ta rabka tagumi ta rasa ta inda zata fara, idonta har ya bushe da hawaye.

"Aneesan Baba? Me kikeyi anan?"

Ganin Hamma Faruk ta mike tana kuka tace an sace kuɗin da kwaryan, riko hannunta yayi yace "Sannu shine kika ki komawa gida? Hankalin su Mama ya tashi, taho mutafi"
Binshi tafara ga yunwa Yana azalzalar cikinta, saida sukaje gida ta rinƙa raɓewa a jikinshi, mama tana hararanta, har yabawa Mama hakuri kafin ya juya zai tafi, binshi tayi, yace "ina zaki?"
"Zan kwana a gidanku yau"
Mama batayi magana ba har suka tafi, tana zuwa gidansu ta ci abinci, su Mairo suna nan, ta zauna suka fara hira.


              "Me martaba ya dawo yau Junayd ya mika mishi sandan mulki, dama abin ya dameshi baison rikewa, Dariya Abba yayi yace "Junayd an samu wani bawan Allah da zai baka magani a can Adamawa a wani kauye Ganye, bafulatani ne shi, saboda haka zaku shirya kaida Asad kuje zanyi muku kwatancen yadda zaku samu har kofan Ruganshi, wata kila zaka dace a wannan karon, kuma muna Addu'an Allah ya dacar dakai"

Girgiza kai yayi alaman "to Abba"
To ka sanar mishi jibi zaku tafi, bamu sani ba ko zaku dawo jibin ko kuka zaku jima acan, koma dai yaya ne zamuyi magana da Asad ɗin.

Giɗa kai yayi, shifa wallahi bayason zuwa wurin magani yanzu, ya gaji iya gajiya, har yanzu bai dace ba, kawai de bazai yiwa Abba musu ba, zaibi unarninshi, wata kila Allah ne ya nuna mishi mai maganinshi.

Ruma bata nan tana school hakan yasa ya zauna cikin kaɗaici yanata tunani, sako ya turawa Asad Asad yace "babu komai Allah ya kaimu jibin"

Da Ruma ta dawo yayi mata bayani jibi zasu tafi bata nuna wani damuwa ba tace "Allah yabada sa'a"
A ranshi yace "kenan baza tayi missing nawa ba? Kofa shike dama ba wani damuwa tayi dani ba"
Kwanciya yayi yana Addu'an Allah yasa ya dace a wannan karon.

Washe gari ya shirya kayanshi kamar yadda Asad ɗin ma ya shirya, Ammi ce take tayashi sa kayan a jaka, wani alkyabba ta ɗauka tasa mishi acikin kayan, cirewa yayi ya rubuta mata "Ammi banson su gane Ni ɗin wayene Gara naje a mai rufin Asiri dan banso na ɗaura musu wahala"
Jinjina kai tayi, tana alfahari da yaron nata akwaishi da tunani sosai.
Sun shirya mishi komai, Asad ne yazo gidan da yamma domin zai kwana washe gari saisu tafi da sassafe, yayi mamaki da Ruma batace zata bisu ba, tana ganinshi yana shirya kaya bata kulashi ba, saida ya gama yakai ɗakinshi wanda Asad yake ciki kafin yayi mishi saida safe yafito yadawo dakin Ruma, tana kwance tasa riga da wando yanzu tayi sauki dan har school taje yau, saida yayi wanka yazo yasa pyjamas ya kwanta a gefenta, kallon yadda take Chatting da friends ɗinta yayi, a hankali yasa hannu ya zame wayan, kallonshi tayi ya rubuta mata _Gobe zan tafi Me zaki bani wanda bazanyi kewa ba idan na tafi?_
Tana karantawa ta yatsine fuska, Ni me zan baka?.

Hannu yasa yana taɓa Breast nata, a hankali yake sauka har ya zagaya jikinta, ya rubuta _duk jikinki nakeso ki bani_

Itafa wallahi tafara gajiya da halin Yarima miye haka kamar aikin maita? Kullum abu ɗaya kamar abinci? Juya mishi baya tayi batace komai ba, ranshi in yayi dubu to yau duka sun ɓaci, a fusace ya tashi yabar mata ɗakin, taɓe baki tayi taci gaba da kwanciyarta, ina sonshi amma yafiye takura.

Ɗakin da Asad yake yaje ya kwanta a gefenshi, kallonshi yayi "malam lafiya?"
Shiru yayi yaja Blanket ya rufa jikinshi a hankali ya lumshe ido yanajin wani haushin Ruma yana bin jikinshi, yana Binta a hankali amma bata gani, Asad yasan akwai matsala shiyasa kullum yake Addu'a Allah yabawa Abokinshi lafiya kodan ya rage raɗaɗin dayake cikin zuciyarshi.

_washe gari_

Safwan da Ammi suka rakasu har wurin mota bayan yayi sallama da mai martaba, ya bashi kuɗi ne yawa kuma yakara yimishi Transfer a account nashi, Driver yace zai jasu Junayd yaki, shi da kanshi yafara tuki Asad na gefe yana ɗaga glass, hannu suke ɗaga musu har suka fita, babu motar Ruma a gidan Alama ta tafi school.

Ammi ce ta ɗaga hannu sama idonta yana cika da hawaye tace "Ya Allah ka taimakawa wannan bawa naka, kabashi lafiya kasa ya tafi a sa'a"
Ameen Safwan yafaɗa yana rikota, a hankali suke tafiya har yakaita ɗakinta ta kwanta.

"Ammi ki daina damuwa insha Allah Yaya zai samu lafiya"
"Allah yasa Saf"
Ameen.

Zama yayi a gefen Ammi yana Chatting da Sophy wacce suka shaƙu sosai yanzu, maganar banza kuma babu irin wanda batayi mishi, tun yanajin kunya bata biye mata har yafara yanzu, da tsakar dare bayan kowa yayi Bacci zai kirata a waya suyita hira, ganin har yanzu yana tsoronta yasa take nema ta saba dashi sosai.

Tafiya suke motar shiru kowa yana tunani, Asad ne ya kunna waka yanaji, da sauri Junayd ya canja zuwa karatu yana kallon Asad ɗin, a ranshi yace zamuyi tafiya ka kunna mana waka? Idan mukayi Accident muka mutu fa? Sai mu tashi da waka ta ranar kiyama?.

Hararanshi Asad yayi yaciro waya yana latsawa, Yasan garin Adamawa domin acan ya auro Ruma, saide baisan Kauyen da ake mishi kwatancen ba, idan sun iso Adamawa zaiyi tambaya.


 Kusan 4:30 na yamma suka isa Adamawa, a haka ma suna tsayawa a hanya suci abinci kuma suyi salla, da kwatance suka gane kauyen, tafiya suke har yanzu basu iso inda aka kwatanta musu ba.

"Anya Junayd bamu ɓata ba? Bana ganin komai sai rami da daji fa"
Girgiza kai yayi shima yana tunanin kamar sun ɓata, Parking yayi a gefen titi ya dafe kanshi da hannu, Lips nashi na kasa ya tura cikin bakinshi yana aikin tsotsa, Asad ne ya kalleshi yace "Kaga bafa wai tsayawa zamuyi kana tsotsan lips ba, bani Motar Zakayi na jamu dan naga Alaman ka gaji"

Buɗe motar yayi suka fita duka, yadawo mazaunin Driver shikuma Junayd ya koma wurin da Asad ɗin ya tashi, da gudu Asad ya jasu dan wallahi yana tsoron ƴan fashi da ƴan kidnapping, tafiya suke daga nesa suka fara hango Shanaye da ciyayi, kallon Junayd yayi yana dariya Alaman sun iso da yaddan Allah.

Gaba sukeyi shanu sunzo wucewa saida suka tsaya suka gama wucewa tass kafin suka wuce, ganin Bukka da ɗakunan fulanai yasa Junayd yaji a ranshi sun iso, mutane suka fara gani kyawawa suna fitowa daga Kauyen, wasu kuma suna komawa, Asad yace "Munzo" saida suka kara tafiya mai nisa kafin Asad ya tsaya yana Tambayan wasu mata da suka tashi daga saida nono inane Rugan Malam Arɗo?

Basajin Hausa sai kallonshi suke da alama ma tsoronsu sukeji dan sun gansu da mota, Junayd ne ya rubuta mishi abinda zai faɗa da fulatanci, a hankali yake karantawa sunaji sukace "ohhh Malam Arɗo?"
Kwatance sukayi mishi har kofar gidanshi, amma da harcen Fulani, Junayd ya gane Asad kuma bai gane komai ba, nuna mishi yake har suka isa Rugan da aka faɗa musu.

Baba lokacin ya dawo daga daji ganin sunyi Parking yasa ya tsaya yana kallon ko su waye ne, Asad ne ya buɗe marfin motar shima Junayd ya buɗe ya fito, kauyen jan kasa ne, ga Shanaye da ciyayi, Asad suka karasa ya gaisheshi, Junayd yayi mishi gaisuwan kurame, Baba ya amsa, Asad ne yayi mishi bayanin duk abinda yake tafe dasu, Baba yayi mishi tambayoyi shikuma ya bashi Amsa, Baba yace "Bismilla ku shigo insha Allahu zai samu waraka"
Kallon kara da zanan da aka kewaye gidan dashi yakeyi, Asad kuma hakalinshi ya koma kan magani ne, baima lura da gidan na zana bane.

A hankali suka shiga suka gaida Mama da take tsakar gida, Baba yayi mata bayani, tayi mishi sannu, ɗakin Hamma Umar ya nuna musu yace su shiga, Junayd ne yashiga shikuma Asad ya koma ya ɗibo musu kayansu, ɗakin a share domin shekaran jiya Aneesa ta share, kallon cikin ɗakin Yayi, ɗakin kasa ne amma a share komai tsab harda katifan dayake cikin dakin a gyare a shimfiɗe, gidan sunada tsabta amma talauci yana ɗawainiya dasu, Baba ne Yashigo musu da damammen Fura wanda Aneesa ta dama kafin su tafi, ajiye musu Yayi, Asad yace "mun gode" wani magani ya ciro yace "gashi yafara da wannan yanzu zan koma daji na tsinko wasu"
Godiya yayi ya karɓa.

Shan Furan Asad yafara Junayd Yana kallonshi, "bazaka sha bane?"
Girgiza kai yayi yana taɓe baki, jin Furan yayi daɗi yace "yakara auki"
Sha yake saida ya shanye tass yace "Masha Allah bazan koma gida ba saina kara shan irin Furan Nan"
Kallonshi kawai Junayd yakeyi.

Mama ta haɗa musu ruwan zafi tace suyi wanka, Junayd ne yafara sannan Asad, bayan sun fito suka sa kayansu wanda suka taho dashi acikin jaka, Junayd ya zauna a bakin katifa Yana pressing wayarshi, saide babu network, nashiga uku Ni Junayd ya zanyi muyi magana da Abba?

Asad yana shirya musu kayan da suka cire, Junayd yaji yanajin fitsari, fita yayi yana kallon cikin gidan ba kowa, hanyan Toilet ɗin yaje hannunshi rike da buta, cire wandon yayi yana kallon bayin har yafara fitsari.

Da gudu tashigo gidan tana matse kafa, a gefe ta wurgar da kwaryan tana tsalle, ɗan kwalinta ta cire, tashiga Toilet ɗin da gudu tanajin fitsari Kamar zai zubo mata, ganin mutum a ciki suka haɗa ido ta zabga wani uban ihu tafita da gudu, Mama!!! Mama!!!

"Meya faru kikemin wannan Kiran?"

"Mama waye a bayi?" 

"Meya faru?"
Ji tayi bazata iya fadawa Mama ba tace "naji kamar da mutum ne aciki" tana maganan tana haɗe kafanta wuri ɗaya fitsari har maranta yana rikewa, Mama tace "baƙi mukayi" 
Fitowa yayi daga bayin, wani haushi yaji dama zata shiga Toilet bazatayi knocking ba? Tsaki yayi a ranshi, bata kalleshi ba tawuce da gudu, saida tayi fitsarin kafin taji hankalinta ya kwanta.

Yana shiga ɗaki ya daure fuska, shikenan yarinya karama ta ganshi a banza, tsaki yakuma ja a ranshi, Asad yana kallonshi baice komai ba.

Surayya ce ta shigo da sallama, Kallon Mama tayi tace "Gaskiya Mama ki rinƙa yiwa Aneesa faɗa idan ta rike fitsari sai ya matseta kafin tayi?"

Mama girgiza kai kawai tayi, Asad dayake kwance ya tashi yana sauraran muryan dayake magana, kallon Junayd yayi yace "kaji wani zazzaƙan murya?"

Bai wuce na wannan yarinyar bane shiyasa ya harari Asad ɗin yaci gaba da latsa wayarshi,
Kallon kofar ɗakin Umar tayi tace "Mama su waye acikin ɗakin Hamma Umar?"

"Baki malam yayi daga birni marasa lafiya ne" Lokacin Aneesa tafito daga bayi tana ɗaura ɗankwalin data kwance.

Harara mama tayi mata, tace "Mama yaushe kuma sukazo?"

"Sai kije ki tambayesu"

Turo baki tayi Allah dai yasa ba kwana zasuyi ba.
Dan batason Baki sosai, musamman bakin ƙazamai ne.

Mama tayi girki amma gani take kamar wannan bazasu iya cin abincin ba, domin tuwon dawa ne da miyan kuɓewa danye da man shanu.

Kallon Aneesa tayi "to uwar dambu sai kiyi musu dambu ko?"
Dariya tayi tace "Tom Mama"
Atake ta hura wuta ta yi dambu, saida ta ɗibi nata me yawa kafin ta zuba musu nasu kaɗan a cikin samira, kai nata tayi ɗaki sannan ta ajiye musu nasu a kitchen, tafita tayi alwala ta koma ɗaki, Surayya ma alwala tayi, Sun shiga ɗaki kafin su yarima suka fito suma sukayi Alwala, kasancewa Mangariba ne bazaiyu suyi kasaru ba, raka'a uku sukayi, suna zaune suna jiran dawowan mai magani.

Mama ce ta kalli Surayya wacce tayi tagumi tace "tashi ki kai musu abincinsu" a hankali ta mike ta gyara zanin dayake jikinta wanda yake fari da adon ja ajiki, gashinta ta kitse wuri biyu, tasa Vest dari, ta ɗaura rigan Fulani irin daidai ciki ɗinnan, farin mayafi ta yafa ɗan guntu dashi, kitchen ta nufa tasan Aneesa da gangan taki sallama domin kada ace ta kaiwa baƙi abinci.

Kitchen taje ta ɗau Abincin a hankali take takawa, a bakin kofa tace "salamu Alaikum"
Asad ne ya amsa, ɗaga labule tayi tana murmushi tana kallonsu, garin baiyi duhu sosai bay hakan yasa Asad ya zuba mata ido, Tsarki ya tabbata ga Ubangijin da yayi wannan halittan, gaidasu tayi Asad ya amsa, kallon Junayd tayi tace "shikam baya magana nai?"

"Yanaji amma baya iya mayarwa"
"Allah sarki" hannu ta ɗaga mishi, shima yana kallonta ya ɗaga mata hannu yana ɗan murmushi.

Ajiye musu tayi ta mike Asad yana Kallonta, ta kawo musu ruwa me sanyi acikin Cup na silver.

Fita zatayi yace "ya sunanki?"

"Sunana Surayya" 

"Wow nice name Surayya" batace komai ba domin bata fahimci komai ba sai Surayyan dayace.

Tana fita yayi shiru yana kallon abincin data kawo, Gara shi zai iya ci amma ya zaiyi da Yarima?
Da mamaki yaga Junayd ya janyo samiran ya buɗe, ci yafara yana jin daɗin abincin, bai taɓa cin abincin da yayi mishi daɗi kamar wannan ba.

Kallonshi Asad yayi ganin yanaso ya cinye shima ya matso yafara ci, sunzo da drinks da snacks Iri-iri acikin motarsu, saide abincin da suka samu a gidan ya tafi da hankalinsu.

Ruwan sukasha daɗi shima babu wani kanwa kanwa ko gishiri gishiri a ciki, matsalan garin rashin wuta, Baba bai dawo ba sai kusan karfe 9 na dare, wasu itatuwa yazo dasu ya daddaka ya jiƙa a kwarya, ajiye musu yayi ya zauna suna hira da Asad, yarima saide yayi dariya kawai, ko kuma ya giɗa kai ko ya girgiza kai kawai, koda wasa Asad bai nuna Junayd ɗan sarki bane, Baba yanada mutunci a dare ɗaya har sun saba dashi, da alama gidan basu da matsala suna da son mutum, saida Baba zai fita yace "idan zaku iya sati anan to zakuyi idan bazaku iyaba sai kuje ku dawo"

Asad yace "Zamu iya" shi burinshi Abokinshi yasamu lafiya, Wani kallon zaka iya dai Junayd yayi mishi.

An kunna musu fitila ɗakin yayi haske kaɗan, kasancewar sun gaji shiyasa suka kwanta da wuri, Katifan nata faɗi shiyasa ya ishesu su biyu.

Aneesa sai cin abinci take, saida ta koshi da dambun kafin tasha Fura ta kwanta zata fara bacci.

"Aneesa kinje kin yiwa bakin nan sannu da zuwa?"

"A,a Adda"

"To ai hakan bai dace ba Manzon Allah SAW yace ka girmama bakon ka"

"Zanje da safe" tafaɗa taja bargo Dan bacci takeji sosai, Surayya saida tayi sallah kamar yadda ta saba kafin ta kwanta tayi bacci abinta.


*washe gari*

Sun tashi sunyi Sallan asuba, yarima yasha maganinshi kamar yadda Malam yace, Asad ne yayi bashi akan ka'ida yana runtse ido har ya shanye.

Saida gari yayi haske suka fita zuwa kofa suna kallon yanayin garin.

Aneesa ta shirya tsab, cikin kayan Fulani saide yau vest Baki tasa maimakon Fari, kitsonta guda biyu wanda ta ajiye a gefe da gefen wuyanta tayi mishi ado irin fari wanda Fulani sukeyi, powder ta shafa kaɗan, ta ɗauko man Baki ta shafa, wani ɗigo baki tayiwa goshinta, ba karamin kyau tayi ba, yau silifas tasa maimakon kundra, Surayya ma ta shirya zasu fita tare, Aneesa a gaba Surayya a baya, tashi Junayd yayi zai shiga gida dan yafara jin yunwa, karo sukaci da ita a bakin kofa, ai kuwa nonon gaba ɗaya ta juye mishi a fuska, jikinshi ya ɓaci, ihu tayi tana kiran Surayya, buɗe ido yayi a hankali ya zuba mata yana ganin yadda take buɗe ɗan karamin bakinta tana tsala ihu, shikam wannan yarinyar ko dai Aljana ce? Shine zaiyi ihu ko ita?

Hannu tasa tafara goge mishi jikinshi tana cewa "sannu" kwacewa yayi yakama hanyan shiga gida, Surayya ce ta ganshi tace "kayi Hakuri ɗan uwa"
Girgiza kai yayi yakoma cikin gida.

Ruwa tabashi ya wanke fuskarshi ya cire rigan ya koma ɗaki ya canja kaya, Asad yana daga baya yana ganin komai, Aneesa data ganshi tace "Ina kwana?"

A ranshi yace "wannan ai har tafi Yayarta kyau, wannan kamar ƴar tsana?"

"Lafiya kalau ya kike?"

"Ina lafiya ka bawa yayanka hakuri ba da gangan nayi ba"

"Kada ki damu babu komai"

Komawa ciki itama tayi ta ɗibo ruwa abuta ta wanke hannunta daya ɓaci, mama na cikin ɗaki batasan me yake faruwa ba, Surayya ce ta ɗau rigan ta wanke, ta shanya mishi.

Wani Nonon ta ɗiba ta daura a kanta, saida ta ɗaga labulan tace "sannu kayi Hakuri bada gangan nayi ba" bata jira me zaice ba ta saki labulen tana tura baki tayi gaba, dama Adda ce ta dameta sai taje ta basu hakuri.

Waya ya ciro yace "Asad gidannan sunada mutunci Amma wannan me kama da aljanun zata zame mana matsala ma lura yarinyar batada kunya"

Asad yana karantawa yafara dariya "tanada sauki kuma da dan har gaisheni tayi"
Ɗauke kai yayi yana Allah Allah agama bashi maganinshi subar gidan.

 *Chapter 11*


                  ~idan kaga Mun tafi saifa ka samu sauki, ko kuma idan Malam yace mu tafi, nikam ma banga ta tafiya ba ai dan wallahi naga mata, kaga kyau kuwa? Alaji ga hankali da nutsuwa ga zakin murya da iya kula da mutane"
Junayd yasan ba karya yayi ba, domin yarinyar akwai kyau amma wannan Kanwar Tata me kama da aljanu itace zatayi sanadiyyan barinsu gidan.

Aneesa suna tafiya itada Surayya tace "waɗannan amma daga gidan masu kuɗi suka fito ko Adda?"
Surayya datakejin haushin Aneesa ɗin tayi mata shiru, itafa Aneesa ko faɗa kukayi Anjima kaɗan zata manta tafara yimaka magana, tanada riko amma bata kin yiwa mutum magana.

"Ki koma ki tambayesu daga ina suka fito"
Bata kara cewa komai ba har suka isa wurin saida nono, yau abin mamaki batayi sha'awan zuwa kogi ba, haka kawai taji batada ra'ayin zuwa yau, saida suka ɗau hanyan tafiya Surayya tace "yau bazaki kogin bane?"

"A,a yau banada burin zuwa sai wani lokacin idan Allah ya kaimu kuma ai sauri nake yau naje na wanke kayana domin gobe zasuyi ranar Fulani na Adda Mairam"

"Umm ta Nan kikafi kauri ai"
Suna tafiya cikin nutsuwa har suka isa gida, Surayya ce tayi sallama Asad dayake zaune a gefen Mama yana hira, ya amsa yana kallonta, dama shi ma'abocin son surutu ne, Mama tana kunyan hira dashi amma saida ya sa ta daina suka cigaba da hira.

Ajiye roban hannunta tayi tana gaisheshi, cikin fara'a yace "Kun dawo?"

"Eh mun dawo"

"Masha Allah kema saiki zauna muyi hiran tare ko?"
Zama tayi a gefen Mama bata cewa komai saide tayi murmushi ta kawai, batada yawan magana, Aneesa tana shiga ta ajiye Kwaryan hannunta taje kitchen, tuwo tasa taci kafin ta fito tana shan ruwa, kallonta maka tayi tace "ke Aneesa? Bakiga bakon anan bane?"

"Yi hakuri Mama yunwa ke damuna shiyasa banga kowa ba dana shigo, amma yanzu ai na koshi ina Wuni Yaya?" Tayi maganar da siririn muryanta.

Dariya yayi yace "lafiya kalau Aneesa ya kike?"

"Lafiya kalau" tafaɗa tana shirin shiga ɗaki, jin muryan Baba ta dawo Baya tana dariya, ganinshi da leda taje ta karɓa tana cewa sannu da zuwa.

"Yawwa Aneesan Baba" 
Zama yayi sukaci gaba da hiran tare, Baba yakalli Asad yace "ina shi Junayd ɗin?"

"Yana ciki Baba bai fiyeson surutu ba shiyasa" 
"Allah sarki"
Aneesa ce ta buɗe ledan ta ciro su Dabino da kwakwan ta zuba akan plate ta dibi nata ta baiwa kowa nashi, Mama dama itace take cewa Aneesa ta raba.
Saida ta tashi zataje daki Baba yace "Aneesa? shi Junayd ɗin fa?"

"Waye kuma Junayd ni Aneesa?"
Yasan bata sanshi ba, yace "wannan na ɗakin" ɗaukan plate tayi tasa mishi dabino da kwakwan dayawa, tayi sallama, ganin bai amsa ba ta buɗe labulen ta shiga, yana zaune akan katifa sai trying na number ɗin Safwan yake amma baya shiga, ya buɗe data yanaso suyi Chatting saide saƙonni sunyi yawa hakan yasa ya ajiye a gefe yana kallon saitin kofan, buɗe labulen tayi ta shigo ta ajiye a gabanshi tace "ina wuni?"
Bai amsa ba sai ɗauke kanshi da yayi, taɓe baki tayi ta juya tabar mishi ɗakin, Da tasan bazai amsa ba wallahi da bazata gaishe shi ba, sai shegen jiji da kai kamar wani ɗan sarki, ko dan yaga yanada kyau ne oho.

Bin bayanta yayi da kallo yadda take tafiya ko waiwaye babu, ɗaga wayarshi yayi yafara yiwa Safwan Text ta Watsapp, shima Saf kamar jiranshi yake yace sunata gwada number ɗinshi baya tafiya, yayi mishi bayani yace ya faɗawa Ammi da Abba ya iso lafiya kuma anakan yimishi magani insha Allah nan da sati ɗaya zasu dawo, yana tura mishi ya karanta yace to Allah yabada sa'a.

Ganin Ruma a online yayi, baya wuce nasaba da tana Chatting da Kawayenta ne, baiyi mata magana ba yaci gaba da chat da friends ɗinshi, tunawa yayi da Ammi saida yace zai buɗe mata watsapp taki yadda da yanzu zasuyita Chatting da ita saboda yana missing ɗinta.


Kwance take akan gadon ɗakinta tana latsa wayarta, gefenta apple ne ta ɗaura kafa ɗaya kan ɗaya ta jingina jikinta da lallausan Pillow tana Chatting da friends nata a watsapp group.

Nadiya ce tace "Ke Gimbiya ina yarima kike online yanzu?"
"Yarima na ya tafi neman magani nifa har kin tunamin wallahi ban kirashi ba, lemme call him"

"Lalle Bakida hankali saiya danƙaro miki kishiya zakisan kin manta dashi"

"Wa? Yariman? Aina zaiyi kishiyar? Qi kinsan babu wata shegiya data isa tashigo ta zauna tsakanina da yarima, You know I love him and he love me more, so banga wata wacce ta isa tashigo gidannan ba"

"Ke Bama wannan ba da fatan bai gane kin zubar da ciki ba?"
"Tayaya zai gane? I know what am doing, kinsa am not illiterate bazai taɓa fahimta ba, kuma koda ya fahimta ta ina zai fara faɗamin? Nifa banson yafara maganan ma saboda banson takura wallahi"

Kashe Data tayi tafara kiran layinshi saide not reachable, komawa online tayi ta ganshi a online, Hi, ta tura mishi, saida yayi kusan 5mins kafin yace "Hello"

"I miss you my prince" haɗe rai yayi sai kace da gaske bacin ko a hanya bata kirasu taji ya suke ba.

Dan haushi ma ya kashe datan ya ajiye wayan a gefe, Dabino da kwakwan yafara ci, yamishi daɗi baisan meyasa agida baya damuwa da irin wannan abin ba, sai kuma gashi yanzu yanajin daɗin su.


Ammi sallah take ba dare ba rana, tana Addu'an Allah yabawa Yarima sauki, so take yafara magana shima yasan me yake ciki, Matarshi tana yin abinda taga dama dan kawai baya iya yimata magana, ta tabbata idan yasamu lafiya zata shiga hankalinta, bataso ta fiye yimata magana domin tasan yaran zamani yanzu zasuce ta takura mata.
Kamar kullum yauma tana zaune akan sallaya tana Addu'a, Safwan da ya maida hankali akan waya yanzu har video call sunayi da Sophy, musamman kwana biyu da Junayd baya nan yafi sakewa.

Kallonshi Ammi tayi ta haɗa dashi acikin Addu'a tana rokon Allah yakara shiryar mata da yaranta, harda Muneer Saida tasashi a Addu'a, bayan ta shafa tace "Kunyi waya da Ibti?"

Baiyi magana ba yanakan danna waya, da karfi tace "magana fa nake maka"
Firgigit ya ajiye wayar yatashi yaje wurin frij yaciro Dudu milk ya kawo mata, da mamaki tace "Saf me kakeyi a waya da baka ji idan anyi maka magana?"

"Babu komai Ammi"
Amma kasan cewa waya yana saurin kai mutum wuta? Kasan cewa ta hanyar waya mutum zai iya shiga wuta? Kwanaki naga baka damu da waya ba, kafi maida hankali akan karatu amma yanzu ka dage da latsa waya na tabbata Akwai abinda kakeyi, to Safwan kaji tsoron Allah, kada ruɗin Duniya yasa ka manta da ubangijinka ka maida hankalinka akan karatunka, kaga Yayanka duk da yake yanada laluri amma hakan bai hanashi dagewa ya nunawa duniya cewar Nakasa ba kasawa bace, yanzu kaga yana da asibiti wanda yake taimakon Al'umma dashi ko? To ka maida hankali kasan me kake ciki".

Nutsuwa yayi yanajin maganan Ammin nashi yana shiga jikinshi, gaskiya ta faɗa ya dauko hanyar lalata rayuwarshi, dolene ya gyara.

A hankali yace "nagode Ammi kuma zan gyara insha Allah"
Murmushi tayi a ranta tana Addu'an Allah yasa ba wani halin yakeson shiga ba.

Saf ɗakinshi yaje wanda yake gefen na Muneer, ganin ɗakin Muneer a buɗe yaje yayi koncking sannan ya shiga, ƴammata bayi ne suke gefenshi sunayi mishi tausa, wasu kuma sunayi mushi firfita, Saf kallonshi yayi yaga yadda ya kishingiɗa akan Timtim ɗin tsakar ɗakin, gefe guda kuma ga Tv a kunne yana kallon wani Film wanda babu abinda akeyi aciki sai baɗala "ku tashi kuje zamuyi magana da ɗan uwana"
Tashi sukayi dama ba so suke ba, shine yake sasu dole, wani haka zai kirasu yayita taɓa jikinsu, duk da baya Zina amma yanason taɓa jikin mata.

Kallon Saf yayi yace "meya faru" yana mikewa daga kishingiɗe dayake, 
"Haba Muneer ya zaka kira mata sunayi maka tausa? Koba komai ai mata sunada daraja, kuma ai hakan bai dace ba a addini"

"Naji yanzu me kakeson ka faɗamin?"
Babu zuwa nayi muyi hira kamar yadda ƴan uwa suke hira tare da ƴan uwansu"

Muneer watarana haka fa kai sarki ne, kasan meyasa nayi maka wannan maganan?

"A,a saika faɗa"
Naga kana kama da Abba ne yadda naga ka kishingiɗa.

"To ai Saf sarauta yana ɗakinku ne ba namu ba"

Da mamaki yace "meyasa kace haka?"
"Saboda Junaid shine Babba a cikinmu kaga yana nan bazaiyu nayi sarauta ba"
Shiru Saf yayi shikam baiyi maganan da manufa ba, amma yaga Muneer yanason canja magana, saida yaɗan zauna kafin yace "saida safe bari naje na kwanta saboda gobe akwai school"

"Allah ya kaimu"
Fita yayi yashiga ɗakinshi, yau bai kula Sophy ba domin maganan da Ammi tayi mishi ya shiga jikinshi sosai, so yakema ya goge number Sophy a wayarshi, saide yadda suka shaƙu bazai iya a lokaci ɗaya ba.


Yau Baba yabashi magani a gabanshi yasha, yace ya buɗe baki yayi magana, a hankali ya buɗe baki yanason yin magana amma maganar taki fitowa, "insha Allah zaka samu sauki kaci gaba da amfani da maganin komai zai daidaita da yaddan Allah"

Girgiza kai yayi, Baba ya fita, kallon Asad yayi, Asad yace "banyi tsammanin zaka iya buɗe baki Bama balle har kayi yunkurin yin magana, da yaddan Allah zamu dace a nan"

Murmushi yayi mishi,. Gyara zama Asad yayi yana kallon Junayd, gira ya ɗaga mishi Alaman me ya faru? 
"Junayd kasan Allah? Inason wannan yarinyar"

Taɓe baki yayi alaman wacce?
"Wannan Surayyan gaskiya ina sonta wallahi har cikin zuciyata, saide da wuya su amince min, dan zasuce Basu san inda muka fito ba".

Waya yayi mishi rubutu, kai magani mukazo nema ba aure ba, me Zakayi da wannan ƴar kauyen?"

"Tanada nutsuwa Junayd baka ganin ko magana zatayi bataso mu haɗa ido? Idan bamu auresu ba, haka zasu karasa rayuwarsu a daji?"

"Hakan yafi musu daɗi yadda rayuwarka take maka daɗi suma hakanne"
Ya rubuta a waya.

Karantawa yayi, yasan yarima bazai fahimceshi ba, yace "kasan me? Bazaka taɓa fahimta na ba"

Fita yayi yabar mishi ɗakin, A waje ya zauna kan wani dutse yana nazarin garin, Junayd baison ya ɓatawa abokin nashi rai amma ya lura kamar yanaso yayi gwaninta ne shiyasa bai bashi goyon baya ba, daga zuwa garin mutane kace kanason yarinya? Yarinyar akwai nutsuwa amma ai akwai ƴammata a Garinsu kyawawa wayayyu.

Surayya da taje zubar da shara ta ganshi yayi shiru, a hankali tace "lafiya kayi shiru bawan Allah?"

"Lafiya kalau Surayya sunana Asad"
"Sannu Asad ina ɗan uwan naka da ka zauna kai kadai? Shi bazai fito bane?"

"Zai fito Anjima zauna ki bani labarin garinku"
Tanada kunya bazata iya zama dashi wuri ɗaya har tabashi labari ba, a hankali tace "yanzu ai aiki nakeyi"

"Kinada saurayi?"
Tayi mamakin tambayan, tace "A,a amma na taɓa aure"
Kallonta yayi yana ganin kamar karya tayi mishi, sam batayi kama da wacce ta taɓa aure ba, "amma da wasa kike ko?"

"A,a gaskiya na faɗa maka na taɓa aure"
Ɗaukan roban sharan tayi "bari na karasa aikin ko?"
Giɗa kai yayi.

Saida ta ɗibi ruwa ta kaiwa Junayd ta gaisheshi kafin ta fito tana aikinta, Junayd shima ya shaida yarinyar akwai hankali to amma ai kauyanci yayi mata yawa, koda shike Gara ita akan wannan me kama da aljanun.

Yau basuje talla ba saboda sunada ranar Fulani na Mairam, Surayya ta gama aiki tass, tasawa su Junayd abincin ranar su hadda na yamma, itada Aneesa sunyi kwalliyan Fulani sunyi kyau sosai, asalinsu ya fito, yau Aneesa takara zama wata fara sosai, domin tayi wanka me kyau, Surayya ma tayi kyau, gashinta ta kama da robalin, gefe da gefe hakan yasa ya taso yayi kyau sosai, sallama suka yiwa Mama zasu tafi, Asad yafito zai ɗau abu a mota ya gansu, ganin yadda kayan yayi musu kyau yace "ina zuwa?"

Surayya ce ta amsa da "zamuje Rigan su Mairam"
"Ku jirani na ajiye abinnan saina kaiku ko?"

Kallon juna sukayi, Aneesa ƙasa ƙasa tace "waye zai shiga mota? Wallahi bazan shiga ba yana shiga gida zan tafi"
Yaji me tace.

Yayi murmushi yace "Ba a mota zamu tafi ba, idan zaki tafi to kije zamu zo da Surayya daga baya"
Kafin ya karasa maganan tayi gaba abinta, Surayya ma tafiya takeso tayi yace "dan Allah ki jirani"
Jin ya haɗata da Allah yasa ta tsaya ta jirashi, saida ya canja kaya yacewa Junayd nikam zan tafi nida Surayya zamuje yawo"

Junayd ya lura Asad ya faɗa cikin soyayyar wannan yarinyar, baiga laifinshi ba domin so baya gani, na tafi.
Murmushi yayi mishi.

Asad yafita ya samu Surayya suka jera suna tafiya, janta yake da hira batason magana amma ganin baida matsala ta buɗi baki tana bashi labari, shiru yayi yana jinta tana nuna mishi wurare ma cikin garin, harda yimishi kwatancen inda suke saida nono.

A take suka saba dashi, shima hira yake mata har suka isa gidansu Mairam, a karkashin bishiya ya zauna ita kuma tashiga ciki, ganin mutane sun taru a gidan taje ta ɗibo mishi ruwa zata kai taga Aneesa tana hira da Kawarta Kulu, tace "ke zo ki kaiwa Asad ruwa yana waje"

Badan taso ba ta mike takai mishi, yana ganinta yayi murmushi, itama mayar mishi tayi ta durkusa ta ajiye mishi "gashi inji Adda"
"Tom na gode Aneesan Baba"
Dariya tayi jin sunan daya kirata dashi, tafiya tayi tabarshi a wurin, haka kawai yakejin yaran a jikinshi, so yake yaga ya taimakawa rayuwarsu, gasu da kyau amma zasu kare rayuwarsu anan? Allah kabani ikon taimaka musu.

*YARIMA JUNAYD*

  Na
Jiddah S Mapi

 *Chapter 13*


                  ~Asad kuka yake yana kuma dariya a lokaci ɗaya, Junayd bai kara gane hankalinshi ba, wani bacci ne ya ɗaukeshi jikinshi yana rawa, a hankali Surayya tazo gabanshi ta zauna, hannu tasa ta dafashi cikin sanyin murya tafara magana "Ka daina kuka Addu'a Zakayi mishi Allah yakara mishi lafiya"
Ciro hannunta yayi daga kafaɗarshi ya rike yana murzawa har yanzu idonshi bai daina hawaye ba, yace "mun gode muku mun gode Allah yabiyaku da gidan Aljanna"

"Allah zamu godewa"

"Surayya na godewa Allah yarima yafara magana"

"Yarima kuma? Junayd dai" da sauri yace "Eh Junayd yasamu sauki"

Aneesa ganin zazzaɓi ya kamashi ta ɗibo wani Ganye ta jiƙa a ruwa, zuwa tayi gabanshi ta janye bargon daya rufa dashi, ganyen ta ɗauka tana shafawa a wuyanshi, zama ta gyara akan katifa jin jikinshi yayi zafi sosai, saida taji jikin yafara sanyi kafin ta mike tana kallon Asad "Hamma Asad a rinƙa shafa mishi wannan Maganin"

"To" karba yayi yafara shafa mishi a jiki, cikin ikon Allah sai gashi jikinshi ya daina rawa kuma ya daina yin zafi sosai.

Surayya tafita zuwa kiran Mama a makota, bayan ta sanar da ita Junayd yafara magana saida Mama tayi sujjada domin godewa Allah, hakika tana tausayin Yaron domin yanzu ne zai fara rayuwarshi me kyau.
Sun koma gida har yanzu bai tashi daga bacci ba, Aneesa ce tayi girki yauma abinda takeso ta dafa wato Dambu.

Asad yana zaune a gefenshi ji yake kamar yayi Text a gida yace Junayd yasamu sauki, saide kawai ya bari saboda yanaso yayi musu surprise, 
Saida ta gama girkin tayi shara ta wanke kwanukan duka, saida tagama komai kafin taje garken shanu ta tatso nono acikin kwarya, gida tashiga dashi, bata bari yasha iska sosai ba, ta nufi ɗakin su, mikawa Asad tayi tace "Hamma Asad? Gashi ka tasheshi yasha kada yasha iska hakan zai kara mishi lafiya"
Karɓa yayi yana mamakin irin baiwan yarinyar, tanada baiwa domin ta iya bada magani, saide kawai tanada shiririta.

Tashin Junayd yayi, a hankali ya mike har yanzu bakinshi bai daina rawa ba, sa mishi Kwaryan yayi a baki yace "kasha" toshe hanci yayi yakarɓa yasha, saida yayi rabi ya kauda kanshi, Aneesa ganin bai shanye ba, ta karaso tana gyara gashinta daya zubo mata a gadon bayanta, tace "duka zai shanye fa"
Kallonta yayi duk da yana cikin ciwo saida yaji ta bashi haushi wannan muguwa ce wallahi.

"Bashi mana Ya Asad"
Ɗago Kwaryan yayi Junayd ya ɗauke kai, dasairi ta zauna a gefe ta karɓa tana haɗa fuska, badan taso ba take bashi so take ya warke yabar musu gida, gashi baison magani, bakinshi takai ta tsareshi da manyan idanunta, ganin cikin idonta yaji bazai iya kin karɓa ba, a hankali yafara kurɓa har saida ya shanye duka, tashi tayi da kwaryan a hannunta tafita daga ɗakin.

Komawa yayi ya kwanta baccin dama bai isheshi ba, har kusan Mangrib yana bacci.

Time da Baba ya dawo Asad yayi mishi bayanin cewa Junayd ya fara magana, Baba yayi farin ciki sosai, sai a lokacin yace "Asad inaso nayi magana da iyayen Junayd"

"Baba akwai matsala ne?"

"Eh akwai matsala amma nafison nayi magana da iyayenshi ne"

Asad ji yayi kamar yayiwa Baba bayani sai kuma ya tuna Junayd yace kada ya faɗa, Baba zanyi musu bayani idan mun koma insha Allah.

"To Ba komai Asad sannan inaso ku kula dashi sosai"

"To Baba" sunkuyar da kai yayi akwai magana a bakinshi amma yanajin kunya da nauyin yin maganan.

Lura da yanayinshi Baba yayi yace "Akwai damuwa ne Asad?"

"Eh..Baba.dama...dama akan Surayya ne" 

"Yi magana babu damuwa ina jinka"

"Baba dama akan Surayya ne idan ba damuwa inaso iyayena suzo ayi magana aurenta nakeso nayi"

Shiru Baba yayi, sai daga bisani yace "kayi magana da ita idan ta amince babu damuwa"
"Tom Baba Kanin Babana zasu zo domin Mahaifina Ya rasu"

"Allah yaji kanshi da rahama, amma zaku bar tafiyan zuwa jibi saboda yasamu ɗan karfi kaɗan"

"To" yafaɗa kanshi a kasa, yaji daɗin maganar da Baba yayi mishi, yasan ta wurin Sumayya bazai samu matsala ba, haka kawai yakejin son yarinyar yana bin jini da zuciyarshi.

Yana kwance akan Katifa rabonshi da yin mafarkin yarinyar ya jima, sai yau ya kara yin mafarki wai gata zata faɗi a ruwa, a firgice ya tashi yana addu'a.
Asad ne Yashigo yayi tsalle yana murna, kallonshi yayi a hankali ya buɗe baki da muryanshi wanda baya fita yace "Lafiyanka?"

"Junayd Baban Surayya ya amince na Turo manya suzo ayi magana"
Junayd ya lura Asad ya faɗa soyayyan yarinyar ba kaɗan ba, hakan yasa yayi murmushi ya gwada tashi, ji yayi jikinshi yayi nauyi sosai, hannu ya mikawa Asad ɗin, a hankali ya taimaka mishi har ya tashi, bayi yakeson zuwa, a hankali yake takawa Asad ya rikeshi da kyau.

Baba dayake cikin ɗaki labule a ɗage yace "Aneesa?" Amsawa tayi tana kwance kanta, kitsone dama guda biyu ta warware duk domin gobe aure, kanta babu ɗankwali ta fito, gashin ya sauka har gadon bayanta, riga da siket ne na Atamfa a jikinta yamata kyau sosai, ɗakin Baba ta shiga ta durkusa "gani Baba"

"Sa mishi ruwan wanka"
Tashi tayi tana kallonshi yadda ya haɗa fuska yana kallonta, taɓe baki tayi taje wurin drum ta ɗibo ruwan a bokiti ta kai bayin kallon Asad tayi tace "Ya Asad nakai Ruwan"

"To Aneesan Baba mun gode" hararan Junayd tayi ta murguɗa baki tabar wurin, ko kallonta bai kara yiba, saida Asad ya tabbata yasamu wuri me kyau kafin yafito yabarshi, wanka yayi yana kallon cikin bayin, me kyau na kasa ne da zana amma komai a gyare tsaf.

Kowa yanajin daɗin rayuwa a inda yake, shikam badan neman magani ba ina zai iya zama anan? Babu fanka bale Ac ga sauro har jikinshi yafara tabo, zafi da sauro ya isheshi.

Yana zaune a gefe yana jiran fitowarshi ganin yana dafa jikin bango Ya rikoshi yana mishi sannu, kallon Asad yayi fuskarshi yayi fayau kamar zaiyi kuka yace "Asad kalli jikina duk tabo sauro ga zafi"
Dama yanaso yayi magana amma bayida bakin yi.

"Sorry jibi zamu tafi ai"
"Gobe ko Jibi?"

"A,a sai jibi gaskiya Yarima ka kwantar da hankalinka kamar yau ne zamu koma gida" 

Yatsine fuska yayi badan yaso ba zai zauna, yayi missing Amminshi wallahi.

Mai ya shafa dama sunzo da Lotion ɗinsu, abinci aka kawo musu yana hararanta itama ramawa tayi tafita a ɗakin, ta lura yanada uban raini da girman kai dolene ta rinƙa zagewa tana rama duk abinda yamata.

Asad sun fita da Surayya aikanta akayi yace zai rakata, batayi musu ba suka fara tafiya yana kokarin yimata hiran soyayya amma tana gocewa, labarin Giɗaɗo tafara bashi, yace baison jin wannan labarin, bata kara yimishi zancen ba har taje tasiyi abun, kwana biyu har ta manta da saurayinta mai saida rake, Asad yashiga zuciyarta sosai.

Aneesa da Mama ne a gida, tana cikin ɗaki tana bacci Mama ta tasheta tayi salla, a hankali take tafiya dan baccin yana jikinta har yanzu, fitowa yayi daga ɗaki zai ya ganta tana yatsina fuska, buta ya ɗauka yayi alwala yana yiwa Mama sannu da gida, Aneesa ma alwala tayi tana kallon yadda yake tafiya kamar zai faɗi, ganin zai faɗi taje da gudu ta rikeshi, ajiyan zuciya ya sauke jin bai faɗi kasa ba, kallonta yayi yadda ta zazzaro ido tana kallonshi, da alama ta tsorata sosai.

Tafiya yafara a hankali tana rike dashi, saida ta kaishi ɗaki taga zai kwanta sannan ta sakeshi, faɗuwa yayi akan katifan kafin ya juyo tafita a ɗakin.


************
Rana bata karya kamar yadda Baba ya sanar musu yau ne zasu tafi, Yanzu yaɗan samu karfin jiki kuma magananshi yana fita sosai, tun safe Asad suka ɗibo ruwa ya wanke motar da kyau, Surayya tana gefe tayi tagumi tana kallonshi, ya naɗe ƙafan wando da hannun riga yana aikin wanke mota, ganin ta zuba mishi ido babu ko kyaftawa yasa ya ɗibo ruwa kaɗan a hannunshi ya watsa mata a fuska yana dariya.

Goge fuskarta tayi saiga hawaye sunabin kumatunta, da mamaki yazo gefenta ya zauna, kallon yadda ta haɗa kai da gwiwa tana kuka yayi, to dan ya watsa mata ruwane take wannan kuka?

"Kiyi hakuri da wasa nayi"

Ɗago kai tayi idanunta sun koma jawur tace "Asad nasan idan kun tafi ba lallene ka sake dawowa ba, kuma ka koyamin sonka, dan Allah kada ka gujeni kada kuma ka yaudareni"

Ya lura tun ɗazu akwai abinda yake damunta, ashe shine damuwan 
"Surayya? Zan ci gaba da sonki har karshen rayuwata, idan kinga ban dawo ba saide in mutuwa nayi, amma insha Allah zan dawo nan bada jimawa ba"

Bai kulata ba domin tuna abinda yafara kira lokacin daya fara magana a karo na farko dayake da wayo a duniya, tunda ya taso yana yaro bai taɓa magana ba, bashida wayo time ɗin dayake magana, yanzu dayayi wayo yafara magana maimakon yafara da sunan Ammi ko Abba ko Saf ko ibti ko Ruma, sai yafara da wata wai Aneesa, yarinyar da bai santa ba, amma wai yafara magana da sunanta, shiga ciki yayi ya jingina da jikin kofan bayin, tunawa yayi da gidansu wanda yake wanka a bayin ciyawa da taɓo, Dambu ya tuna wanda suke kawo mishi da kuma Fura wanda yakesha kullum da yamma, a hankali ya lumshe ido yana tuna yanayin garin.

Wurin shower yaje bai cire gajeren wandon dayake jikinshi ba ya kunna ruwa, a hankali ya lumshe ido yanajin ruwan yana bin jikinshi, gashin kanshi yasa hannu yana murzawa ruwan yana shiga jikinshi, saida yaji sauki kaɗan daga tunanin da yake, yayi alwala yafita, bayan ya fito tasa riga da wando ta ɗaura after dress a sama, da alama fita zatayi dan tasa glass, kallonshi tayi ta cikin glass ɗin tace "Baka bani amsa ba"

Yasan idan ya faɗa mata to yau babu kwanciyan hankali a gidan, mai yashafa yasa riga longsleev ligt yellow, da wando baƙi dogo wanda yake da ado a wurin aljihun, sajen fuskarshi yakeso yaje yaɗan rage, kanshi ya gyara yashafa hair oil da perfume, waya ya ɗaga zai fita tace "Yarima magana fa nake kuma kana jina"

"Such a nice voice" zata iya rantsuwa bata taɓa jin namiji me murya zazzaƙa kamar na yarimanta ba, so take taji yakara magana.

"Eh inason ji koda bazai min amfani ba"

"Gimbiya Ruma meyasa kika damu haka? Naga time ɗin dana tafi baki damu dani ba, ko kirana bakiyi ba"
Wow yarima nada zaƙin murya, gaskiya yanzu Yakamata tafara ɗamara domin yaki da ƴammata masu bin mazan mutane, domin fa ita babu kishiya a lissafin rayuwarta.

Ganin tafaɗa duniyar tunani ya juya yafita daga ɗakin yana kallon agogon dayake ɗaure a tsintsiyar hannunshi, ganin kusan 9 kuma yanason zuwa office yau yasa yaɗan yatsine fuska, Umma Suwaiba ce ta tsayar dashi tana kallonshi tace "ɗan gidan Abba jiya ban samu na tayaka murna ba, Alhmdllh Kasamu sauki Allah yasa ka amfanar da mutane"

Junayd ko juyawa bai kuma yiba balle yasa tana kallonshi, dakin Abba yaje suka gaisa yace zai wuce Asibiti

"No Abba akwai Abinda ban karasa ba shiyasa nakeson zuwa yau ɗin"

Kallon Ammi yayi wacce take gefen Abba tana cin abinci, yanajin daɗin zaman iyayen nashi, abin farin ciki ne kaga iyayenka suna zaman lafiya cike da so da kaunan juna, abin yana birgeshi.
Gaisheta yayi yace zai wuce, Albarka tasa mishi tace Allah ya tsareshi, Da Ameen ya amsa yafita.

Tafiya yake cike da izza da mulki, kowa sai aika mishi gaisuwa da sakon taya murna suke, ɗaga musu hannu yake, har ya isa gaban mota, wani lafiyyayen motane kiran Bugatti ya je ya tsaya a wurin, Driver ɗinshi ne yazo da gudu yana gaishe da Yarima, Buɗe mishi mota yayi ya shiga ya zauna a baya, kallon Agogo yake fuskarnan babu alamun murmushi ko walwala, Yarima miskili ne Bana wasa ba, dama kuma sai ya haɗu mishi da cuta a baya, yanzu kuma rashin magana yariga yabi jikinshi.

Yau Excort sun rakashi motoci sunkai biyar a bayan nashi, duk sun da bakaken kaya Suit da glass a fuskarsu Baki, dogari kuma mota ɗaya su kuma da bulala a hannunsu, kallon cikin garinshi yake ta cikin tinted glass ɗin dayake motar, yayi missing ɗin garin sosai, basu jima ba suka isa cikin Asibitin Yarima Junayd wanda yake ganin kamar ma yakara kyau ne, komai yana tafiya yadda ya ɗaurasu akai.

Da gudu Excort yazo ya buɗe mishi marfin mota, karamin leda yaciro daga mota ya kunna yanabin bayan yarima wanda yake tafiya a hankali yana kallon cikin Hospital ɗin, duk inda suka wuce sai an durkusa an gaidashi, hannu yake daga musu wani kuma ya wuce kawai batareda ya amsa ba.

Har cikin Office nashi aka kaishi, saida ya zauna akan Kujeran da aka gyara mishi mai kyau aka canja yanayin Adon daga silver color zuwa ja da fari irin na gidan sarauta.

fara yimishi yayi saida ya gama Junayd yakalli fuskarshi yaga yadawo normal, fita yayi dama sai wata ake biyanshi, saida ya kimtsa wurin kafin ya tafi, Junayd ya koma wurinshi ya zauna yana cigaba da Aiki.

Makulli ya ɗauka batareda ta sani ba, ya zame wayarta dayake gefe yafita ya kulleta ta waje, bata ankara ba saida taji karan rufe kofa, ganin babu wayarta tafara ihu a ɗakin tana bubbuga kofa, yana jinta bai ko waiga ba yawuce wurin Abbanshi, Zama yayi suna hira aka kira Abba, Dadyn Ruma ne ya yiwa Abba bayanin abinda yake faruwa wanda Momynta ta faɗa mishi, yace "zan kashe muyi magana dashi saina kiraka"

"Meya haɗaka da Ruma?"

Giɗa kai tayi, tace "to Abba"
