"Gobe ibtisam Zata dawo hutu"
"Allah yakowata lafiya" Saf yayi maganan yana jin daɗi, idan Ibti tana nan suna yawo sosai, domin suna zuwa gidan Kawayenta, shikuma bayida Freinds dayawa, sai Ahmar shima yanzu bai fiye shiga harkanshi ba domin yana neman yasashi a hanyan Zina, suna Chatting da Sophy amma ba sosai ba.

"Adda Yaufa wata biyu da sati uku da tafiyansu kin tabbata bazasu dawo ba ko?"

A hankali yake takawa yana kallon Asad ɗin dayake tsaye yana rike da hannun get, sai yau kaga daman zuwa gidana? Gaskiya Junayd bakamin adalci ba"
Dariya yayi kawai yana shiga ciki, a hankali suke tafiya suna hira, a babban palour ya zauna Asad yakira Surayya tazo suka gaisa, ya rinƙa tsokanar ta wai Amaryarsu, dariya kawai Surayya takeyi tana ɗan ɓoye fuskarta dan kunya yake bata.

Aneesa tasa Abaya baki tayi Rolling kanta ta kame gefen da pin, Wanda yake pink color, Fadwa Kuma pitch ɗin abayane a jikinta sunyi kyau sosai, jikinsu yana fitar da kamshi, Aneesa ta shafa powder da Lips yakara mata kyau, harda kwalli tashafa yasa farin idonta yin kyau, ga gashin idon dasuke zara zara ta shafa musu mascara, kamar wata balarabiya haka tafito, jaka ne a hannunta tashigo palour a gajiye ta ajiye tana kwanciya akasan Tiles ɗin, bata kula yana ɗakin ba, Surayya ta gani da Asad, "sannu da gida ya Asad"
"Yawwa Aneesan Baba"

Turo baki tayi tace "lafiya kalau"

Ameen.

Bata damu dasa hijabi ba dan tasan yanzu kam ai ya tafi koda shi ɗin mayene, fita tayi tanajin Muryan ya Asad a waje da Alama waya yake.

Babu Surayya a cikin gida a hankali take takawa zuwa palour, tasan yanzu kam ya tafi jin ana waka a Tv tafara rawa kaɗan tana shiga palour, batasan yana zaune a gefe ba, taje gaban Tv tana canja channel ido ya zuba mata yana kallon karfin halinta, a zatonshi tasan yana nan.

*YARIMA JUNAYD*

Jiddah S Mapi

 *Chapter 32*


                  ~washe gari su Unty Surayya ne suka haɗa mata kayanta sunyi mata wayo da cewar su sai Anjima zasu tafi, ita tafara tafiya Kallon Fadwa tayi wacce aka jawa kunne kada ta kuskura tace ba tafiya zasuyi ba, ta rungumeta lokacin da zata shiga motan Ya Asad ɗin, ɗagawa Adda hannu tayi tace "Sai kun dawo jibi ɗin"
Itama Adda murmushin yaƙe kawai takeyi, ɗazu sunyi waya dasu Mama da Baba hadda Hamma Umar Amma bata bawa Aneesa ba dan tasan zata iya rike
Ice mata tace zata koma gida itakam.

Asad yace "Aneesan Baba?"
"Na'am ya Asad"

"Inaso kiyi hakuri da zaman kwana biyu da zakiyi a gidansu Junayd kinji?"

"To Ya Asad" tana wasa da yatsanta tayi maganan.
Tausayi take bashi tayi karama har yanzu da wannan rayuwar na auren me mata kuma baya sonta bata sonshi.

Har cikin ɗakin Ammi ya kaita, tayi murnan ganinta musamman Ibtisam tafi kowa farin ciki, taje fadan sarki ta gaisheshi taje ɗakin Umman Muneer ta gaidata, sai harara take aika mata ta kasa.

A ɗamin Ibtisam ta yada zango, suka fara hira, Safwan dayaji tazo ba karamin farin ciki yaji ba.

Junayd kuma yana kallonta tana ninke mayafin jikinta ya juya ya koma Part ɗinshi, idan ya tuna abinda sukayi sai yaji kaman ya shaƙeta domin itace tafara nemanshi.

Da dare suna wurin ɗinner da Abba da kowa da kowa, Aneesa kanta a kasa takasa cin abincin, bata kuma tsorata ba saida suka haɗa ido da Ruma, Ammi tace su koma ɗaki suci acan, ɗiba musu Ibtisam tayi suka koma ɗakinta acan ga sake taci kaɗan, Safwan Yashigo sukayita hira, shima ya jonasu sunacin abincin tare, sauƙin kanshi yasa take sonshi.

Shi da Ruma sai kallo ta bashi hakuri ta rokeshi ya rufa mata asiri tayi rantsuwa da Allah bazata kara zubar da ciki ba, bai kulata ba amma bai faɗawa kowa ba, har yau su Ammi basusan abinda ya faru tsakaninsu ba.
Saide baya shiga ɗakinta koda tashigo nashi fita yake yabarta.


****************
Ruma ta tafi school Junayd yau yana hutu bazashi aiki ba, kwance yake a ɗaki yana tunanin duniya, tunanin mafarkin dayake yawan yi yayi, Ammi ganin Ruma ta tafi ta fito da Plate wanda akasa snacks da glass cup da Drinks tana tafiya, Aneesa da take zaune tana gyara farcenta ta tashi da sauri ta karɓi plate ɗin, kallonta Ammi tayi cikin murmushi tace "ɗakin Junayd za'a kai"
Bataso ba amma bazata iya yiwa Ammi musu ba.

Wata ƴar aiki ce tayi mata jagora har zuwa bakin kofan, so take ta bata tace takai mishi amma tana ganin kamar tayiwa Ammi raini ne.

A hankali ta tura kofar da kafanta bakinta ɗauke da sallama, Allah yasa baya palour shine Addu'an datakeyi.

Ai kuwa tana shiga ta ganshi yana kallon kofa a tsorace Plate ɗin ya faɗi Cup din ya tarwatse ji kake tasssss, jikinta yafara rawa, hannu tasa da sauri tana kwashe glass ɗin dayake kasa.
Kallonta yayi yadda take rawan jiki wurin kwashewa, Dressing ɗin jikinta ya kalla babu ma ko mayafi haka tazo?

Cikin wani irin tsawa dayasa ta rikice tafara kuka yace "ke wace irin kazama ce?Bakida hankali ko? Sa'anki ne Ni? Banza kazama karuwa"

Manyan idanunta ta ɗago tana kallonshi jin sunan daya kirata "karuwa?"
"Eh karuwa idan baki saba da hakan ba tayaya ranan kikasan yadda ake kissing ɗin namiji?"

Ranta idan yayi dubu ya ɓaci,  zaki kwashe ki fita ko sai nakira dogari sun zanemin ke.

Ai da wani irin rawan jiki tafara kwashewa saida hannunta ya fashe glass ɗin ya sossoketa, fita tayi tana sharan kwalla "karuwa?"
Yau bazata kwana a gidannan ba, ko a Bola zata kwana bata damu ba amma banda wannan gidan.

A firgice da ɓacin rai take tafiya ranta a tafarfashe, Ammi ce ta hangota yadda take share kwalla tana ciza leɓe, a hankali takira sunanta, da sauri ta share hawayen tana kakalo murmushin yaƙe, juyowa tayi kamar babu abinda ya faru tace "Ammi barka"
Hannunta datake ɓoyewa wanda yake jini Ammi ta kalla "meya sameki?"
"Babu komai faɗuwa nayi shine glass ɗin...."
"Aneesa meya sameki?"
Ya riko hannunta yana kallon yadda jini yake ɓulɓula, janyota yayi suka zauna akan Sofa Ammi tana tsaye har yanzu takasa sauke hannunta sai binsu take da ido, da gudu yaje ya ɗauko firstaidbox yazo, saida ya tsaya da jinin ta hanyar toshewa da audiga kafin ya wanke mata yana aikin cewa "Sannu"
Kallonshi takeyi tana murmushi, Ammi ta juya cikin sanyin jiki ta koma ɗaki, karya kai tayi tana kallonshi "Nagode ya Saf"
"Ki dainamin godiya is pleasure"

"Ya Saf yau zan koma gida"

"Zaki koma kuma? Ai su Ya Asad sunce sai sunyi 2days to a ina zaki zauna?"

Riko hannunshi tayi tana hawaye tace "bazan iya zama a gidanku ba Ya Saf bazan iya ba"
A rikice yace "me akayi miki? Nine? Ko Ibtisam? Ko Ammi ce?"

"Ba ku bane ku masu sona ne amma Junayd baya sona nima na tsaneshi Ya Saf banson ko ganin fuskarshi ne, I really hate him bansonshi na tsaneshi"
Janyota yayi jikinshi yana cewa "sorry Baby ki daina kuka kibarshi ki daina shiga harkanshi kinji?"
Ɗago kai tayi tace "ban shiga harkanshi ba ina taka tsantsan da shiga duk abinda ya shafe shi amma ya tsaneni ya tsani ganina kamar yadda nima ban taɓa tsanan wani halitta kamar shi ba"

"Sorry Baby"
Saida ya lallaɓata kafin ya kaita ɗakin Ibtisam yace ta kwanta tayi bacci, Kwanciya tayi tana kallonshi tace "bazan iya bacci ba Mr love zuciyata tana tafarfasa"
"Dan Allah Baby kiyi hakuri idan na ganki cikin wannan damuwan nima zan shiga damuwa Baby ki daina damuwa Please"

"Shikenan na daina kaje zanyi baccin"
Tafiya yayi, yana fita ta tashi ta zauna, ganin zaman bazaiyi mata ba, ta mike taje gaban mirror, kallon jikinta tayi ta juya takara kallo, "me yayi kama dana karuwai a jikina? Kibani amsa Aneesa me yayi kama dana karuwai a jikina?"
Ita da kanta take Tambayan kanta.

Ganin Batada amsa tasa kanta a jikin stool ɗin gaban mirror tafara kuka, babu wanda ya taɓa cimata mutunci kamar Junayd meyasa zai kirata da wannan sunan? Yace mata kazama bata damu ba gashi yau har yana cemata karuwa?"
Ibtisam ce ta buɗe kofa tana murza ido da alama bacci tayi, ganin Aneesa ta kifa kai tana kuka, ta karaso da sauri tana ɗagota, "meya sameki Anee?"

"Ibtisam ta tsani Yayanki Junayd na tsaneshi, nasan bazakiji daɗi ba amma yazama dole na faɗi abinda yake raina domin kada ya dameni har ya kasheni, na tsani Junayd"
Zama tayi a gefen Bed tana kallon Aneesa, yayi mata laifi ne shiyasa take faɗan haka, saida ta huce kafin tace "kiyi hakuri baki fahimceshi bane Amma yanada sauki"
Batayi magana ba sai jan hanci take, saida Ibtee ta lallaɓata kafin ta kwanta ta fasa tafiya.

Ammi dafe kai tayi anya basuyi kuskure ba? Basuyi kuskuren haɗa Aneesa da Junayd aure ba kuwa? Sunyi hakan ne domin wannan shine hanyan da zasu taimakawa mahaifinta wanda shima ya taimaka musu amma tana ganin kamar fa abin zaizo yazama damuwa, Gara ta bayyanawa kowa abin idan Aneesan tace bataso saisu raba auren kawai.

Yadda ranshi ya ɓaci yasan idan yaci gaba da zama zai iya samu heart attack, makulli ya sura yafita daga ɗakin a zuciye ya mugun tsani fuskan wannan yarinyar koda yayi niyyan daina tsanarta sai yaji sabon tsana yafara shiga zuciyarshi, fita yayi a gidan gaba ɗaya, ya kunna waka yana saurare, hanyan gidan gonanshi ya nufa so yake yaje can ya huta.
Tafiya yake hankali a kwance, gani yayi kamar ana binshi ta cikin madubi, da sauri ya gyara madubin yaga kuma Babu kowa, a ranshi yace kodai gizo idonshi ke mishi, cigaba yayi da tafiya ba idonshi bane tabbas ana binshi, ido ya zubawa madubin yana ganin wasu mutane guda biyu masu bakaken kaya akan Mashin suke binshi, canja wurin zuwa yayi yarinka shiga cikin mutane bai yadda yaje inda babu mutane ba.

Zagaya yayi ya kama hanyan komawa gida, bayan wani wuri wanda yake babu mutane dayawa yaga ɗayan yaciro bindiga daga Aljihu yayi saitin tayanshi, "Subhanala inni kuntu minazzalimin"
Shine abinda yake maimaitawa.
Kwana yayi  batareda ya shirya ba, jikin motan ne ya bugu da bango bai tsaya duba ciwon dayaji ba, yabar wurin da mugun speed, this is the second time da aka bishi haka, sau biyu yana tsallake rijiya da baya, bai tsaya ko ina ba sai gidansu, buɗe mishi Get akayi yashiga a rikice ba karamin tashin hankali yashiga ba, Parking ɗinma baiyi mai kyau ba yafito, Fada yaje domin yanaso Abba yasan halinda yake ciki.

Yana kishingiɗe, suna hira shi dasu waziri, a rikice ya shigo Abba ya kalleshi yace "Lafiya?"
Umarni yayiwa su waziri da su fita, fita sukayi ya zauna yace "Abba second time kenan dana tsira da raina a wurinsu"
A kiɗime Abba yace "su wa?"
"Abba wasu mutane ne suke bina akan Mashin kullum sai sun ciro bindiga zasuyi harbi Allah yana tseratar dani"

"Innalillahi wa inna ilaihiraji'un Junayd ba shiyasa nake cewa ku rinka fita da security's ba?"

"Abba naga wai ba nisa zanyi ba"
"No Junayd rayuwarka tana cikin hatsari shiyasa banso kana fita kai kaɗai"

"Abba to ya akayi suke sanin idan na fita Ni kaɗai?"

Shiru Abba yayi, hakika wannan abin tunani ne tayaya suke sanin time ɗin daya fita shi kaɗai?

"Kasan me? Jeka ɗaki ka kwanta ka huta zanyi bincike akan hakan ka kwantar da hankalinka kaji? Everything will be successful insha Allah"

"To Abba" yafaɗa yamike.

Bin bayanshi yayi dakallo tun yana yaro haka yake cikin tsaro saboda gudun kada yafaɗa cikin matsala sun barshi da jimawa amma yanzu sun dawo suna farautarshi gadan gadan? Yarima Junayd Allah ya tsaremin kai ya bani ikon rike wannan sirrin a zuciyata, kada ka fahimci komai sai abinda na faɗa maka, waya yaciro daga cikin wani kwali ya danna calla, Kira ɗaya aka ɗaga yace "lokaci yayi kowa ya shirya"
Kashe wayan yayi ya maida cikin kwalin, tabbas lokaci Yayi.

2:4pm

Sun dawo daga school tana sauri tashiga ciki domin cikinta yana murɗata tun a school ɗin, tasan Period ne shiyasa take sauri ta isa ɗaki ta shirya kanta, ke?

"Dole kice nayi hakuri kinsan nawane kuɗin carpet ɗinnan? To ko garken shanun Ubanki aka siyar da kuma ruganku gaba ɗaya bazai siyi wannan ba saboda haka kafin na fito inga kin maidamin palour na yadda kika yake ko wari kaɗan banson ji"
Tashi tayi tabar wurin, Aneesa kuma cikinta yana murɗawa sosai dama haka yake mata, ɗankwalin kanta ta cire tana goge wurin dashi, saida ta gama gogewa ta ɗaga carpet ɗin tana ganin yadda ya ɓaci da mai, tsaki taja kaɗan, ta mike ta ɗau mopper tafara gogewa ganin daɗa ɓaci ma yake yasa ta zauna a wurin tama rasa abinyi ga cikinta yana ciwo sosai.

Dama idan yana murɗa mata ciki baya zuwa da wuri sai can Anjima sai yazo, kwanciya tayi akan carpet ɗin tafara bacci, mopper a gefenta, bacci take sosai tasa hannu ta dafe cikinta dayake murɗa mata.

Sallama yayi yashigo, ajiye rigan yayi domin daga kan aiki yafito, yanzu ma jiyayi ya gaji shiyasa yadawo domin ya hutu a garden ɗinshi, ganin mutum a kwance kan carpet ga mai ya zube a wurin ga ɗakin yana warin petir, ya kalleta da kyau daga gashin kanta yagane itace, wannan yarinyar meyasa duk wurin ɓarna itace a gaba? Charger ya ɗauko wani baƙi a gefe yazo wurinta, watsa mata yayi a jiki ta tashi tana wani irin ihu, domin ba karamin zafi taji ba.

Wanka yayi itace ta bashi kayan da zaisa, ita ba son haihuwa take ba shiyasa wannan dabaran yayi mata daɗi.

Yashiga Part ɗin Aneesa da niyyan yau koda karfi saiya yi, tana kwance suna waya da Fadwa taga mutum a kanta ya rike Waist yana kallonta, kashe wayar tayi ta kalleshi lafiya malam?

Baiyi magana ba bai bar kallonta ba, tashi tayi dan gaba ɗaya ta tsargu, takara cewa "lafiya?"
Janyota yayi jikinshi ya matseta da karfi a kunnenta yace "ke ai matata ce to nazo karɓan hakƙina"

Tureshi tayi da iya karfin da Allah yabata tace "ka sakeni banso ɗan iska kawai"

Kin sakinta yayi tafara marinshi tana dukanshi tako ina, riketa yayi gam yace "Ko me zakiyi yau saina yi"

Junayd kai mugu ne bakada tausayi, kwantar da ita yayi akan bed ɗin, ya ɗau Veil nata ya rufe bakinta dashi, tana ihu tana kakkare jikinta domin yafara cire kayan dayake jikinta, ihun baya fita dan ya rufe bakinta, saida ya rabata da Duk kayan jikinta kafin taja hannunta da kyar ta janye Veil ɗin tana ihu, rigan jikinta ganin baizai fita ba ya yayyaga rokonshi tafara tana kuka ganin ya cire kayan jikinshi duka, wutan ɗakin ya kashe jin yadda take ihu tana rokonshi ya haɗe bakinshi da nata yafara tsotsa, fizge kanta tafara tana harba kafafunta sama, saida ya danneta yafara shiga jikinta da mugunta, jin yakasa shiga yasa iya karfinshi ya shiga jikinta, wani irin malalacin ihu tayi, Junayd kasa gane kanshi yayi yana rasa awace duniya yake, shima so yake yayi ihun amma yakasa, a hankali ya cire bakinshi daga nata yana wani irin nishi me wuyar fassarawa, Ruma tana ɗaki takasa zaune takasa tsaye, itace ta amince ayi hakan gashi yanzu ji take kamar taje ta shaƙe Aneesa.
Watsi ta fara da kayan dayake gaban mirror tanajin karan Aneesan kamar a kunnenta takeyi.

Ya manta itaɗin yarinya ce, saida yayi kusan 3hiurs akanta kafin ya sauka yana jin jikinshi yayi zafi, ganin bata motsi kamar gawa ya ɗagata sama sai Toilet, ruwan zafi ya haɗa ya tsomata ciki kafin ta buɗe ido tana kara kwalla wani uban kara, fita yayi ya barta a cikin bathtub ɗin, tana kuka kamar ranta zai fita, Babu abinda take faɗa sai Allah ya isa.

Ɗakinshi yashiga yayi wanka ya kwanta akan Bed yanajin jikinshi Yana zafi, Blanket ya rufa jikinshi dashi a hankali bacci yafara ɗaukanshi.

Kuka take har tasamu ta gama wankan, a hankali ta fito daga cikin Toilet ɗin batako shafa mai bata janye Bedsheet ɗin daya ɓaci da blood, takai toilet, a hankali ta kwanta akan bed bayan tasa wani riga mara nauyi, baccin wahala da raɗaɗi ne ya ɗauketa.

Ruma ganin har yanzu bai fito ba, ta ɗau kwalban turare ta fasa, tsaga jikinta tayi saida jini ya zuba kafin taji ranta yaɗanyi sanyi.
Itace ta jawa kanta datayi ta zubar da ciki yau gashi saide tayi surgery da cikin wata yadawo nata.
Daɗin abin ma yarima baison yarinyar.


*Washe Gari*

Ta gagara tashi tana kwance takasa koda buɗe ido ne, bakinta sai rawa yake, Ibtisam data shirya zataje school tana jiran Aneesa ta fito taji shiru, ɗakin Aneesa taje da niyan kiranta du tafi, ganin bata palour tashiga Bedroom da sallama, Aneesa na kwance sai miko mata hannu take, da gudu ta haura gadon tana tambayarta meya faru?

"Ki kiramin Ammi"
Da sauri Ibtee ta sauka taje ɗakin Ammi ta kirata, cikin tashin hankali Ammi tazo, ganin Aneesa a kwance bata ko iya magana tagane abinda ya faru, amma abin mamaki shine ina Junayd ɗin? To kodai kunya ne yasa tafita bayaso su haɗa ido da ita?

Kallon Ibtisam tayi tace "ki tafi school kada kuyi latti ita batajin daɗi"

"Ammi meya sameta?"

"Babu komai kawai zazzaɓi ne zan kula da ita jeki".

Fita tayi, Ammi ta ɗagata da taimakon ta ta kaita Toilet, Saida ta haɗa ruwan zafi sosai kafin ta sata ciki, sai rike hannun Ammi take tana cizan Lips dan wani azaba datakeji.

Hakuri da lallashi Ammi takeyi mata har saida ta gama yimata wanka, da taimakonta tafitar da ita zuwa kan gado ta bata mai tashafa, magani ta bata na kashe gajiya tasha daganan bacci ya ɗauketa.

Fita Ammi tayi tamata girki haɗe da ferfesun kayan ciki ta kawo mata, Ruma da sassafe tafita a gidan dan batason ganin kayan bakin ciki.

Shima wanka yayi da safe ya shirya cikin kayan doctor yafita a gidan.

Aneesa bayan ta farka ta rinƙa kuka, saida Ammi ta lallaɓata kafin tayi shiru, ta bata abinci taci, A zuciyarta babu abinda takeyi sai Allah isa.

 *Chapter 38*


                  ~Haka tayi jinyan kanta itada Ammi, Tun ranan da bin yafaru bai kara shigowa ɗakinta ba har yau, itama bata fita saita tabbata shida Ruma sun fita.

Ruma tayi graduation na gaba school ɗinta yanzu Burinta ta fara zuwa aiki, kuma Abban Junayd ya nema mata saide suna jiran Governo yayi sign kawai.

Hankalinta a kwance domin tana ganin tsanar Aneesa a fuskan Junayd kuma burinta zai cika da Yaddan Allah.

Junayd yana zuwa Asibitinshi yana kula da marasa lafiya yana taimako sosai, shida Asad, Surayya yanzu kam ta waye tasan kan garin komai ta sani da taimakon matar da Asad ya aiko tana koya mata, wacce take tsohuwa ce tasan komai.

Aneesa bayan ta warke ta fita a harkan su tazama shiru shiru bata yawan magana.

Yanzu Junayd baya samun matsala daga fitan dayake domin babu masu binshi.

Yau yakama ranar Monday bayan Aneesa ta dawo daga school ta ganshi yadawo ɗaukan abu a gida,
Ido ya zuba mata yana nazarinta gaba ɗaya ta sauya tunda tazo gidan tazama shiru shiru, tausayi tabashi amma ya lura yarinyar akwai raini shiyasa baya kulata, tana tafiya tana waiwaye saboda kada yayi yunkurin taɓata, ganin zata faɗi yazo da gudu ya riketa, kwace jikinta tayi tace "banso kada ka taɓani dan Allah" sakinta yayi yana kallonta ta juya ta tafi tana sharan hawaye.

Shiri tayi zataje gidan Adda Surayya, Shadda tasa maroon da adon baki a jiki, fita tayi zataje ɗakin Ammi taga Umman Muneer na tsaye tana kallonta, murmushi tayi tace "Umma? Ina wuni"

"Lafiya lau Aneesa ya kike? Ina zuwa haka?"

"Zanje gidan Adda Surayya"

"Allah sarki Aneesa ki kula da yayar taki kinji? Sannan kisa ido sosai akan makiyanki Kinsan gidan sarauta akwai tarin makiya kuma komai zai iya faruwa dana kusa dakai sanadiyyan gidan sarauta, sannan kinga shi Yarima yanada makiya sosai zasu iya shafan kowa da kowa na kusa dake, ki kula kinji ƴata?"

"Tom Umma"
Bata kawo komai a ranta ba tashiga ɗakin Ammi tayi mata sallama, fita tayi taga Security biyu sunabin bayanta, itafa ta tsani wannan abin nan da gidan Adda Surayya shine wanann masu bakaken kayan zasu bita, bata musu magana ba amma ta ɓata rai tana tafiya.

Da motarshi ya fito yana tuki a hankali yana tunani, ganin yadda take tafiya yasa yayi kamar zai bugeta ihu tayi ta koma gefe tana waro ido, sauke glass yayi yana aika mata harara.
Turo Baki tayi Alaman Allah ya isa.

Daga glass nashi yayi yafara tafiya yana kallonta ta cikin madubi, she's Beautiful, da sauri ya kawar da zancen ya kunna waƙa yana saurare.

Tana isa gidan Adda Surayya ta sameta a zaune suna karatu itada matan, zama tayi a gefe sukayi tare, saida suka gama ta gaidasu, matar ta tafi.

"A,a babu komai Adda, kawai dai inaso muyi waya dasu Baba tun jiya mafarkinsu nake"

"Tom" waya ta janyo tana neman layin Hamma Umar, kusan sau uku kafin ya ɗaga tasa a handfree tana gaisheshi.

Yana cikin tashin hankali yace "Surayya? Kada ki gayawa Aneesa wasu ƴan ta'adda sun shigo garinnan sunata kisa, kuma sun kashe Mama Baba ma bansan inda yake ba"

Jikin Aneesa yafara ɓari Surayya cikin tashin hankali tace "nashiga uku, mun shiga Uku"
Kashe wayan yayi tana kiran Sunanshi, juyawa tayi tana kallon Aneesa, A sume ta ganta bata ko numfashi, wani irin ihu Surayya tayi sannan tafita a ɗakin tana aza hannu aka, kiran Fadwa tayi itama a kiɗime tazo tana cewa "meya faru Unty?"

"Ki kiramin Asad"
Waya ta ɗaga takira Asad tace yadawo gida ba lafiya.

Yana Office ɗin Junayd time ɗin da suka kira, baisan lokacin daya mike yana shirin fita ba, Junayd yace "lafiya?"
"Akwai matsala a gida"

"To muje mana"

"A,a ka zauna zanje yanzu"
"No bazan iya zama ba ai"

Fita sukayi atare suka ɗau hanya.

Suna shiga gida sukaga Fadwa tana fifita Surayya wacce take kwance idanunta a juye, da gudu Asad yaje wurin yana tabata, meya sameta?

"Yaya Wai ƴan ta'adda ne suka shiga Garinsu sukayi kisa kuma harda Mamansu Babansu kuma basu ganshi ba"

Kallon inda Aneesa take kwance Junayd yayi da sauri ya karaso yaga itama ta suma, ruwa ya ɗibo ya shafa mata a fuska, a hankali ta buɗe ido tana cewa "ina Mama?"
Da sauri yace "bari nakira waya"

Wayarshi yakira Umar, ɗagawa yayi yace "ya dai? Meke faruwa?"

"Junayd Sun kashe Mama da Baba yqnzu Naga gawan Baba Kuma mutane sun watse a garin, farkon wanda suka fara shiga gidansu shine mu, da alama domin Baba sukazo garin"
Aneesa bai karasa ba takara kwanciya akasa a sume, ɗagata yayi hankalinshi a tashe ya ɗaurata a kafaɗa yafita da ita, a mota ya sata bai tsaya jiran su Asad ba.

Hospital nashi ya kaita, mutane suna kallon yadda ya daga mace yana tafiya da ita, special Room ya kwantar da ita yafara gwaje gwaje,saida ya gwadata me kyau, ya ɗibo ruwa ya shafa mata a fuska, allurai yayi acikin ruwan sannan ya ɗibo ruwa a karamar Bowl da karamin Towel yazo ya zauna kusa da ita yana matsa goshinta da Towel ɗin, a hankali tafara buɗe ido tana haɗa ido dashi hawaye suka fara kwararo mata bakinta ta buɗe a hankali tana magana, cikin tausayi yakai kunnenshi domin jin abinda take faɗa.

Ji yayi tace "Baba bashida Abokin gaba, ƴan ta'adda basu taɓa zuwa garinmu ba, kaine ka kaisu domin baka sona kaine wallahi"
Wani irin sambatu yarinyar nan takeyi? Taɓa goshinta yayi yaji da zafi, da Alama zazzaɓi ne yasata wannan surutun.

Kiran waya yayi a gida ya sanarwa Abbas abinda yake faruwa, Abba dayake zaune saida ya mike yace "what? Ƴan ta'adda?"

"Eh Abba kuma sun kashe kowa"

Kashe wayan yayi, yakira Ammi, tana zuwa tace "lafiya?"

"Maryam abinda muke gudu ya faru, sunje kauyen su Aneesa sun kashe mata iyaye, maryam sun kashe kowa"
Ammi saida ta zauna dan ji tayi wani jiri ya kadata kasa.
"Innalillahi wa inna ilaihiraji'un"
Shima Abba sai Innalillahi yake faɗa, Umman Muneer tashigo tana Tambayan meya faru? Abba yace "ƴan ta'adda sunje kauyen su Aneesa sunyi kisa basu bar kowa ba"

Junayd dayake zaune a gefenta gaba ɗaya jikinshi yayi sanyi, sai aikin shafa mata ruwa yake a goshi.
Temperature ɗinta yayi high.

Surayya bayan ta farfaɗo babu abinda takeyi sai kuka, Asad yana bata hakuri, tace Ina Aneesa.

"Junayd ya tafi da ita Hospital"
"Ku kaini wurinta"

"No ki zauna anan zuwanki zaisa ki tada hankalinki"

Kwanciya tayi a jikinshi tana kuka sosai.

Ruma har kusan dare bataga Junayd ba kuma ta lura Aneesa bata nan, hankalinta ne ya tashi wato Junayd zaici amananta? Ɗakin Ammi taje duk da ta lura bata hayyacinta tace "Ammi bakiji labarin Junayd ba? Naga yau bai dawo da wuri ba".

"Bazai dawo ba yana tare da Aneesa a Hospital nashi domin batada lafiya"
Tashi Ammi tayi tashiga ciki dan batason magana a halin yanzu.

"What? Hospital? Da wannan yarinyar? Lalle Junayd I will teach you a lesson for life, Ni Zakayi Betraying?"
Tana surutu tana tafiya, motarta tashiga batareda ta yiwa wani Magana a cikin gidan ba.

Fita tayi da mugun gudu bata tsaya ko inaba sai Hospital, parking tayi tafito tana gyara karamin mayafin dayake kanta, saida ta isa cikin Office ɗinshi taga baya nan, a zuciye ta fita, Dr Bobby ya ganta yace "barka"

"Yawwa Barka ina Yarima?"
Nuna mata ɗakin dayake, tashiga ta buɗe da karfi, Aneesa kwance akan Bed na marasa lafiya hannunta ansa ruwa da kanula, shikuma Junayd ya kwantar da kanshi akan cikinta yana bacci da alama baccin ya ɗaukeshi bada saninshi ba"

Da wani zafin nama ta tureshi, firgigit yayi yana rike Aneesa saboda kada ta faɗi, hawayene yafara bin kuncin Ruma wato har kulawa na musamman yake bata, baki ta buɗe cikin kuka zata fara magana ya riko hannunta yace "shiiiiiii"
"Ban gane shiii ba me kake nufi?"

Janta yayi zuwa waje yace "kada kiyi magana da karfi zata iya tashi kuma da kyar nasamu tayi bacci"
Tureshi tayi da karfi tana kuka tace "betrayer, wato kada ta tashi daga bacci ko? To bari ka gani"

Shiga ɗakin tayi ta janye ruwan dayake hannun Aneesan ta yadda ledan, a firgice Aneesa ta tashi jin wani irin zafi daya ziyarci jikinta.

Hannun Ruma ya rike da karfi ya kikkifa mata mari, jajayen Lips nashi dayake yawan tsotsa ya ciza da karfi yanuna mata hanyan waje yace "Out"
"Bazan fita ba Junayd itaɗin a matsayin wacece da zakamin wulakanci a kanta?"

Cikin zafin rai yace "a matsayin matata"

Hannu Ruma ta ɗaura akai ta tsaka wani uban ihu tace "Matarka? Ya mukayi dakai?"
"Ruma ki fita ki daina ihu akan Yarinyar nan"
Kukan kura tayi ta cafko wuyan Aneesa ta shake kamar zata kasheta, sai kakarin amai Aneesa take tana waro ido.

Da karfi ya ture Ruma saida ta buga kanta da bango, jini yafara zuba, hannu tasa ta taɓa goshinta ganin jini ta juya tana kallon Junayd, ya rike Aneesa yana maida ruwan, tana kuka yasa hannu yana share mata hawayen tareda janyota jikinshi yana bubbuga bayanta.

"Ai ba haka ya kamata kayi ba, bawai buga kaina sau ɗaya ya kamata kayi ba, kasan sau nawa ya dace? Kalli kaga"
Riko kanta tayi tafara haɗawa da jikin bango da iya karfin da Allah ya bata, jikin bangon dayake ɗauke da fenti fari a take ya sauya kala ya koma jajur jininta ya ɓata, ganin zata iya kashe kanta Aneesa ta tureshi tace "ka sakeni mugu kada ka kara taɓani kaine sanadiyyan mutuwan iyayena kuma bazan yafe maka ba"
Cire ruwan tayi taje wurin Ruma tana hanta, Ruma tayiwa kanta illa jiri ne da ciwon kai suka kadata kasa, Aneesa tana kuka ta ɗagata da kyar ta daurata akan ɗayan Bed na marasa lafiya sannan ta koma nata ta kwanta dan itama ba daɗi takeji ba kuma batada karfin tsayuwa"

Maganganun Aneesa sunyi tasiri a ranshi baiji daɗi ba, ta yaya zaiyi sanadiyan mutuwan iyayenta? Kuma sune wanda suka taimakeshi har yafara buɗe baki yayi magana, gashi tahaɗa kai da gwiwa tanata kuka, shine ma abinda yake kara ɗaga mishi hankali kuma taki bari ya taɓa jikinta.
Ruma na kwance batasan inda take ba domin ba karamin buga kanta tayi ba.

A hankali yaje gaban Aneesa ya zauna, da karfi ta tureshi amma ko gezau baiyi na, ta taɓe bakinta tana kuka sosai tace "bazan yafe maka ba, da farko nayi zaton tsanan dakayimin kaɗanne sai yanzu nagane tsanan gaskiya kayimin, yanzu ma kana zuwa wurina ne kana nunamin kulawa saboda kasamu ka cire cikin dayake jikina wanda kayimin shi ta karfi da yaji kasa a jikin matarka ko? To bari kaji na gaya maka Ni Aneesaa yarinya ce Amma ba sokuwa ba, inada wayo na, bazan taɓa haɗa jini da kai ba, cikin jikina saina zubar dashi kaima ka ɗanɗana abinda na ɗana a yau bayan jin mutuwar iyayena, Allah baiyi zaka samu yaro ba a duniya indai ta karkashina zaka samu, nayi rantsuwa da Allah koda a jikin wata ne takeda cikinka saina zubar.

Jijiyoyin jikinshi a take suka mike kanshi yaɗau zafi, idanunshi suka firfito sukayi jajur, bakinshi yakara zama Red sosai, zufa yafara keto mishi, baiyi zaton Aneesa tasan shirin dayake ba, kallonshi tayi tace "ya dai? Ka tsorata ko? Kaji tsoro danace zan zubar da cikin ko? To ba dagaske nake ba ka kwantar da hankalinka bazan zubar ba, yawwa yarima na"

Gangar jikinta yana nuna irin ɓacin ran datake ciki tace "bazan zubar yanzu ba saina bari yafito a cikin jikina sannan nasa wuka na daddatsa shi kuma na yayyanka a gabanka, ina nufin a cikin cikina kanaji kana gani sai nabari cikin yafara girma kafin nasha maganin da zai maidashi pieces, ya tarwatse Koda ko nima zan tarwatse ne"

Kunnuwanshi bazasu iya ɗaukan wannan maganan ba, matsowa yayi kusa da ita yana shirin janyota jikinshi dan yayi zaton ta fita a hayyacinta ne, da karfi tace "Don't dare touch me"

Cakk ya tsaya yana kallon Aneesa bakinshi yakasa buɗuwa balle yayi magana bai taɓa zaton zaiji wannan maganan daga bakin Aneesa ba, kallon Ruma datake kwance yayi, a hankali ya mike yaje wurinta ya ɗau allura zaiyi mata, da karfi ta fizge alluran tafara caccakawa jikinta, ranta ya ɓaci bazata iya jure ganin Junayd da wata ba.
Kwatan Alluran yafara saida hannunshi yaji ciwo kafin yasamu ya kwace, komawa yayi gefe ya zauna a kasa yana kallonsu.

Meyasa yazama yarima? Meyasa?inama yau dashi talaka ne da baiji wannan tashin hankalin ba, tunawa yake da maganan da Aneesa ta faɗa mishi, Allah baiyi zaka haihu ba, kanshi tafasa yake idan ya tuna da kalamanta, meyasa ta ɗaura mishi alhakin kisan iyayenta?
Bashida amsa saide ya tambayeta.

Aneesa da bacci yafara ɗaukanta, da wani ihu ta buɗe idonta ganin gawan su Mama da Baba datayi, fizge fizge tafara akan Bed ɗin tana shiri saukowa kasa, da gudu yaje ya tareta, kwace kanta take tana tureshi, wani allura ya janyo ya danneta da kyar yasamu yayi mata, a hankali tafara rufe idanunta tana komawa, gashin kanta ya kwance daga kitso biyu datayi mishi, ya bazu ya rufe mata fuska, ga fuskan yayi zufa sosai kuma yayi jaa, idan ka ganta zaka rantse mahaukaciya ce.

 *Chapter 41*


                  ~A hankali ya mike yazo gabanta yana shirin ɗagata, tureshi tayi da karfi, da ihu tace "kada ka kuskura ka taɓani i hate you, I Hate you Junayd"

To kayi Hakuri mijina"
Cikin idonshi ta kalla tana huci tace "a haka zan rinƙa ɗanɗana maka bakin ciki saika fara jin daɗi kafin na katse maka, mugu azzalumi"

Tashi yayi yabar mata ɗakin, bai tsaya ko inaba sai cikin Fada, ko sallama baiyi ba yasamu Ammi da Abba suna tsaye da Alama Ammi masifa take, tana ganinshi ta canja magana tana kokarin ɓoye faɗan da sukeyi, ya durkusa kan gwiwanshi ya haɗa hannu biyu ya ɗaga sama Alaman rokonsu zaiyi, Safwan dayake jikin kofa yana kallonshi shima ji yayi kamar yayiwa Junayd kuka.

A wurin ya kwana cikin sanyin Tiles, bacci me cike da wahala yakeyi domin kukan yasashi ciwon kai ba kaɗan ba.

Firgigit ya tashi yana salati, kallon gefenshi yayi baiga kowa ba, wani irin tsoro yaji dan akwai duhu a ɗakin, da sauri ya fita zuwa kofan ɗakin ya kwanta inda zai iya jiyo sautin mutane daga cikin gida, a wurin ya karasa baccin da bai gama ba, yanada tsoro sosai shiyasa yakasa bacci a ɗakin.

Saida tayi salla ta kwanta akan sallayan bacci ya saceta tana cikin tunani, mafarki tayi wai Mama da Baba su rike hannunta sukace Aneesa zamu jefaki wani wuri duk wanda ya karɓeki ki rikeshi hannu biyu, tana cewa A,a mama ku bari, saida suka jefita wurin wani mutum wanda yake rufe da fuskanshi tasa hannu zata janye abin fuskan saita tashi, salati tayi tana kallon gefenta ganin ba kowa ta karanta auzubillahi minashaiɗanirrajim sau uku ta tofa a gefenta na hagu sannan ta canja wurin kwanciya tafara bacci.

Ɓangaren Ammi itama dakyar tasamu ta runtsa a ranan domin tunanin halinda Junayd zai shiga take, duk da ya nuna bai wani damu ba, tasan dole abin ya dameshi idan ya zauna, Allah dai yasa Aneesa ta bashi kulawa ta lallasheshi Ameen

 *Chapter 39*


                  ~Ammi ce ta kirashi yana ɗagawa a hankali yayi magana, jin muryanshi da sanyi tace "ya jikin Aneesa?"
Cikin dauriya yace "da sauki"
Ina take?
Wani ɗan Marayan kuka ya fashe dashi, Ammi datake jinshi a waya taji hankalinta ya kuma tashi, dama dauriya kawai takeyi, "meya faru Junayd? Wani abin ne yasamu Aneesa?"

"A,a Ammi tausayi take bani ga Ruma ma tazo tana yiwa kanta rauni"

"Duka suna tare dakai?"

"Eh muna nan Hospital"
Kashe wayan tayi ta ɗauko hijabi me zanen alkyabba tasa, Waya takira tace "a shirya mata tafiya yanzu zata fita"
Kafin ta fito an shirya komai harda security dazasu rakata, Safwan yaso ya bita tace "a,a yabari sai gobe"
Wani jeep Baki tashiga Driver yajata sauran motocin sukabi bayanta, kusan 10 na dare shiyasa suke gudu a titin.

Suna isa Hospital ɗin tasan ɗakin da ake kwantar da relatives na gidan sarki, shiga tayi kai tsaye, yana ganinta yaje da sauri ya Rungumeta yana kuka, shafa suman kanshi tayi tace "Calm Down Dear"
A hankali ya sauke ajiyan zuciya yace "Ammi Aneesa"
Taji daɗi daya damu da Aneesan, cireshi tayi a jikinta taje wurin Aneesan tana taɓata, ganin tana bacci yasa ta koma wurin Ruma, idonta biyu tayi kamar tana bacci, tayiwa jikinta rauni shiyasa Ammi taji tausayinta tasani akwai kishi mesa Hauka Amma na Ruma ya wuce misali, tace "Junayd kawo firstaidbox kayi Dressing ɗin ciwonta"
Babu musu yaje ya ɗauko yazo ya wanke ciwon ya manna bandage, Tasha paracetamol me karfi sannan Ammi ta riketa sutafi gida, bin Ammi tayi har suka shiga Mota batayi magana ba, Ammi ta dawo tace Junayd ya kula da Aneesa sai gobe zasuzo, Amsawa yayi tace "Good night take care"

Kwanciya yayi a gefen Aneesa wacce take bacci, Kallon Yadda Lips nata ya fashe yayi jaa, ga fuskarta ta kumbura, kyawawan idanunta a rufe eyelashes ɗin sun kwanta akansu, gyara mata gashin daya zubo a goshinta yayi da yatsanshi guda ɗaya, tausayi take bashi tunda ta rasa iyayenta, tunawa yayi da yadda ake cemata Aneesan Baba da alama sun saba da Baba sosai, gashi acan ma sun shagwaɓata komai takeso anayi mata a gidansu, saide shikam bai rike musu alkawari ba yazo yanata wulakanta yarinya, gata karama bata wani gama sanin komai ba, dogon hancinta ya kalla yadda yayi wani Red dashi, tanada kyau sosai babu ma haɗinta da Ruma, saide magananta ke bashi tsoro, shin dagaske tanada cikin? Kodai ta faɗane dan ranshi ya ɓaci? A hankali ya janyota ya rungume yanajin wani sanyin daɗi yana shiga jikinshi, insha Allahu zan kula da ita albarkacin iyayenta, bazan bari kiyi kuka ba, zan kuka dake duk da ba sonki nake ba.
Bakinshi yakai kan goshinta yayi kissing, lumshe ido yayi yanajin bacci na shirin ɗaukanshi.

Asad sai gwada numer ɗin Umar yake amma baya tafiya, tunda yafaɗa musu yaga gawan Baba har yanzu basu sameshi a waya ba, sannan a rahotanni ance basu bar kowa a garin da rai ba, kuma har yanzu ba'a gano menene abinda ya kaisu garin ba, Surayya babu abinda takeyi sai kuka yadda sukaga rana haka sukaga dare.

Ammi ma ɓangarenta batayi bacci ba ko kaɗan, tsoron rayuwar da Junayd zai shiga takeyi sosai, tana tsoron kada wani mummunan abun ya faru dashi, saide akwai Allah komai zaizo da sauki.

Yarima cikin dare Aneesa ta rinƙa farkawa tana fizge fizge, da kyar yasamu ya riketa tayi bacci, yadda yaga rama shima haka yaga dare.


*Washe Gari*

Safwan da Ammi da kuma Ibtisam harda Muneer da Abba suka shirya duka sukaje Asibiti domin duba Aneesa, tana zaune abakin gadon tayi tagumi hawaye yanabin kuncinta kamar a mafarki take tuna wai babu mama kuma babu Baba?
A hankali ya tura kofar ɗakin Yashigo idanunshi sun ɗan kumbura Alaman bai samu bacci ba jiya, kallo ɗaya tayi mishi ta watsar tana cigaba da kukanta, Cup ɗin Tea ne a hannunshi Yana fitar da tururi, wurinta yazo ya mika mata Cup ɗin, hannu tasa kamar zata karɓa ta buge ya zube akan hannunshi, wani irin raɗaɗin zafine ya ziyarci Junayd, hannun Atake ya koma jaa yana shirin ɗayewa, kallon yadda ya runtse idanu tayi, tun jiya sai yau tayi murmushi tace "kaji zafi ne? To haka nakeji a zuciyata a duk lokacin dana buɗe idanuna na ganka, ji nake kamar na tsiyayar da ruwan idanuna domin na daina ganin fuskar my Parent murderer"

Shiru yayi duk masifanshi yau yakasa tankawa mata, kallon Cup ɗin yayi yadda ya tarwatse a kasa, ɗibe glass ɗin yayi da hannunshi saida yagama yafita ya zubar, sai kallonshi ake a Hospital din Domin abinda bai taɓayi ba kenan ya karɓo Tea da kanshi saide akai mishi.

Yana dawowa ya zauna a gabanta yana janyo ruwan allura acikin sirinji, harara take aika mishi har yanzu hawaye bai daina bin fuskarta ba, a hankali ya mike yazo gabanta zai riko hannunta domin yi mata allura, Safwan ne ya buɗe kofa da wani irin gudu ta tashi taje ta faɗa jikinshi ta ƙankameshi tana kuka, hannu yasa yana shafa kanta tareda bata hakuri, Tsayawa yayi da alluran a hannunshi yakasa koda motsi,  ganin yadda ta kwanta ajikin Safwan tana kuka yakara bashi mamaki, Saf kallonshi yayi yadda ya faɗa gashi kuma idanunshi sunyi Red da alama bacci ne baiyi ba, ajiye alluran yayi ya raɓa ta gefensu har alokacin tana jikinshi, fita yayi sukaci karo da Ammi, tace "ina zuwa?"
Sosa kai yayi yanajin ranshi babu daɗi cikin in Ina yace "zanje na zanje nayi.."
Riko hannunshi Ammi tayi tace "muje ciki" da hijabi a jikinta irin me daurewa da igiya ɗinnan, Su Ibtisam da mai martaba da Muneer suma suka shigo, Babban darduma ya shimfiɗa musu suka zauna akai, Gaida Aneesa sukayi tareda yimata ya hakuri, a hankali tace "Alhamdulillah"

Da sauri yace "Abba dawa zanyi kishin?"

"Da Kaninka Mana"

"A,a Abba kawai de.."

"Kawai de me? Gashi kishi ya bayyana ƙarara a fuskarka"
Shi kanshi baisan me yake ba, yadai san yanajin raɗaɗin abinda ta faɗa mishi ne amma ai bazaiyi kishi da Safwan ba, dukda yaji haushin abinda tayi a gabanshi.

Abba ya karaso ciki ya dafa kafaɗarshi yace "ita mace tanada saukin zuciya da wuri ake sace zuciyarta, kayi kokari ka janyo matarka jiki ka nuna mata kulawa na tabbata bazataso kowa ba sai kai"
Yana gama.faɗa mishi haka ya fita.

Zama yayi akan kujera yana jujjuyawa yana kallon Slin ɗin Office ɗin, Junayd meke damunka? Ya kamata ka saita kanka, kasani tausayinta kakeji.
Saida ya gama magana da zuciyarshi kafin yatashi yakoma cikin ɗakin, lokacin Surayya da Asad sunzo, sai kuka suke itada kanwarta Abba da Ammi suna aikin bata hakuri.

Tsayawa yayi a jikin kofa, Asad yazo ya janye Surayya dan ya lura basuda niyyan daina kukan, Ganin haka tafaɗa jikin Safwan dayake zaune a gefenta tana kuka sosai, "sorry" yake faɗa yana shafa kanta, ina Junayd ya kasa tsayawa ya kalla, kara buɗe kofan yayi yafita, jingina yayi da jikin kofan yanajin wani zafi a ranshi.

Ammi ta lura da hakan amma bata wani damu ba, Aneesa tafi sabawa da Safwan kuma tunda a gaban kowane suke hakan babu matsala ai, idan anyi magana ne zasu fara tunanin kodai zargisu take shiyasa tayi shiru.

Muneer na gefe yana danna waya duk abinda sukeyi yana recording a kanshi, duk yana kallonsu ta gefen ido.
Fadwa ma tana zaune tayi shiru tana sharan kwalla domin Aneesa sun bata tausayi sosai.

                  ~kashe wayanshi yayi gaba ɗaya yashiga yayi alwala yazo yana salla yana rokon Allah ya kareshi daga sharrin masu sharri, sannan ya wankeshi a wurin Aneesa ta gane cewar bashida laifi ko kaɗan, akan sallayan ya kwanta, yana tuna yadda ta tureshi ɗazu, shifa dama ba sonta yake ba tausayi kawai take bashi, yanzu gani take kamar yana sonta shiyasa take rainashi, da ace da ne da bata isa ta rainashi ya kyaleta ba, amma yanzu dan ankashe mata iyaye shiyasa yake ɗaga mata kafa.

Aneesa ba abinda yake bata haushi kamar fyaɗen dayayi mata, Eh mana fyaɗe tunda bada sonta ba, kuma da iya karfin da Allah yabashi yayi mata ya zalunceta yaci amanan iyayenta itada Mama tace tunda ta fara Period kada tabari tana raɓan maza shine yayi mata wannan muguntar? Ai da Mama tana raye da sai taci masa mutunci.
 

   *Washe gari*

Yau ta kuduri niyyan zuwa school, shiri tayi cikin uniform, a kasa ta zauna tasha ruwan gora kawai, dama ba wani yunwa takeji ba, biscuit da chocolate tasa acikin jakanta, Hijabinta dayake fari guntu tasa, bayan yaɗan ɗago domin ta kame gashinta wuri ɗaya, takalminta sneeker tasa sannan ta rataya jakan a bayanta tafito tana jan kofan, tayi kyau saide ta ɗan rame, lokacin shima ya fito da shiri alama Hospital zaije, kallo ɗaya tayi mishi ta ɗauke kai, Yanada kyau shiyasa yakeda raini, tafaɗa a ranta.

Kallonta yake yadda uniform ɗin ya karɓeta gashi ta kara girma jikinta yakara kyau, shagala yayi da kallonta saida tazo ta wuce kafin ya dawo hayyacinshi, Kafin ya fita saida ya kalli ɗakin Ruma yanaji kamar bata mutu ba, ji yake inama ta dawo koda bazata rinka jin maganarshi ba, koba komai yana ganinta zaiji sanyi, baiji daɗi ba da Ruma ta tafi ta barshi da wuri haka, ɗauke tunanin yayi yana ɗan kallon gaban wayanshi, ganin misscalls daga Asad bai kira ba domin yanzu zasu haɗu a Asibiti.

Ɗakin Ammi taje suna zaune a palour duka dasu Ibtisam, itama zama tayi tana gaida Ammi, cikin son jin yadda Aneesa ta tashi Ammi ta amsa mata gaisuwan.

Kallon Yadda Ibtisam takecin abinci tayi tace "Kici a hankali bamuyi latti ba"
Ammi ta kalleta tace "ke Aneesa bazakici bane?"
"Ammi na karya yanzu acan"
"To"

Shigowa yayi hannunshi rike da makullin mota, yana ɗan girgiza hannun, a gefen Ammi ya zauna yace "Ammi good morning"
Shafa kanshi tayi ganin ya rame a kwanakin tace "Junayd meyake damunka ka rame haka?"
Kakalo murmushi yayi yace "Babu komai"
Tashi tayi tasa mishi abinci akan plate ta miko mishi, Ammi na koshi, yafaɗa yana satan kallon Aneesa wacce ta ɗauke kai kamar batasan yana wurin ba.

"A,a baka koshi ba"
Zama tayi ta ɗibo abincin tafara bashi a baki, couscous ne jallof wanda yaji kayan lambu, saida yayi rabi kafin ya ɗauke kai Alaman ya koshi.

Ajiyewa tayi ta ɗibo ruwa ta miƙa mishi, babu musu ya karɓa yasha, Aneesa ta ɗan saci kallonshi ganin yadda yake cin abinci baima damu da duk wani mutuwa da akayi ba, tashi tayi ranta a ɗan ɓace tanufi hanyan fita.

Ammi tace "dakata Aneesa zaku tafi tare da Junayd ita Ibtisam zata biyoku"
Juyawa tayi tana kallon Ammi so take tayi mata musu amma ta kasa, a hankali tayi murmushi ta jijjiga kai Alaman to.

Kallonshi Ammi tayi tace "Tashi kaje" lumshe idanu yayi yana kallon Aneesa wacce da ganin fuskanta kasan ba da sonta bane.
A hankali ya mike kafin ya fita tafita daga ɗakin, Ammi tana kallon bayanshi tace "Allah ka haɗamin kansu"
A hankali yake takawa har ya iso wurin motarshi wanda aka wanke yana sheƙi sosai, sa key yayi ya buɗe, fuska ba yabo ba fallasa tazo ta shiga gaba ta zauna tareda cire jakan dayake bayanta ta rungume ta gaba, Abba sojoji yasa suke gadinsu koda zasu fita yanzu soja ne zasuyi musu rakiya, tunda abin ya faru Abba ya karo masu tsaro kuma masu power.

Tafiya suke babu me yiwa juna magana Aneesa ta ɗauke kai tana kallon gefe shikuma Yarima ya maida kanshi akan titi yana tuki, kallonta yayi kaɗan sannan ya kara maida hankali kan titi ganin yadda ta murtuke fuska yace "Aneesan Baba"
Ji tayi kamar ta danna duk abinda tagani a cikin motar su kife gaba ɗaya su mutu, wai Aneesan Baba dama yasan itaɗin Aneesan Baba ne kuma yasa aka kashe mata Baba?

Yasan bazata amsa ba, a hankali ya ɗaura hannunshi kan lallausan hannunta ya ɗago yana murzawa, Kwace hannunta tafara, yace "Stop it ba'aso Mata tana yiwa mijinta Raini kinji?"

So take tayi mishi rashin kunya Amma ta gagara, kokarin kwace hannunta kawai takeyi, shi kuma yaki saki, da hannu ɗaya yake tuki, akai akai yana juyawa yana kallonta.

Ganin bazai saki hannunta ba tace "ka sakarmin hannu"

"No ai bazan iya ba saboda hannunki da laushi, zanso in rinka taɓawa koda yaushe"
Kuka ta fashe dashi tana yaguninshi, ko gezau baiyi ba yasan abin nata a haɗe da yarinta shiyasa yafara Binta a hankali, bai saketa ba saida suka isa school ɗinsu, har cikin haraban makarantar ya tsaya, yana sakin hannunta tafara kokarin buɗe kofa, ya rufe idan bashi ya buɗe ba bazai taɓa buɗuwa ba, jakanta dayake gabanta tasa kanta akai tafara kuka, matsowa yayi wajenta ya ɗago kanta, runtse ido tayi tana kuka sosai, yatsa ɗaya yasa yana share hawayen dayake. Sauka akan fuskanta, janye hannunshi take daga fuskanta tana cigaba da kuka.

Saida ta dakata da kukan kafin ya saketa yasa hannu a Aljihu ya ciro wani katon Chocolate yasa mata a hannu, da sauri ta yasar tace "banso"
Ɗauka yayi yasa acikin jakanta yace "daga yau nine Zan rinƙa kawoki school kinji?"

Cikin fitsara tace "saide na daina zuwa school ɗin indai kaine zakana kawoni"
Murmushi yayi yace "Okay Ai niɗin mijinki ne kinga kuma dole miji ya kula da matarshi"
Kin Kallon cikin idonshi tayi domin yana hanata yimishi rashin kunya yadda taso, "matarka? Ni ba matarka bace hasalima nafi son Safwan akanka..." Bai bari ta karasa ba ya janyota jikinshi ya riketa sosai, ka sakeni.

"Kada ki kara faɗamin wannan kalman Aneesa Dan Allah"
"Saina faɗa Nima so kake ka rinƙa kawoni school domin idan anzo nemanka ka bani kayanka ka turani su kasheni kamar yadda kayiwa Unty Ru..."
Bakinta ya haɗa da nashi yana rufe idonshi cikin zafin nama ya kamo Lips nata wanda suke faɗa mishi magana marasa daɗi ya rinƙa tsotsa kamar wanda baya hayyacinshi, bugunshi take kota ina, ganin bazai saketa ba tayi shiru tana sauke ajiyan zuciya, saida yaji ranshi yayi sanyi kafin ya buɗe motan ya ɗauke kai daga kallonta yace "fita"
Saida ta share hawayenta ta goge Lips nata kafin taɗau jakanta ta rataya, sa kafa tayi tabar mishi motan kafin ya rufe tace "Allah ya isa".

Rufe motan yayi yabar cikin school ɗin da gudu sosai, dama Sojojin suna jiranshi a waje yana fita suka bishi abaya.

Motan da ake kawo Ibtisam ne Yashigo cikin school ɗin, saida ta jirata tafito kafin tace "sai yanzu?" Tana kokari ɓoye damuwan datake ciki.

Kallon yanayinta Ibtisam tayi sannan ta tuna yanzu motar Junayd ya fita kenan tun ɗazu suna tare? Murmushi tayi na jin daɗi tace "sai yanzu ya Junayd ya tafi?"
Jijjiga kai tayi, "ummm love birds"
Shiru Aneesa tayi mata batason tana faɗan abinda yake faruwa tsakaninta da mijinta, so take kawai rana ɗaya ya saketa.
Hannunta ta riko suka shiga cikin class nasu Fadwa, tana ganinsu taje da gudu ta rungumesu, kallon Aneesa tayi tace "ya karin hakuri?"
Kasa tasa kanta tace "Alhamdulillah"

"Allah yaji kansu da Rahama"

"Ameen summa Ameen"
Zama sukayi akan Benci dama malamai basu fito ba domin yau sunyi fitan wuri, hira suka fara an daɗe ba'a gamu ba, Aneesa har ta warware tafara Hira, dama zama take cikin damuwa amma tunda Allah yasa yau tafito school gashi sun haɗu da Fadwa ai sai yadda Allah yayi.

Exam sun kusa farawa, dasun gama  kuma za'a basu hutu, idan sun dawo Aneesa zata koma Ss1 sukuma zasuje Ss3, Ammi tace idan zasu Ss3 zataje school ɗin da kanta ayiwa Aneesa tsallake domin tafara jami'a da wuri.

Saida malamai suka shigo kafin Aneesa ta koma class, yanzu sun saba da ƴan ajin, kowa yanayi mata ya hakuri, cikin sakin fuska take amsa musu da "Alhmdllh"
Zama tayi akan Kujeran data saba zama, taciro takaddu tana karantawa domin so take tayi kokari a Exam ɗin.

*YARIMA JUNAYD*

  Na
Jiddah S Mapi

 *Chapter 45*


                  ~Aneesa garkame ɗakinta tayi, shiga Toilet ɗin da aka ƙayata mata da kayan duniya komai na ciki a tsare yake, ga sabulai ga Shampoo sai Wanda ta zaɓa, cikin Toilet Amma kamar ɗaki, kallon katon Bathtub ɗin tayi a fili tace "miye amfanin wannan tunda banida iyaye yanzu? Miye amfanin kuɗin da babu kwanciyar hankali, na gommace nayi aure a kauyenmu na zauna cikin taɓo da zana da kara, na rinƙa zuwa daji ina ɗauro itace kafin nayi girki akan wannan gidan, gidan da sukeda komai na duniya kuɗi sarauta, amma bana jin daɗin ko guda ɗaya acikinsu, na tsani ma ace niɗin Gimbiya ce matar ɗan sarki, naso ace niɗin Aneesa ce matar mai sonta.
"Ya Allah ka rabani da wannan bawan naka, Allah kafin nima ya kasheni kamar yadda yayi sanadiyyan kashe matarshi, Allah kada ka haɗa jinina da nashi"
Ruwa ta tara sannan tayi wanka ta ɗaura Towel ta fito tana maida gashinta baya, drayer ta bushar da kanka dashi, sannan ta zauna akan stool tashafa mai, kallon kanta tayi, haske kam da kiɓa tayishi amma a 2days tayi rama kaɗan, kuma badan komai ba sai dan ganin fuskar wannan mutumin.

Riga mara nauyi tasa sannan ta kwanta akan Bed tana latsa ƴar karaman wayanta, so take itama ta samu waya babba tafara Chatting, abin yanayi mata daɗi yadda Fadwa da Ibtisam suke chat, ta koya tasan komai saide yanzu batada wayan da zatayi dashi.
Ajiye karaman wayar tayi bayan ya isheta, ta mike a wurin tanaso tayi bacci, lumshe ido tafara a hankali Bacci yayi awon gaba da ita.

Bai samu yadawo normal ba Saida bacci ya ɗaukeshi, hakan take faruwa dashi a kowani lokaci, awaje mutane suna ganinshi kamar wanda yake cikin kwanciyar hankali, a zuciya kuma shi kaɗai yasan me yake ciki.


****************
Rayuwa suke babu me shiga harkan wani, Yau Aneesa sunje Ss3 an kusa basu hutu dagashi sai graduation, tasa kanta a karatun tunanin Ya Umar yana damun kanta amma ba yadda ta iya Addu'a takeyi kullum Allah ya bayyana shi da sauran ƴan garin nasu.

Junayd yana aikinshi amma babu kwanciyar Hankali, a fili suna nunawa Ammi suna shiri, sai sunje Part nasu kowa yakama harkanshi.

Yau suna zaune su duka a fada Abba yanayi musu nasiha kamar yadda ya saba kowani Jumma'a, Junayd yasa jallabiya fari da rawani jaa, kyau yayi sosai yafito kamar asalin Balarabe, Aneesa kuma bakin Hijab ne a jikinta tayi Rolling kanta da bakin gyale, tanaso idan Abba ya gama saitaje gidan Adda.

Sallama akayi suka amsa duka suna kallon kofa, mamaki sukaji yadda akayi sallama a wannan lokacin, idan suna wannan zaman babu me shigowa sai ahalinsu, Kafarshi yafara sawa wanda yake cikin takalmi sahu ciki wanda aka ɗaure da igiya, kowa ya maida hankalinshi wurin, Shigowa yayi ya tsaya yana kallonsu, a firgice Abba ya tashi yana nunashi, "Kabeer?..."
Murmushi yayi yace "Eh nine" kallonshi Junayd yayi yanaso ya tuno inda ya taɓa ganin fuskar.

A hankali ya karaso gaban Junayd ya shafa fuskanshi yace "Kana tuna inda ka taɓa ganina ko? To basai kayi dogon tunani ba, nine Wanda ka taimakawa ranan da aka kaini asibitinka jikina da Bullet.

Abba yace "Kabeer meya kawowa gidannan?"

Murmushin gefen baki yayi ya haɗa hannu biyu yace "Barkanku ahalina niɗin ɗan uwanku ne"
Ya maida hankalinshi kan Abba yace "Nazo na zauna tareda mahaifina da kuma kannena"
Saf ya gane wannan shine yayan Junayd, ran Junayd a ɓace yanufo wurinshi ya shaƙe wuyanshi "Ƴan uwanka? Mahaifinka? Mahaifinka da ka daɗe da kashewa?"
Cire hannun Junayd yayi daga wuyanshi yana cigaba da murmushi, yace "na kashe kuma? To idan na kashe waye Wannan?"

Abba ya gane ba abanza Kabeer yazo ba yazone da niyyan yin wani abunda babu kyau, so yake a fallasa komai saiya samu yaɗau mulkin, a hankali ya karasa wurin Junayd wanda yake huci yana kallon Kabeer idan ya kyaleshi zai iya yiwa Kabeer ɗin illa a halin yanzu, dafa kafaɗarshi yayi "Junayd ai wannan ɗin ɗana ne shima, shine Kabeer yayanka danake baka labari shima zai iya zama tare damu"
Wani kallon mamaki ya aikawa Abba jijiyoyin kanshi sun mimmiƙe jikinshi har rawa yake, idan ya kalli Kabeer sai yaga gawan iyayenshi a cikin idanuwanshi.
Ganin zai iya rasa control ɗinshi Abba yace "Aneesa zo"
Tana tsaye tana kallon abinda yake faruwa zakasa gane komai, ga mai kama da Junayd kana ganinshi kasan sun haɗa jini amma daga gani Akwai wani abu a kasa.

Zuwa tayi tace "gani Abba"
"Tashi mamana"
A hankali ta mike kanta a kasa, yace "rike mijinki ki kaishi ɗaki, ki kwantar mishi da hankali kinji?"
Jijjiga kai tayi, tariko Junayd wanda yake huci har yanzu, idanunshi suna hawaye jikinshiyana rawa, meyasa Abba ya karɓeshi? Kuma meyasa ya hanashi ɗaukan fansa akan wannan mutumin?

Janshi tafara, idonshi yakai kan Ammi wacce take murza yatsu tana kallon kasa, Aneesa ma ta kalleta, fita tayi da Junayd a ɗakin, Ba abinda yake sai sharan hawaye, so take ta tureshi amma tausayi ya bata ganin yana kuka, ɗakinshi ta kaishi, murɗa handle ɗin tayi hannunta acikin nashi, sassayyan kamshi ne ya bugi hancinta, akan Sofa ta ajiyeshi, juyawa tayi zata tafi taji ya fashe da kuka ya ɗaura kanshi akan hannun sofan, a hankali ta juyo da gaske yake kukan, har hannayenshi suna rawa, "meya sameshi?" Tafaɗa a ranta, harta buɗe kofa zata tafi taji bazata iya barinshi a wanna halin ba, a hankali ta maida kofan ta rufe, wurin frij taje ta ciro Ruwa, wani karamin glass cup ta ɗauko ta tsiyaya ruwan sanyin aciki, wurinshi taje ta mika mishi, bai ɗago ba yana cigaba da kuka.

Kallon Gashin kanshi daya hargitsa tayi, hannu tasa akan gashin tace "tashi"
Ɗan ɗago kai yayi, fuskarshi har tayi Red, bashi ruwan tayi yaki karɓa, hannu tasa ta ɗago fuskarshi ta buɗe bakinshi ta fara tsiyaya ruwan aciki, saida ya shanye tass kafin ta ajiye Cup ɗin a gefe, tsintan kanta tayi da zama a kusa dashi, ta ɗago kanshi ta ɗaura a cinyarta tana shafa kanshi dayake cike da kwantaccen lallausan gashi.

Lumshe ido yayi a hankali yace "ya kashemin iyaye kuma ya dawo ya tsaya a gabana nakasa yimishi komai? Tirr dani, tirr da kai Junayd..."
Hannu tasa a wuyanshi tana taɓawa kodai zazzaɓi ne yasashi wannan surutun?, ji tayi kuma jikinshi babu zafi, kallon yadda yake zubar da hawaye tayi har yanzu bai daina maimaita maganan ba.
Da kyar bacci yayi awon gaba dashi, kwantar dashi tayi a hankali tafita daga ɗakin, Fada ta koma domin tabbatar da abinda kunnuwanta suka jiyo mata.

Ganin Abba yana baiwa bakon Ruwa ya durkusa kasa ba karamin faɗuwa gabanta yayi ba, "waye wannan? Meke tafe dashi? Meyasa yakeyin abinda yaga dama?"
Su Saf suna tsaye a wurin kowa yana kallon juna, Umma Suwaiba da Muneer suna gefe guda suma suna kallon juna, Ammi kuma tana ji a ranta kamar tasamu wuka ta yanka wannan mutumin daya kashe mata ƴar uwa, cikin kakkausan murya tayi magana "me kake bukata Kabeeru?"

"Haha abinda nake bukata? Sarauta shine abinda nake bukata daga wurin wannan mijin naki na bogi"

Hannayenta ta dunkule wuri ɗaya zuciyarta tana tafasa tace "Aneesa, Safwan, Muneer, Ibtisam ku koma ɗaki"
Aneesa da bata fahimci komai ba itada Ibtisam suka shiga gaba, Safwan yace 'Ammi ba inda zanje domin nasan komai"
Muneer ma yace bazai fita ba domin bazaiyu ana wulakanta mishi mahaifi yana gani ba, Bayan Aneesa sun fita ta matso gabanshi inda yake zaune akan kujeran sarauta yana shan Ruwan da Abba ya ɗibo mishi, ya ɗaura kada ɗaya kan ɗaya.

"Kabeer? Kanada bakin magana akan Sarauta? Kasan Wanda ya dace ai yazama sarki shine Junayd kaida ka kashe Mahaifinka da hannunka? Ka kashe mahaifiyarka da hannunka shine zakazo kace mu baka sarauta?"

"Ke Maryam? Ki iya bakinki keba komai bane a gidannan face Baiwa, Baiwar ma kaskantacciya ko kin manta ne na tuna miki?"

"Hmmm Kabeer ban manta ba ina sane Ni baiwa ce amma a wurin Mahaifinka bawai a wajenka ba, sannan ka sani Ba kai ba sarauta kuma yanzu zakabar gidannan dan ba gidan ubanka bane"

Dariya yayi sosai yana nuna Ammi, cikin dariyan yace "Haba Maryam ga mahaifina a raye ina kuma zanje? Ai zama yazama dole nayishi agidan mahaifina ko ke na hanaki zama a gidan Babanki ne?"

Ranta ya ɓaci sosai ta cika saura ta fashe, baki ta buɗe cikin ɓacin Rai tace "kafi kowa sanin wannan ba Mahaifinka bane"
"Mahaifina ne mana idan ba mahaifina bane to meya faru? Shine ya canja fuska irin na Babana ya kasheshi domin yazama sarki?"

Abba dayake durkushe a kasa yayi shiru dan Yasan Sharrin Kabeer yanzu ma saida ya shirya kafin yazo gidan.

"Bazaka taɓa samun sarki ba..."
Da sauri Abba ya ɗaga mata hannu yace "ya isa, Baizo nan da Alkhairi ba yazama dole mubi yadda yakeso"
Wani shu'umin dariya Kabeer yakeyi harda rike ciki, watsewa sukayi daga Fadan kowa ranshi babu daɗi, Munner yakalli Ummanshi datake murmushi, bayan sun shiga ɗaki yace "Umma? Me kika shirya kike dariya? Yana miki daɗi da kikaga ana cin zarafin Abba?"

"Muneer kenan kai bakasan komai akan wannan masarautar ba, kayi shiru da bakinka, komai da kakeji kuma kake gani anan ba haka yake ba, bazaka taɓa sanin komai akan wannan masarautar ba har sai ka gani da idonka, kada ka yadda da kowa acikin gidannan domin kowa ba abin yadda bane, hatta shi Mahaifinka ba abun yadda bane, balle wannan matar Maryam, ga kuma wannan kasurgumin ɗan Daban wato Junayd, sunfi kowa sanin waye wannan sunfi kowa sanin tarihinshi, sunfi kowa sanin menene ya kawoshi gidan nan sannan sunfi kowa sanin abinda yake bukata".

Shiru yayi yana hango gaskiya acikin maganar Mamanshi, 
Aneesa data laɓe a bakin kofa taji duk abinda sukace, dama so take ta tambayi Umman waye wannan? Saide yanzu kam tajiyewa kunnenta komai.

Tafiya tafara tana tunanin menene acikin wannan masarautar? Me Junayd suka sani gameda wannan mutumin Kabeer? Kodai zuciyarta batayi mata karya Junayd mugu ne, ya shirya wani abin, tabbas Akwai abinda yake faruwa acikin wannan gidan kuma yazama dole na binciko ma sani.

 *Chapter 47*


                  ~Saida tayi tunani me kyau ta fara gano hanya kafin ta koma ɗakinta, cigaba tayi da kula da mijinta, kallonta Umma Suwaiba tayi tace "To Maryama yanzu ya zamuyi da wannan sabon al'amarin?"
"Akwai yadda zamuyi amma na barwa kaina sani"

Ta barwa kanta sani kuma? Kenan bazata faɗamin ba? 
Murmushi tayi "to nidai inada shawara Maryama a matsayina na Babba"

"Tabbas kece Babba amma anan ba magana Babba ake ba, magana ta mafita akeyi, shi wannan Kabeer ɗin na tabbata yataki wani abu kuma nasan me yataka, zamuyi anfani da hakan muyi maganinshi"

"Ta yaya?"

Kallonta Ammi tayi tace "sanin ta yaya bashine mafita ba, mafi amfanin shine yin maganinshi ɗin"

Badan taso ba tace "hakane Aah yashige mana Gaba"
Ameen.

Safwan yana rike da hannun Abba jikinshi duk yayi sanyi, bai taɓa ganin Abbanshi cikin wannan halin ba, abinda yake bashi haushi shine yadda wannan baƙon yake bawa Abba umarni, abin yanacin ranshi sosai.

 *Chapter 57*


                  ~A jikina nakeji Kabeer bashine yakashemin iyaye ba, kaima ba shine ya kashe maka iyaye ba, Junayd ka sake tunani.

"To ka rabu dani amma ka zauna da ɗan uwanka"
Cikin ɓacin rai yace "shikenan tunda haka kika zaɓa na sake...."
Da Sauri Kabeer ya toshe bakinshi, kwacewa yake ya hanashi.

"Akaina zakayi saki?"
Sakinshi yayi yaje yaɗau wukan da Junayd ɗin ya ajiye yana saita cikinshi yana kuka yace "Tunda ka yadda niɗin makashine  ba komai, so kake ka kasheni ko? To zan kashe kaina amma kafin na mutu inaso nabaka wani labari wanda baka sani ba, akwai wani sarki yanada yara da iyalai dayawa, matanshi uku ya auro wata baiwa itace ta huɗu Baiwar tanada kanwa wacce suke uba ɗaya uwa daban daban, kanwarta taji haushi data auri Sarki ita kuma aka barta tana soyayya da waziri"

"A fili ta nuna tanason Auren saide a zuciya ba haka taso ba, Yayarta tana bata kuɗi komai na bukata idan ya taso mata itace take taimaka mata, ta ƴantata daga baiwa zuwa me enci acikin gidan sarautan, wata rana ta zubawa Yayarta maganin bacci a ruwa tayi bacci ta kwashe gwala-gwalai da zinarai na yayar taje ta sayar, suka haɗa baki da saurayinta waziri suka kaishi kasar waje akayi mishi Plastic surgery yadawo Kamar Sarkin Garin, wannan baiwar ta rinƙa ɓatawa ɗaya daga cikin yaron Sarkin suna, koda yaushe saide tayita faɗan aibunshi kuma tana neman a kasheshi, watarana ta haɗa baki da waziri wanda ta ɓoyeshi a gidan sarkin cikin rijiya, Sun shigo gidan sukayita kisa ciki harda sarki suka kashe, saide ta ɗauke yaron Yayarta domin shine kaɗai zai iya taimaka mata kada a koreta a garin, idan an ganta da yaron sarki zasuce ta rikeshi, ta kashe hadda Yayarta da kowa na gidan, Mutum ɗayane ya tsira shine yaron sarki datake yimishi sharri har ubanshi ya tsaneshi, da kanta suka binne sarki ta haɗa baki da waziri tace shine asalin sarki, bayan yaron Yayarta ya girma tana neman hanyan kasheshi bata samu ba, wata rana yafita ta aika a kasheshi harda kalan kayan dayasa saida tafaɗa, sunzo kasheshi matarshi ta tari kisan suka kasheta"

 *Chapter 58*


                  ~Asad bai Basu labarin komai ya tafi gida abinshi.

Junayd ya kalli Kabeer, to kodai akwai wani abune har yanzu?

Tabbas akwaishi.

Aneesa suna kula dashi sosai Ammi tana shigowa amma basa wani yimata magana sosai, a ranta tasa idan Kabeer ya warke zata basu labarin karya, domin tasan Kabeer ya faɗa musu gaskiya ne.

Abba Yashigo ɗakin ya rufe Kofa Aneesa ta kalli Junayd wanda yake haɗawa Kabeer Tea, wulane a hannun Abba yazo ya riko Junayd zai caka mishi da sauri Kabeer ya tare da hannunshi nan hannun yafara zubar da jini, Junayd ya juya a fusace zai kaiwa Abba duka, ji yayi bazai iya ba, sai huci yake, Aneesa kuma ta riko Kabeer tana wanke hannun nashi.

Shima Abba kuka yake "da ban barku ba da yanzu sarauta baya hannunmu, Maryama da Waziri sun hada baki domin su kasheni, a lokacin Umman Junayd ta jisu, tasan inda suka ɓoye Wazirin, ranan da suka kawo mana hari nikuma nayi sauri naje wurin rijiyan na canja mana kaya nida Waziri sai na ɗaukeshi nakaishi Fada, bakinshi baya iya magana domin na buge mishi baki da ice, bayan na ajiyeshi a fada saina gudu cikin rijiyan na zauna kamar yadda naga ya zauna.

Sun kasheshi a matsayin nine suka kashe, sai tazo da kanta ta kwanceni suka naɗani sarki basusan nine asalin Sarkin ba, har yau Maryam batasan Waziri aka kashe ba, ina Binta da halinta domin nasan inda ta dosa, yakai sau uku ina kaucewa Junayd mutuwa, kaina Kabeer ranan da aka harbeka nine na aika Asad yaje ya taimaka maka, babu wanda yasan wannan labarin sai Asad, dama wannan ranan nake jira yazo, gashi yau har kuna iya tarewa junanku mutuwa nagodewa Allah da kuka haɗa kanku.

A tsorace Aneesa tace 'eh"

Ji sukayi an faɗi a bakin kofa da sauri suka buɗe kofan, Safwan ne kwance a sume da alama yaji duk abinda suka faɗa, Junayd ya ɗagashi ya kaishi ɗakinshi, ruwa ya wanke mishi fuska dashi, a hankali ya buɗe ido yana kallon Junayd ya janyoshi yana kuka, Junayd ma share hawaye yake yana cewa "ka daina kuka"

"Ke ana gobe suna bazakizo bane kike nufi?"

Cikin kuka tafara bawa Adda Surayya labarin abinda ya faru.

Surayya itama saida hankalinta ya tashi, ta rinƙa bata hakuri, Junayd ne ya shigo jikinshi a mace wannan labarin nasu ya matukar razanashi.

Ɗaukanta yayi yashiga Bedroom dan ita, kuka Dukansu suke, Yafara cire kayan jikinta, rike hannunshi tayi tace "Bama cikin mood me daɗi kada kayi komai dan Allah"

Jin abinda yafaɗa yabata tausayi, barinshi tayi ya rinƙa laguɗa jikinta kamar bai taɓa Kasancewa da ita ba.

Ammi ta lura kamar kowa yasan komai a gidan neman hanyan gudu kawai take bayan Safwan ya irga mata komai cikin kuka da jamata Allah ya isa, cikin dare ta tashi zata gudu taga kowa idonshi biyu acikin masu gadi, ganin zasu kamata kuma kamar Abba ne yasa hakan, ta mugun razana dataji Sarkine ba Waziri ba tasan idan tashiga hannunshi bazataji da daɗi ba.

Ɗakinta tashiga ta rufe, Rataye kanta tayi a jikin fanka kafin ta ture kujeran data hau, ita da kanta ta kashe kanta.

"Babu komai"

"To ku daina damuwa kunji?"

Ihu tayi jikinta yana rawa, da gudu suka shiga ɗakin suna son ganin me tayiwa Ibtisam ɗin, Ganin Ammi ta rataye kanta, Kowa saida jikinshi yayi sanyi, Abba dayake bakin kofa yayi murmushi yace "Tayiwa kanta hukunci da nine Zanyi Mata Wanda yafi wannan"
Juyawa yayi yafita, Safwan ya janyota yaga bazata sakko ba, a firgice yahau kujera da taimakon Junayd da Kabeer suka kwanceta, jikinta ya bushe ta sanƙare idonta a buɗe Alaman ta mutu.

Aneesa tana daga tsaye saida ta zauna, Ibtisam kuma tana aikin kuka jikinta yana rawa, Safwan yace "hakan shine ya dace da Ammi kada kowa yace rataye kanta tayi mubari a bugun zuciya ne ya sameta"
Gaba ɗaya sunji tausayin Safwan da Ibtisam saide suma sun san Abinda tayi shine daidai da ita, zataje kuma suyi hisabi a gaban Allah.

Su Asad da Surayya wanda ake sunan ƴarsu yau suma sunzo gidan akayi jana'iza tare dasu aka kaita kabari, Surayya tana dakin Aneesa sai kuka take tana bata labarin abinda ya faru, Innalillahi wa inna ilaihiraji'un kawai take maimaitawa.

Umman Muneer da ɗanta suka sun tsorata da Ammi ta kashe kanta, a halin yanzu sun san Suda mulki saide suga anayi, domin Junayd da Kabeer da Abba sun fisu Power.

Saida akayi kwana uku kafin kowa ya watse, Abba ya haɗa taro acikin fada duk suka hallara yakalli Umman Muneer yace "Suwaiba kinfi kowa sanin babu aure a tsakaninmu domin niɗin ba mijinki bane kamar yadda na sanar miki"

"Kuma kinsan Muneer ba ɗana bane, shin zaki hakura ki tafi ne ko kuma zaki canja hali keda ɗanki ku shiryu na aureki?"

Da sauri tace "nama canja hali yallaɓai shima Muneer wallahi ya canja hali kwana uku kenan tunda akayi wannan rasuwan bayashan komai ya nutsu"

"Idan kuka kara me zanyi muku?"

"Yallaɓai ka sakeni ka koremu a garin gaba ɗaya"

Tayi maganan tsakaninta da Allah.

Kallon Muneer yayi yace "kanaji ai?"

"Eh Abba"

"To Junayd da Kabeer ku shaida komai zan auri Suwaiba, Safwan kuyi hakuri kaida Ibtisam kuma ƴaƴane a wurina kunji?"

Atare sukace "tom Abba"

"Kai safwan Ka fito da mata nayi maka aure dan nasan tun ba yau ba kakeson aure"

Kanshi kasa yace "Abba Ni bafulata nakeso"

Dariya sukayi, Abba yace "Indai Bafulatana kakeso da gaske akwai wata yarinya a wani kauye kusada Abuja, Ƴar mai garin Garinsu ce Sunanta Safiya, tanaso ta auri Ɗan birni hakan yasa take jiran wani matashi sunanshi Sadauki, shikuma yayi mata alkawarin Aure saide yaje yayi aure acikin abuja ya auri ƴar kanwar Matar babanshi, Kaje ka auri Safiya zata zame maka Alkhairi da yaddan Allah"

(Safiyya na cikin littafin MUTUNCINA kunsan bamu aurar da ita ba)

Taɓe baki tayi tana ɗan dariya.

"Abba jiyane"

Da sauri Aneesa ta koma bayan Junayd dan taji tsoro data ganshi.

Kafin yayi magana yakai mishi naushi abaki.

Kabeer da ranshi ya ɓaci yazo da gudu ya shaƙe Safwan ɗin yafara dukanshi tako ina.

Junayd ne ya kwace daga rikon da Aneesa tayi mishi yaje da gudu ya rike Kabeer tare suka fara dukanshi da Safwan saida sukayi mishi jina jina kafin suka barshi.

Aneesa tana basu hakuri basu yadda sun bari ba, kwace Kabeer ɗin tayi ta janyeshi ta kaishi wani ɗaki, tsintan kanta tayi da ɗibo ruwa tafara wanke mishi fuska inda suka farfasa mishi sai jini yake zuba, ganin jinin bai tsaya ba ga kanshi ya fashe ta ciro ɗankwalin dayake kanta ta ɗaura mishi akai, nan take jini ya daina zuba, kwantar dashi tayi a gefe ta janyo wani akwati ta ciro Babban mayafi ta shimfiɗa mishi akasa, taimaka mishi tayi ya kwanta tace "Sannu"
Giɗa kai yayi yana kallonta, Hannunshi taga ya fashe yana jini, yaga Riganta tayi ta ɗaure mishi dashi.

"Kwanta ka huta kada kanka yayi ciwo"

"Meyasa kika taimaka min bayan kinsan niɗin mugune"

Murmushi tayi "ba dolene yazama kai mugu ba, wani a fuska yanada mugunta a zuciya kuma yanada sanyi, wani kuma a zuciya yanada mugunta a fuska kuma yanada hankali"

"Amma Ni ai kinsan mugu ne"

Tana goge jinin daya zuba a kasa tace "Mugu ai baya faɗan kanshi kuma ai da kai mugune kamar yadda ka faɗa da ranan daka duke Junayd ba zaka ɓuya kana kuka ba"

Da mamaki ya kalleta "ya akayi kika sani?"

Ɗago kai tayi tana dariya kaɗan tace "Da ƙwaƙwalwa nake aiki bada ido ba"

Fita tayi a ɗakin bayan ta rufeshi, Junayd ta gani yanata safa da marwa hannunshi ya naɗe a bayanshi yana tsoron abinda Kabeer ɗin zai yiwa Aneesa.
Ammi na gefenshi tana sharan kwalla.

Ganin ta fito lafiya yaje da gudu yana dubata, "babu abinda ya miki?"
Ajiye tsumman dayake hannunta tayi tace "Baimin komai ba, wani lokacin abinda kake gani ba haka yake ba, na gyara mishi ciwon da kukaji mishi yanzu yasamu bacci"
Tana gama magana ta bar wurin.

Da kallon Mamaki Ammi ta bishi, meke faruwa? Aneesa ta taimaka wannan mugun meyasa?

Junayd kasa jurewa yayi saida yabi bayanta, ɗakinta tashiga tana wanke hannunta, Binta yayi har Toilet ya rikota da karfi ya juyo da ita.

"Ka sakeni kana jimin ciwo"

"Bazan sakeki ba saikin gayamin dalilin dayasa kika duba Kabeer"

"You're Hurting me Junayd ka sakeni"

Cikin tsawa yace "bazan sakeki ba, bakisan cewa shine ya kashemin iyaye ba? Kuma shine ya kashe iyayenki? Ko bakiga irin wahalan dayake bawa Abba na da Ammi ba? Bakida hankali ne? Aneesa ki dawo hayyacinki meyake damunki?"

Ture hannunshi tayi itama da karfi tace "babu abinda yake damuna, a cikin hankali na nake, Kabeer ba mugu bane kamar yadda kake gani, Ɗan uwanka ne, duk lokacin da kukayi faɗa ɓuya yake yana kuka, shi kaɗai yasan abinda yake damunshi acikin zuciyarshi ka daina wannan Banzan tunanin"

Wani irin mari ya wanke fuskarta dashi, saida taga taurari a sama, cikin fusata da ɓacin rai yace "bakisan me kike faɗa bako? Ammi ce zatayi karya ko kuma Abba ne?"

A hankali ta ɗago idonta har ya canja kala ya koma jajur, tace "Bance sunyi karya ba, amma akwai abinda ba daidai ba, ko ka yadda ko kada kayadda akwai abinda suka ɓoye maka,sannan bazan daina faɗa ba Kabeer ba mugu bane, lokacin salla baya taɓa wuveshi sannan koda yaushe idan kunyi faɗa ɓuya yake yana kuka, kuma akwai tsana me yawa acikin idonshi wanda yayiwa Abba da Ammi, kai baiyi maka ba, idan mulki yakeso kaine farkon wanda zai fara kashewa kafin ya kashe Abba amma ka tuna ranan da kuke faɗa yana kare kanshi ne bawai yana dukanka ba"

Tana gama magana tafita a Toilet din ta barshi tsaye yana huci, kan Sofa ta kwanta tanajin kirjinta yana mata zafi.

Jikinshi ya ɗanyi sanyi amma ai yasan ba gaskiya take faɗa ba, fita yayi yabar ɗakin, tana jinshi ya banƙo kofar kamar zai karya, tanada yakinin Kabeer ba mugu bane.

Ammi ta kalli Ibtee da Safwan tace "me Aneesa tayi? Itada zatayi supporting ɗin mijinta meyasa take goyon bayan Kabeer?"

Shiru sukayi ɗan babu me amsa a cikinsu, Junayd ne yazo ya rike Ammi ya kaita ɗakinta sai hakuri yake bata yanaso ya kwantar mata da hankali.

Abba ya koma ɗaki ya kwanta yanaji kamar kanshi zai rabu biyu tsaban tunani da Tashin hankali, sarauta ko masifa? Innalillahi gidana babu kwanciyar hankali? Ya zanyi.

Ammi ta shafa fuskan Junayd tace "kabi Aneesa a hankali kada ranka ya ɓaci dan ta kula da Kabeer koba komai shi ɗin ɗan uwanka ne"

"Kiyi hakuri Ammi"

"Kada ka damu ba komai"

Fita yayi yaje dakin Abba, ganin Umma Suwaiba ya gaisheta ta amsa, zama yayi yafara bawa Abba hakuri, Abba yace "kada ka damu sannan kabi matarka a sannu banson kayi mata faɗa kowa da irin tunanin shi kaji?"

"Tom Abba Nagode"

Fita yayi yanajin haushin Aneesa ta yaya wannan mutanen da suke nuna mata soyayya zatayi zargin sun faɗi karya a labarinshi? Meyasa Aneesa zatayi mishi haka?.



Sunyi kwana uku basa magana kullum sai taje ɗakin da Kabeer yake ta dubashi, wani takai mishi abinci wani kuma abinsha, ya hanata amma taki yadda.

Junayd yau yaga tana fitowa daga ɗakin ranshi ya ɓaci sosai, da karfi yazo ya mannata da bango yace "me kike zuwa yi a ɗakinshi?"

"Abinci nake kai mishi ko kana zargi ne?"

Dafe kanshi yayi yace "Aneesa banso nayi miki abinda bazakiji daɗi ba ki fita a harkan Kabeer"

"Junayd Bazan fita ba"
Ranshi ya ɓaci sosai ya wanketa da mafi, ko kuka batayi ba tace "Ko kasheni Zakayi saina kula dashi"

Barin wurin yayi kamar zai tashi sama dan bakin ciki.

An kirata a waya Adda Surayya ta haihu, tasamu ƴarta, daɗi taji sosai a daren taje gidan, sai can tsakan dare tayi shirin dawowa domin basu da nisa, a hanya taga ana Binta, a tsorace ta juya tafa wasu mutane da bakaken kaya, gudu ta fara kamar kafarta zai fita, saida ta shiga gidan kafin ta zauna akasa tana haƙi, da kyar ta mike ta koma ɗakinsu, Junayd yana palour yaga ta shigo tana haƙi, a tsorace ya tashi yana kallonta zuwa wurinta yayi ya riketa "meya sameki?"

"Ya Junayd? Wasu mutane ne suke bina da bakin kaya jikinsu"
"Sorry zauna dama ai kinyi dare kuma ke kaɗai"
Yama manta sunyi faɗa, ruwa ya kawo mata yace "Basu miki komai ba kam"

"A,a basumin komai ba"
Ɓoye tashin hankalin dayake ciki yake domin ya tsorata ba kaɗan ba, saide baison ta gane dan zata fishi jin tsoron.

Zama yayi ya janyota jikinshi yana shafa bayanta yace "is okay"
Knocking akayi yace "yes"
Da sauri Ammi ta Turo kofan tashigo "Aneesa!!! Wai an biki? Basu miki komai ba kam?"
A tsorace take maganan.

Aneesa ta tashi daga jikinshi tace "A,a basumin komai ba Ammi"

"Tom kibi a hankali kinji?"

"Tom Ammi"
Fita tayi tana sauke ajiyan zuciya, Aneesa ta koma ta kwanta a kirjinshi.
Lumshe ido tayi da sauri ta gyara kwanciya a ranta tace "waye ya faɗawa Ammi an biyoni? Banyi maganan da kowa ba sai Junayd danake faɗa mishi yanzu, ta yaya akayi ta sani?"

Abin ya ɗaure mata takasa rikewa tace "ya Junayd?"

"Na'am"
 "Waye ya fadawa Ammi an biyoni ban faɗawa kowa bafa"

Yace "maybe wasu sun ganki a waje"

Shiru kawai tayi, amma tasan babu wanda ya ganta sai waɗanda suka biyota.

Bata kuma yimishi maganan ba tadai bar Tambayan wa zuciyarta.

Kabeer ya samu sauki yadawo fada yaci gaba da abinda yake, sai abinda ya faɗawa Abba yakeyi.

Junayd yana gani amma Abba ya hanashi magana, wani irin tsana yake yiwa Kabeer ɗinnan yanzu kam yasa a ranshi kome zai faru saide ya faru amma dole saiya kashe Kabeer.

Yau cikin dare ya shirya cikin bakaken kaya ya rufe fuskanshi saida yatabbatar Aneesa tayi bacci kafin ya ɗau wuka yasa a gefen wandonshi yafita, buɗe ido tayi bayan taga yafita, dama ba bacci take ba, tasan wannan ranan zaizo domin Junayd yana nuna tsanan Kabeer a fili.

Binshi tayi abaya cikin sanda, bai tsaya ko inaba sai ɗakin da Kabeer yake kwana, wani Extra key yaciro daga Aljihunshi ya buɗe yashiga, binshi tayi dan bai rufe ɗakin ba.

Kunna wuta yayi yaga Kabeer ɗin yana bacci ya rungume Pillow da alama baccin yanayi mishi daɗi.

A hankali ya taka zuwa wurinshi ya ɗaga wukan bayan ya cire Pillow daga kikinshi ya saita daidai cikinshi zai caka, Aneesa ta rike, jin An rike ya juyo yana son ganin Wanda ya hanashi aikata abinda ya jima yana Plan ɗinshi.

Ganin Aneesa tana tsaye tana kallonshi hannunta yana zubar da jini Alaman ba karamin yankewa tayi ba, ya zaro ido yace "Aneesa? Kin haukace ne"

Kabeer ne ya farka jin mutane a kanshi, da kallo yake binsu ya fahimci abinda yake faruwa Junayd ne yazo kasheshi Aneesa ta tare da hannunta.

Junayd ta rude ya rike hannun Aneesa yana cewa "kinji Ciwo Aneesa sannu meyasa kikayi haka?"

"Yarima Inaji ina gani bazan bari ka kashe ɗan uwanka ba, Kabeer yayanka ne sau nawa zan faɗa maka? Sau nawa zan faɗa maka ka daina neman kasheshi shiɗin yayanka ne"

Sakin hannunta yayi cikin tsawa yace "shiɗin ba Yayana bane shiɗin makashin iyayena da naki ne"
