*YARIMA JUNAYD*

  Na
Jiddah S Mapi

 *Chapter 59*


                  ~Junayd Yana Bata kulawa sosai, kullum saita aika an karɓo mata ƴar Adda Surayya wacce ake kira da Farhat.

Junayd ya koma bakin aiki yana cigaba da Aikinshi na doctor, yanzu masarautar tadawo yadda akeso babu wanda yasan sirrin abinda akayi a baya sai mutanen dasuke cikinta.

Abba ya auri Umman Muneer ne saboda rufe sirrin masarautarsu, zamanta kusa dashi shine mafi maslaha a rayuwarshi.

Zaune suke a Dining sunacin abinci Safwan ne Yashigo yana waya sai dariya yake, zama yayi a ɗaya daga cikin kujerun yana cigaba da wayan, saida ya gama Junayd yace "dawa kake waya haka?"

"Nida Ya Muneer ne yanacan a school zasuyi exam Sai Addu'a yake wai Allah yasa kada ya fadi kasan ba karamin wasa yayi da damanshi ba"

Umma Suwaiba tace "Ai kuwa shiya sani babu irin nasihan da banyi mishi ba yaronnan yaki jina gashi yanzu ai yana ɗanawa a school ɗin nikam subashi zero ma ko zanji daɗi"

Dariya sukayi su duka, Aneesa tace "umma ina kika tabajin anci zero a school?"

Kallonta Safwan yayi yace "zan tona fa idan kika kara magana wallahi"

"To ka tona mana me nayi dahar zaka tona."

"Ohhh kin manta ranan da aka baki report sheet Kika Nemo Biro Kika canja position....?"

Plate na roba ta ɗauka ta wurga mishi a jiki, da sauri ya kauce tace "karyane ba kaine ka zugani ba"

"Ni ban zugaki ba"

Junayd dayake cin abinci yayi kyau sosai cikin kananan kaya ya saci kallonta yace "Oh dama ashe kece kika gyara har nace kinada kokari ashe ashe..."
Cokali ta ɗauka ta rinƙa bugunshi dashi tana kukan wasa, riko hannunta yayi yana kaucewa yace "ke tsaya kada ki jimin ciwo"

A kunneshi tace "wallahi zanga me kulaka yau a da dare"

Da sauri yace "na tuba a yafemin Gimbiya Aneesa"
Abba yace "Ku daina tsokananta"
Shiru sukayi kowa ya maida hankali yanacin abinci.

Kabeer kam dama bai fiye surutu ba saide yayita kallon Ibtisam kawai, a taƙure take sosai dan yasa mata ido dayawa, bata wani koshi ba ta mike zata tafi Umma tace "mamana har kin koshi?"
Satan kallon Kabeer ɗin tayi tace "eh"
Saida ta tafi Junayd ya matso kusa dashi yace "Ya Kabeer? Dan Allah ka rage kallemin kanwa gaba ɗaya takasa sakewa a taƙure take idan kana wuri"
Marin fuskan Junayd ɗin yayi cikin wasa yace "bazan rage ba"

Tashi yayi yace "Alhamdulillah"
Ɗakin Ibtisam yaje ta zauna akan Sofa ta rungumi Pillow ɗan karami tana tunani, ya zauna a gefenta ya zuba mata ido, kallonshi tayi tace "sannu?"
Tasan idan tashine saide su wuni a wurin baiyi magana ba, suna cewa ya Junayd miskili ne ashe yanada surutu a wurin Kabeer.

Baiyi magana ba yana kallonta, idanunshi ba karamin tasiri sukeyi a cikin zuciyarta ba, har wani lunshe ido yake yana karyar da kai.

Saida ta rufe fuskarta da tafin hannunta tace "nikam ka daina kallona"

Hannu yasa ya janye hannunta yana cigaba da kallonta, saida tafara tara hawaye a idonta kafin ya saketa yana dariya cikin sanyin muryanshi yace "kunyata kikeji?"

Jijjiga kai tayi tana Turo baki.

"To ki daina dan nikam banso anajin kunyana, ki saki jikinki dani banine zan aureki ba?"
Giɗa kai tayi

"To banson wannan kunyan Dan zaki cutar dani idan munyi aure nafison ki cire kunya ki saba dani sosai kinji Baby na?"

"Tom, Ya Kabeer?"

"Na'am Baby Ibtee"

"Ka yafemin da fari nayi maka kallon mugu bansan haka kakeda sanyi ba, Ka yafemin dan Allah"
Tayi maganan tana sunkuyar da kanta.

Matsowa yayi kusa da ita yace "kin ɗaukeni a matsayin yaya?"

Jijjiga kai tayi, ya matso sosai ya buɗe hannunshi Alaman tazo matsowa tayi ta rungumeshi tafara kuka, shafa kanta yayi yace 'Ki daina kuka bakimin komai ba, naji daɗi da Allah yasa nine Zan aureki bazan iya jurewa naga kina tare da wani ba, nine Zan iya kula dake yadda nakeso, Mahaifinku Allah yayi mishi rahama haka itama Amminku, ki manta da baya muyi rayuwa me inganci, banso na kara ganin kina kuka kinji?"

"Tom Nagode"

Cikin wasa yace "to tashi a jikina tunda bamuyi auren ba kada kisani a wani hali kinsan fa na jima banyi aureba har ji nake kamar ace gobene auren"

Tureshi tayi tana Turo baki "Ni banson irin wannan maganar"

"Nikuma inaso"
Matsawa tayi daga wajenshi tana jin kunya, miskili ne amma sai sakin zance.

"Yi hakuri mana Baby ba nabaki hakuri ba tun ɗazu?'
Junayd ne zaune a gefen Aneesa ya rike kunne yana bata hakuri domin ta cika tana neman fashewa.

"Nikam ban hakura ba"

"To me kikeso nayi miki saiki hakura?"

"So nake ka kwana a palour na kwana uku kafin na hakura"

"Baby kinsan bazan iya ba ki canja wani"

"To saide ka kwana akan Sofa nikuma akan gado"

"Wannan ma ki canja"

"To nikam bazan hakura ba"

Janyota yayi jikinshi yana kallon yadda cikinta ya fito sosai shafawa yayi yace "Allah ya saukeki Lafiya sai nakara yimiki wani kinga zamu haifi yara da wuri wuri ko?"

Tureshi tayi "banso dan bakai bane da cikin shiyasa, da kasan wahalan danake ɗanawa da bakai wannan maganan ba, tayi maganan idonta yana cika da hawaye.

Ganin zatayi kuka yace "yi hakuri Da wasa nake"

Murmushi tayi tace "zanso na haihu dakai sosai amma jikina yana nauyi wallahi bazan iya ba, cikina kullum sai yayi ciwo, gashi kayana duk sunmin kaɗan nazama wata katuwa"

Dariya yake kunshewa domin idan yayi saita kwana uku batayi mishi magana ba, yasan masifa da bala'i zasuyi idan yayi dariyannan, Kallonshi tayi "dariya kake ɓoyewa?"

"A,a ba dariya nake ba, nikam tausayi kika bani"

"Gaskiyane niɗin abin a tausayawa ce ka duba ka gani da Ni siririya ce banida nauyi yanzu kuma nazama katuwa ya zanyi ne?"

"Kiyi hakuri idan kin haihu zaki dawo daidai kinji?"

Jijjiga kai tayi, harga Allah batason wannan girman jikin, abinda yafi bata haushi shine babu kayanta Atamfa dayake karɓanta saide tayita sa dogayen riguna.

Sai lallashinta yake shima yana addu'a Allah ya sauketa lafiya.

Surayya tana kula da ƴarta wacce tasa mata takwaran Mama.

Asad ma yana kokari wurin sanyata farin ciki, Fadwa da Umar har an fara maganan sa ranan aurensu domin suna soyayya sosai ba kaɗan ba.

Aneesa kuma ta tsaya da karatu har sai ta haihu tukun 


تممت بحمد الله 

Anan nakawo karshen littafin Yarima Junayd, kuskuren dake cikinta Ubangiji Allah ya yafemin, Alkhairin dayake ciki Allah ya bani lada, Nagode muku da bibiyan littafina saimun haɗu a littafina me zuwa insha Allah, nice taku Jiddah S Mapi.
